# 1. Product

This is the **master product documentation**. It includes:

- **Header & Footer Always Visible Elements (For ALL Users)**
*(Public visitors, Home-Hunters, Owners — everyone sees these)*
    
    ---
    
    # **Header Navigation (Always Visible)**
    
    ```
    [Yalla.House]   [Services & Pricing]   [About]   [List Your Place]  
    ```
    
    - **Header Link Routing Guide (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ---
        
        ## **1. Purpose (1 sentence)**
        
        A clean, always-visible top navigation bar that uses Dashfolio+ defaults and leads users to core public pages and the “List Your Place” onboarding flow.
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Header Layout (Updated)**
        
        ### **LEFT**
        
        ### **🏡 Yalla.House**
        
        - Permanent link to **Home** (/)
        - **Always displayed in Yalla Yellow (#F8D22A)**
        - Hover: same yellow, no underline
        - No logo image needed — text only
        
        ---
        
        ### **CENTER NAVIGATION**
        
        *(Normal Dashfolio font + white text)*
        
        - **Services & Pricing**
        - **About**
        - Hover: slightly darker yellow (Dashfolio default hover behavior)
        
        ---
        
        ### **RIGHT CTA**
        
        **[ List Your Place ]**
        
        - Primary button
        - Fill color: **Yalla Yellow**
        - Hover: slightly darker yellow (Dashfolio default hover behavior)
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Colors & Typography**
        
        - Typography: **Dashfolio+ default** (Plus Jakarta Sans)
        - Header background: **Dashfolio dark**
        - Default link color: **White**
        - Hover color (non-brand text): **Yalla Yellow**
        
        > Only the “Yalla.House” brand text is ALWAYS yellow.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **4. Header → Page Routing (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ### **Yalla.House**
        
        - **Route:** /
        - **What opens:** The public landing page
        - **Used by:** Everyone (Owners, Home-hunters, Public)
        
        ---
        
        ### **Services & Pricing**
        
        - **Route:** /services
        - **Page type:** **One Wireframe**
        - **Contents (simple boxes):**
            - 360° Scan
            - Floorplan creation
            - Professional photos
            - Legal support
            - For Sale board (Sign)
            - Advertising packages (Rightmove / Zoopla etc.)
            - Hands-on support
            - Pricing tiers
        - **Design:**
            - Cards/boxes
            - Short descriptions
            - “Add to my Listing” buttons (later phase)
        
        ---
        
        ### **About**
        
        - **Route:** /about
        - **Page type:** **Single page**
        - **Contents:**
            - Short mission (“No fees. No commission.”)
            - Why Yalla.House exists
            - Founder info (optional)
            - Trust symbols / data protection
        
        ---
        
        ### **List Your Place**
        
        - **Route:** /list
        - **Flow:**
            1. Shows login prompt (if user not logged in)
            2. After login → jumps directly to **WF-O2 (My Listings)**
            3. Starts at **First-Time Wizard** (Step 1 – Basics)
        - **Design:**
            
            Dashfolio “form panel” style with progress bar. See  WF Owner 2 
            
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Developer Summary**
        
        - Use Dashfolio header component
        - Insert our nav labels
        - Set brand text color = #F8D22A
        - Set CTA color = #F8D22A
        - Ensure routing works as defined
        - Do NOT add login button (login lives in sidebar only)
        
        ---
        
    
    ---
    
    # **FOOTER (Always Visible)**
    
    ```jsx
    								                   YALLA.HOUSE FOOTER
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    
    COLUMN 1 — Brand & Company           COLUMN 2 — Policies           COLUMN 3 — Legal & Compliance        COLUMN 4 — Contact
    ────────────────────────────────     ───────────────────────────    ───────────────────────────────       ──────────────────────────────
    Yalla.House                          Privacy Policy                GDPR & Safety Statement              Support (mailto:support@yalla.house)
    “No fees. No commission.”            Terms of Service              Imprint                              WhatsApp (chat link)
    Company No: 1234                     Cookie Policy                 Security & Data Protection           
    Registered in England & Wales.                                                                          
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    © 2025 Yalla.House — A UKConsultant Project. All rights reserved.
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    ```
    
    - **Footer Link Routing Guide (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ---
        
        **COLUMN 1 — Brand & Company**
        
        ### **Yalla.House (Logo / Text)**
        
        - **Action:** Always routes to **Home Page** (/).
        - **Designer note:**
            
            Use standard Dashfolio+ header style. Hover = Yalla yellow.
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Set as a global navigation home link. No other behavior.
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 2 — Policies (all use a shared layout)**
        
        ### **Privacy Policy**
        
        - **Action:** Opens dedicated policy page (/privacy-policy).
        - **Designer note:**
            
            *Uses the unified “Legal Page Wireframe”—simple headline, left-nav anchors, clean text layout.*
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Anchor-ready sections (#data, #rights, etc.).
            
            SEO index allowed.
            
        
        ### **Terms of Service**
        
        - **Action:** Opens (/terms).
        - Designer/Developer rules:
            
            Same template as Privacy Policy. No custom design per page.
            
        
        ### **Cookie Policy**
        
        - **Action:** Opens (/cookies).
        - Designer/Developer rules:
            
            Same shared “Legal Page” template. No new wireframe needed.
            
            Cookie banner must link to this page.
            
        
        > Developer note:
        > 
        
        > All Policies share one React/Framer template (3 pages, 1 component). Reuse banner, spacing, typography.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 3 — Legal & Compliance**
        
        ### **GDPR & Safety**
        
        - **Action:** Scrolls to GDPR section inside /privacy-policy
            
            → **Anchor link:** /privacy-policy#gdpr
            
        - **Designer note:**
            
            No new page. Just a highlighted section inside Privacy Policy.
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Must support scrolling to anchors even on mobile.
            
        
        ### **Imprint (DE only)**
        
        - **Action:** Opens /imprint
        - Designer note:
            
            Only appears once Germany rollout is active. Same “Legal Page” template.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Controlled by country toggle in admin (show_imprint = true/false).
            
        
        ### **Security & Data Protection**
        
        - **Action:** Opens /security
        - Designer note:
            
            Reuse “Legal Page” layout.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Simple static content page; no integrations needed.
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 4 — Contact**
        
        ### **Support**
        
        - **Action:** mailto:support@yalla.house
        - Designer note:
            
            Simple link—no modal.
            
            Keep consistent with other footer links (white text + yellow hover).
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Use mailto: with subject prefilled:
            
            ?subject=Support Request - Yalla.House
            
        
        ### **WhatsApp**
        
        - **Action:** Opens WhatsApp chat
            
            → https://wa.me/<NUMBER>
            
        - Designer note:
            
            Use text-only, no icon in footer.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Must open WhatsApp on mobile or WhatsApp Web on desktop.
            
        
        ---
        
        # **🔧 Developer Routing Summary (one-line per link)**
        
        | **Link** | **Route** | **Template** | **Special Rules** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | Yalla.House | / | Home | Always visible |
        | Privacy Policy | /privacy-policy | Legal template | Anchor-ready |
        | Terms of Service | /terms | Legal template | — |
        | Cookie Policy | /cookies | Legal template | Linked from cookie banner |
        | GDPR & Safety | /privacy-policy#gdpr | Legal template | Anchor scroll |
        | Imprint | /imprint | Legal template | Conditional (DE only) |
        | Security | /security | Legal template | — |
        | Support | mailto:support@yalla.house | — | Subject prefill |
        | WhatsApp | wa.me/<number> | — | Auto-detect device |
        
        ---
        
        # **🎨 Designer Summary**
        
        - All **Policies**, **Legal**, and **Imprint** pages use **one unified legal-page layout**.
        - Footer links are text-only, white → yellow on hover.
        - Layout = simple, minimalist, no extra icons, no images.
        - Must visually match Dashfolio+ dark theme.

    ### **PERMISSIONS SUMMARY**
    
    | **Area** | **Logged-Out Public** | **Home-Hunter** | **Owner** | **Admin** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Header | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Footer | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Owner Sidebar | ✘ | ✘ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Owner Profile Menu | ✘ | ✘ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Home-Hunter Sidebar | ✘ | ✔ | ✘ | ✔ |
    
    This ensures clean separation between user roles.
    
    ---
    
- **WF-ACC — Unified Account Settings (Owner + Home-Hunter)**
    
    > WF-ACC is a single, role-aware Account Settings page for Owners and Home-Hunters, with auto-detected country, shared identity & security sections, and role-specific blocks for billing, integrations, services (Owners) and buying position, documents, and purchased surveys (Home-Hunters).
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ---
    
    ## **1. Designer Checklist**
    
    - Use **Dashfolio+ dark** layout, standard form styles.
    - Page structure = **single column**, split into sections:
        1. Personal Details
        2. Contact Information
        3. Notifications
        4. Security
        5. GDPR & Data
        6. **Owner-only: Billing, Integrations, Services**
        7. **Home-Hunter-only: Buying Position, Documents, Purchased Surveys**
    - Sections should be **collapsible** for long pages.
    - Show **success state** after save (small “Saved ✓” status).
    - Use **Yalla Yellow** only for:
        - Primary buttons
        - Important labels (e.g. Verified)
    - Mobile: same content, stacked.
    
    ---
    
    ## **2. Developer Checklist**
    
    - Single page, single route:
        
        GET /account/settings / POST /account/settings
        
    - **Role-aware rendering**:
        - If role === "owner" → show Owner section.
        - If role === "homeHunter" → show HH section.
    - Auto-detect **country** on first login via GeoIP:
        - Default to **United Kingdom** if nothing detected.
    - All labels must use **i18n** (language-ready).
    - Each section saves **independently** (partial updates).
    - Integrate:
        - Stripe (billing)
        - Twilio/WhatsApp (phone verification, later)
        - Internal services for “services & add-ons” and “purchased surveys”.
    
    ---
    
    ## **3. Journey Summary (Short)**
    
    - **Owners** use this page to:
        - Keep contact info up to date
        - Manage billing & plan
        - See/add services (photos, signs, EPC, surveys, etc.)
        - Manage integrations (Google Calendar, WhatsApp)
    - **Home-Hunters** use this page to:
        - Complete their profile
        - Set buying position (Cash / Mortgage etc.)
        - Manage notification preferences
        - See purchased surveys
        - Upload docs later (ID, proof of income)
    
    This page feeds trust + smoother offers + less friction.
    
    ---
    
    ## **4. Where This Page Sits**
    
    **For both roles:**
    
    - Accessible from:
        - Sidebar “Account Settings” (top)
        - Profile/avatar dropdown (if used)
        - “Complete your profile” prompts in:
            - Booking confirmation
            - Offer / Application flow
    
    ---
    
    ## **5. Purpose**
    
    - Give **one central place** to manage:
        - Identity
        - Contact details
        - Notifications
        - Security
        - Country / locale
        - Role-specific tools:
            - Owner: billing, integrations, services
            - HH: buying status, docs, surveys
    - Reduce support load and confusion.
    
    ---
    
    ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
    
    - Owners know:
        - Which plan they’re on
        - Which services they’ve ordered
        - What’s connected (Calendar, WhatsApp)
    - Home-Hunters know:
        - How “strong” they look to Owners
        - Which surveys they’ve unlocked
    - Both:
        - Can keep email/phone current → fewer failed messages
        - Can manage notifications & privacy
        - Have one place to manage their account
    
    ---
    
    ## **7. Layout & Sections (Designer Spec)**
    
    ### **7.1 Header**
    
    **Title:** Account Settings
    
    **Subtitle:** Manage your profile, services and preferences.
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.2 Section 1 — Personal Details (Shared)**
    
    Fields:
    
    - First Name
    - Last Name
    - Preferred Name (optional)
    - **Country**
        - Dropdown:
            - Auto-filled from GeoIP on first load
            - MVP: United Kingdom as default
        - Copy for designers:
            
            > “Auto-detected & editable. For MVP, only UK is active; more countries can be added later with no layout change.”
            > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.3 Section 2 — Contact Information (Shared)**
    
    Fields:
    
    - Email
        - Show “Verified ✓” or “Verify” link
    - Phone
        - with “Verified / Not Verified” chip
    - Preferred Contact Method:
        - Email
        - SMS
        - WhatsApp
    
    Small hint:
    
    > “We only share your details when it’s needed to progress your viewing or offer.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.4 Section 3 — Notifications (Shared)**
    
    Toggles:
    
    - Viewing reminders
    - New messages
    - Offer / Application updates
    - Price changes for saved places *(only shown if role = homeHunter)*
    - Service & billing notifications *(only shown if role = owner)*
    - “Tips & product news” (marketing opt-in)
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.5 Section 4 — Security (Shared)**
    
    - Change Password
    - 2FA (placeholder, Phase 2)
    - “Log out of all devices” (Phase 2)
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.6 Section 5 — GDPR & Data (Shared)**
    
    - **Request Data Export** (button)
    - **Delete Account** (button)
    - Link: “Read our GDPR & Safety policy”
    
    ---
    
    ## **8. Owner-only Block (Conditional)**
    
    > Show only when role === "owner"
    > 
    
    ### **8.1 Billing & Subscription**
    
    - Current plan:
        - e.g. “Starter / Pro / Full Service”
    - Renewal date & charge:
        - e.g. “Next billing: 12 Apr 2026 — £29/month”
    - Buttons:
        - [Update Payment Method]
        - [Download Invoices]
        - [Upgrade Plan]
    
    ---
    
    ### **8.2 Integrations**
    
    List:
    
    - Google Calendar — Connected / Not Connected
    - WhatsApp (Twilio) — Connected / Setup Pending
    - Airtable / Internal CRM — Connected / Not Connected
    
    Buttons per integration:
    
    - [Connect] / [Disconnect] / [Configure]
    
    ---
    
    ### **8.3**
    
    ### **Your Services & Add-ons (Owner Services)**
    
    This ties into Admin **Tasks & Fulfilment**.
    
    Show per listing:
    
    **Example block**
    
    > Your Services for 12 King Street
    > 
    - ✓ Professional Photos — Completed (12 Mar)
    - ✓ Floorplan — Delivered (PDF)
    - ⧗ For Sale Sign — Scheduled (18 Mar, 10:00)
    - ○ Pre-Sale Survey — Not ordered
    
    > 
    > 
    
    > [Order More Services]
    > 
    
    Designer notes:
    
    - Use a simple card per **Place** with a list of service items.
    - Status pills: Not ordered / Ordered / Scheduled / Completed.
    
    Developer model (concept):
    
    ```
    {
      "serviceId": "srv1",
      "ownerId": "o1",
      "propertyId": "p1",
      "type": "photos | floorplan | sign | epc | presale_survey",
      "status": "not_ordered | ordered | scheduled | completed",
      "scheduledFor": "2026-03-18T10:00:00Z"
    }
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **9. Home-Hunter-only Block (Conditional)**
    
    > Show only when role === "homeHunter"
    > 
    
    ### **9.1 Buying Position**
    
    Dropdown:
    
    - Cash Buyer
    - Mortgage in Principle
    - Mortgage in Progress
    - Just Browsing
    
    Hint:
    
    > “Owners are more likely to accept offers from buyers with a clear buying position.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **9.2 Documents (Phase 2, but space reserved)**
    
    Slots:
    
    - ID (passport / driving licence)
    - Proof of address
    - Mortgage in Principle (upload)
    - Proof of income (for renting)
    
    Statuses: “Not uploaded / Uploaded / Verified”.
    
    ---
    
    ### **9.3**
    
    ### **Purchased Surveys**
    
    This ties to WF-H4/H5 and Admin WF-A6 (Survey Marketplace).
    
    List:
    
    > Your Surveys
    > 
    - 12 King Street — RICS Level 2 — Purchased on 5 Mar
        
        > [Download Report]
        > 
        
        > [View Property]
        > 
    
    > 
    > 
    
    > If none:
    > 
    
    > “You haven’t unlocked any surveys yet.”
    > 
    
    > [See available surveys when viewing places]
    > 
    
    Developer model (concept):
    
    ```
    {
      "surveyId": "sv1",
      "userId": "hh1",
      "propertyId": "p1",
      "type": "level_2 | level_3 | valuation_only",
      "purchasedAt": "2026-03-05T10:00:00Z",
      "downloadUrl": "..."
    }
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **10. Developer Requirements (Key Points)**
    
    - Use **GeoIP** at first login to set country, fallback to "United Kingdom":
    
    ```
    const defaultCountry = request.geo?.country || "United Kingdom";
    ```
    
    - 
    - Only show extra countries in dropdown later when ready (DE, etc.).
    - Use **role-based rendering** for Owner vs Home-Hunter sections.
    - Connect **Owner Services** to:
        - Orders created from Services & Pricing page
        - Admin task board (WF-A4)
    - Connect **Purchased Surveys** to:
        - Survey marketplace logic (WF-A6, HH flows)
    - All labels must use **translation keys** (i18n-ready).
    
    ---
    
    ## **11. KPIs (for Admin / Founder)**
    
    - % of users with:
        - Verified phone
        - Completed personal details
        - Set buying position (HH)
        - Active integrations (Owner)
    - Services per Owner per listing
    - Surveys purchased per Home-Hunter
    - Correlation:
        - Profile completeness → Offer acceptance
        - Survey purchases → Offer conversions
    
    ---
    
    ## **12. Permission Logic (Summary Table)**
    
    | **Area** | **Guest** | **Home-Hunter** | **Owner** | **Admin** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Personal details | ✖ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Contact info | ✖ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Notifications | ✖ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |

    | Owner services & add-ons | ✖ | ✖ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Buying position | ✖ | ✔ | ✖ | ✔ |
    | HH documents & surveys | ✖ | ✔ | ✖ | ✔ |

    ---
    
- Wireframes (Owner, Home-hunter, Admin, Public)
    
    This section contains all wireframes for the full NoAgent product. To keep this structured and easy to navigate. We have four **groups**:
    
    ---
    
    - **🧩 WF O1- 4 +1 Wireframes & UX (Owner)** (selling / renting a place)
        - **🧩 WF-O1 — Owner Dashboard (Command Center)**
            
            > One clean page that shows: performance, buyer quality, viewing pipeline, and actions.
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **0. GLOBAL REQUIRED UI COMPONENTS (ALWAYS PRESENT)**
            
            | **Element** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Header** | Yalla.House (Yalla Yellow) · Services & Pricing · About · List Your Place — fixed at top. |
            | **Owner Sidebar** | Dashfolio+ standard: Dashboard (active) · My Listings · Inquiries (with badge) · Calendar · Documents · Settings. Login / Account sits at **top of sidebar** (Dashfolio default). |
            | **Footer** | Links to: Privacy Policy · Terms of Service · Cookie Policy · GDPR & Safety · Imprint (DE) · Support (email) · WhatsApp (chat link). |
            | **Theme** | Dashfolio+ dark theme, Plus Jakarta Sans, Yalla Yellow highlights. |
            
            ---
            
            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ```jsx
            ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Services & Pricing | About | List Your Place      │
            └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌───────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ SIDEBAR        │  OWNER DASHBOARD                                      │
            │  Dashboard ●   │  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────     │
            │  My Listings   │                                                       │
            │  Inquiries     │   ┌───────────────────── KPI ROW ───────────────────┐ │
            │  Calendar      │   │  [Views]  [Inquiries]  [Viewings] [Offers/Apps] │ │
            │  Documents     │   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │  Settings      │                                                       │
            │                │                                                       │
            │                │   ┌───────────────── FUNNEL CHART ──────────────────┐ │
            │                │   │   Views → Inquiries → Viewings → (Offers/Apps)  │ │
            │                │   │   → Converted                                   │ │
            │                │   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │                │                                                       │
            │                │   ┌──────────── SOURCE BREAKDOWN (Pie/Donut) ──────┐ │
            │                │   │  Yalla · Rightmove · Zoopla · WhatsApp · QR     │ │
            │                │   │  Direct · Unknown                               │ │
            │                │   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │                │                                                       │
            │                │   ┌──────────────── RECENT ACTIVITY FEED ──────────┐ │
            │                │   │  • New inquiry — Sarah L (Verified, Cash)       │ │
            │                │   │  • WhatsApp contact yesterday                   │ │
            │                │   │  • Viewing booked by Omar (Sat 11am)            │ │
            │                │   │  • Offer £612,500 submitted                     │ │
            │                │   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │                │                                                       │
            │                │   ┌──────────────── QUICK ACTIONS ─────────────────┐ │
            │                │   │  [Add New Place]  [Manage Listings]  [Calendar]│ │
            │                │   └────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            └───────────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ FOOTER: Privacy Policy · Terms · Cookies · GDPR/Safety · Imprint · Help │
            └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **A1. Purpose**
            
            | **Goal** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Give Owner instant clarity on how their sale/rental is performing. |
            | 2 | Highlight **buyer quality** (verified, cash/mortgage, renting position). |
            | 3 | Show where interest comes from (Yalla, portals, WhatsApp, QR, etc.). |
            | 4 | Make next actions obvious: reply to messages, schedule viewings, adjust listing. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A2. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            | **Step** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Owner logs in → lands directly on **Dashboard**. |
            | 2 | Sees KPIs for views, inquiries, viewings, offers/applications, conversions. |
            | 3 | Glances at funnel and source breakdown to understand performance. |
            | 4 | Checks **Recent Activity** to see latest inquiries, viewings, offers/applications. |
            | 5 | Clicks **Inquiries**, **Calendar** or **My Listings** to take action. |
            
            **Entry from:**
            
            - Sidebar → Dashboard
            - After finishing first listing in WF-O2 (“Ready to Publish”)
            - After login redirect
            - In future: from email link “Go to your dashboard”
            
            **Exit to:**
            
            - My Listings (WF-O2)
            - Inquiries (WF-O3)
            - Calendar (WF-O4)
            - Account Settings (WF-ACC via account area in sidebar)
            
            Dashboard = **daily home base**.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A3. UI Components List**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** | **Notes for Designer** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | **KPI Row (4 cards)** | Views, Inquiries, Viewings, Offers/Applications. | Each card: big number, small label, small trend arrow (+X% vs last week). |
            | **Buyer Status Chips** | Chips like “Verified”, “Cash”, “Mortgage ready”, “Employed (Docs Ready)” etc. used in Recent Activity. | Style as small, pill-shaped, colour-coded chips. |
            | **Channel Icons** | Icons for Inbox, WhatsApp, Viewing. | Used in activity feed and possibly small legends. |
            | **Funnel Chart** | Horizontal funnel: Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers/Applications → Converted. | Single component; labels switch automatically between Sale and Rent wording. |
            | **Source Breakdown Chart** | Pie/donut or bar chart of traffic sources. | Legend: Yalla.House, Rightmove, Zoopla, WhatsApp, QR Signboard, Direct, Other. |
            | **Recent Activity Feed** | Vertical list of last 5–10 events. | Icon + text + timestamp + badges (buyer chips). |
            | **Quick Actions Block** | Buttons: “Add New Place”, “Manage Listings”, “View Calendar”. | “Add New Place” = primary (Yalla Yellow). Others secondary/ghost. |
            | **Sidebar (Owner)** | Standard Dashfolio sidebar with Dashboard highlighted and Inquiries with badge (e.g. ●3). | No redesign needed; just show active state. |
            | **Mobile Layout** | Stacked layout: KPIs → Funnel → Sources → Activity → Quick Actions. | No side-by-side grids; keep it simple. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4. KPI Definitions (Owner-Friendly Microcopy)**
            
            | **KPI** | **UI Label** | **Owner-facing explanation** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Views | “Views (last 7 days)” | How many times people opened your property page in the last 7 days. |
            | Inquiries | “Inquiries” | How many people contacted you (Yalla inbox + WhatsApp). |
            | Verified Inquiries | Shown as subtext: “22 verified” | How many of those inquiries are from buyers/renters who verified their phone number. |
            | Viewings | “Viewings” | How many visits are booked (upcoming + completed). Includes **private & open house** viewings. |
            | Offers | “Offers” | (Sale) How many purchase offers have been submitted. |
            | Applications | “Applications” | (Rent) How many rental applications have been submitted. |
            | Converted | “Converted” | Accepted offers (sale) or approved applications (rent). |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A5. Funnel & Sources (Designer Detail)**
            
            ### **A5.1 Funnel Variants (same visual, different labels)**
            
            | **Mode** | **Steps** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Sale** | Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Accepted Offer |
            | **Rent** | Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Applications → Approved |
            
            Designer: keep the **same component**, just swap the labels “Offers / Applications / Accepted / Approved” depending on context.
            
            ### **A5.2 Source Breakdown Segments**
            
            | **Source Key** | **Label in UI** |
            | --- | --- |
            | yalla | “Yalla.House” |
            | rightmove | “Rightmove” |
            | zoopla | “Zoopla” |
            | whatsapp | “WhatsApp” |
            | qrcode | “Yalla Signboard (QR)” |
            | direct | “Direct share (link)” |
            | unknown | “Other / Unknown” |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A6. Dummy Content (Use in Figma / Framer)**
            
            **KPI row (Sale example)**
            
            - Views: **1,247** (↑ 18%)
            - Inquiries: **36** (22 verified)
            - Viewings: **4 upcoming / 7 completed**
            - Offers: **1 active**
            - Converted: **1 accepted**
            
            **KPI row (Rent example)**
            
            - Views: **1,031** (↑ 9%)
            - Inquiries: **24** (15 verified)
            - Viewings: **3**
            - Applications: **3**
            - Converted: **2 approved**
            
            **Funnel (Sale example)**
            
            - 4,562 Views
            - 123 Inquiries
            - 17 Viewings
            - 3 Offers
            - 1 Accepted
            
            **Funnel (Rent example)**
            
            - 4,112 Views
            - 98 Inquiries
            - 14 Viewings
            - 4 Applications
            - 2 Approved
            
            **Recent Activity Examples**
            
            - “New inquiry from **Sarah L. (Verified, Cash Buyer)** — 2h ago”
            - “**3 WhatsApp contacts** yesterday”
            - “Viewing booked — **Omar R. · 12 King Street · Sat 9 Nov · 11:00**”
            - “**Offer submitted** £612,500 (awaiting reply)”
            - “**Application received** — Jessica K. (Employment Verified)”
            
            ---
            
            ### **A7. Rental Logic (Integrated — No Separate Layout)**
            
            | **Area** | **Sale Behaviour** | **Rent Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | KPI #4 | “Offers” card | “Applications” card |
            | Funnel step 4 | “Offers” | “Applications” |
            | Funnel last step | “Accepted Offer” | “Approved Application” |
            | Activity text | “Offer submitted / accepted” | “Application received / approved” |
            | Buyer chips | Cash, Mortgage ready, Mortgage in progress, Just browsing | Employed (Docs Ready), Student (Guarantor Ready), Self-employed (Docs Ready), Just browsing |
            | Viewing logic | Same — both use Calendar WF-O4 | Same — both use Calendar WF-O4 |
            
            Designer: **one screen**, auto-labelled based on listing mix.
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ### **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            | **Behaviour** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Aggregation scope | All KPIs, funnel steps and sources are aggregated across **all active listings** for this Owner. |
            | Sale vs Rent mode | If Owner only has rent properties, labels use “Applications/Approved”. If mixed, aggregate counts but still use neutral wording like “Offers / Applications” in UI. |
            | Time range | MVP: last 7 days. Keep configurable in backend (e.g. windowDays = 7 for now). |
            | Inquiry aggregation | inquiries = inbox inquiries + WhatsApp contacts (WhatsApp only counted as events with timestamp, no message body). |
            | Verified flag | verifiedInquiries includes only buyers/renters with phoneVerified = true from Home-Hunter profile. |
            | Viewings | viewingsUpcoming + viewingsCompleted include both **private viewings** and **open house slots** from Calendar WF-O4. |
            | Onboarding state | If Owner has 0 listings → API should mark hasListings=false; UI shows an onboarding tile instead of charts. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B2. API / Data Model Requirements**
            
            ```
            OwnerDashboardData {
              hasListings: boolean
            
              kpis: {
                totalViews7d: number
                inquiries: number
                verifiedInquiries: number
                whatsappOnly: number
                viewingsUpcoming: number
                viewingsCompleted: number
                offers: number        // sale only
                applications: number  // rent only
                converted: number     // accepted offers or approved applications
              }
            
              funnel: {
                views: number
                inquiries: number
                viewings: number
                offersOrApplications: number
                converted: number
              }
            
              sources: {
                rightmove: number
                zoopla: number
                yalla: number
                whatsapp: number
                qrcode: number
                direct: number
                unknown: number
              }
            
              recentActivity: ActivityEvent[]
            }
            ```
            
            ```
            ActivityEvent {
              id: string
              type: "inquiry" | "viewing" | "offer" | "application" | "whatsapp" | "system"
              timestamp: number
              title: string               // human-readable text
              meta?: Record<string, any>  // optional deep link ids, etc.
            }
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **B3. Calculations (Funnel & KPIs)**
            
            | **Metric** | **Formula** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Inquiry Rate | inquiries / views |
            | Viewing Rate | viewings / inquiries |
            | Offer Rate (sale) | offers / viewings |
            | Application Rate (rent) | applications / viewings |
            | Conversion Rate | converted / offersOrApplications |
            
            For MVP, these can be **either** computed in backend **or** client if numbers are small. No need to expose separate % fields yet; raw counts are enough.
            
            ---
            
            ### **B4. Integrations**
            
            | **Integration** | **How O1 Uses It** |
            | --- | --- |
            | WhatsApp | Each click from WF-H1 or WF-O5 that opens WhatsApp creates an ActivityEvent (type="whatsapp") and increments sources.whatsapp and kpis.inquiries. No message bodies stored. |
            | Calendar (Google / internal) | Used to compute viewingsUpcoming and viewingsCompleted, including both private and open house slots from WF-O4. |
            | Portals (Rightmove, Zoopla) | MVP: track source using links/UTM or partner callback — just enough to increment sources.rightmove / sources.zoopla. Full sync is Phase 2. |
            | QR Signboard | QR code resolves to URL with source=qrcode so page views and inquiries can be attributed to qrcode. |
            | Stripe (Phase 2) | Not required for MVP dashboard. Later can expose revenue-based KPIs here. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B5. Event Tracking**
            
            Fire minimal analytics events:
            
            - dashboard_loaded (on page load, once)
            - dashboard_widget_clicked (with widgetId = kpi_views, kpi_inquiries, funnel, sources, etc.)
            - dashboard_chart_viewed (if user hovers or opens chart details)
            
            These feed into Admin Analytics (WF-A9) later.
            
            ---
            
            ### **B6. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Expected Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | hasListings=false | Show onboarding tile “Start by listing your first place” with CTA → WF-O2 Step 1. No charts or KPIs. |
            | No activity yet | KPIs = 0, funnel = 0s, sources = 0. Show helper copy: “No activity yet — share your link or order a Yalla signboard to get more views.” |
            | Only rent or only sale | OK — use appropriate naming and keep combined funnel. |
            | Buyer deletes account (GDPR) | RecentActivity strips name/email, but aggregated counts stay intact (still part of KPIs). |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B7. Phase 2 Ideas (Not Required Now)**
            
            | **Idea** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Per-listing drilldowns | Clicking a listing in O1 jumps to dedicated mini-dashboard for that place. |
            | “Compared to local market” | Use external data to show “Top 20% in IG1 for 3-bed houses”. |
            | Smart suggestions | AI hints: “Update photos”, “Consider adjusting price”, “Boost on Rightmove”. |
            | Revenue overlay | For subscription users, show what they’ve spent vs what they saved vs typical agent fees. |
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O2 — Owner “My Listings” Page**
            
            > The place where Owners **create, see, manage** (and where the **first-time listing flow)**
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ```jsx
            ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Services & Pricing | About | List Your Place       │
            └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

            │ SIDEBAR        │  MY LISTINGS                                             │

            │  My Listings ● │                                                          │
            │  Inquiries     │   ┌────────────── TOP BAR ────────────────────────────┐ │
            │  Calendar      │   │  [Add New Place]   [Sort: Active | Draft | Hidden]│ │
            │  Documents     │   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │  Settings      │                                                          │
            │                │                                                          │
            │                │   ┌──────────────────── LISTINGS GRID ─────────────────┐ │
            │                │   │  [Listing Card 1]  [Listing Card 2]  [Card 3...]  │ │
            │                │   │                                                   │ │
            │                │   │  Each card shows:                                 │ │
            │                │   │   • Cover photo                                   │ │
            │                │   │   • Short address                                 │ │
            │                │   │   • Badge: For Sale / For Rent                    │ │
            │                │   │   • Status: Active / Draft / Hidden               │ │
            │                │   │   • Mini KPIs: Views · Inquiries · Viewings       │ │
            │                │   │   • Buttons: Edit · View Public Page · Inquiries  │ │
            │                │   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │                │                                                          │
            │                │   ┌──────────── EMPTY STATE (if 0 listings) ──────────┐ │
            │                │   │  “You haven’t listed a place yet.”                │ │
            │                │   │  [List your first place]                           │ │
            │                │   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            └───────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ FOOTER: Privacy Policy · Terms · Cookies · GDPR/Safety · Imprint · Help  │
            └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            ## **0. GLOBAL REQUIRED UI COMPONENTS**
            
            | **Element** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Header** | Yalla.House (Yalla Yellow) · Services & Pricing · About · List Your Place — fixed at top. |
            | **Owner Sidebar** | Dashboard · **My Listings (active)** · Inquiries (with badge) · Calendar · Documents · Settings. Login / Account at top of sidebar (Dashfolio default). |
            | **Footer** | Privacy Policy · Terms · Cookies · GDPR & Safety · Imprint (DE) · Support (email) · WhatsApp link. |
            | **Theme** | Dashfolio+ dark theme, Plus Jakarta Sans, Yalla Yellow accents. |
            
            ---
            
            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **A1. Purpose**
            
            | **Goal** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Give Owners **one place** to see and manage all their places. |
            | 2 | Make it **trivial to start a new listing** (first-time wizard). |
            | 3 | Show **high-level performance** per listing (views, inquiries, viewings, offers/applications). |
            | 4 | Keep the page usable for **both Sale and Rent** listings, no extra layout. |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A2. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            | **Step** | **Experience** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Owner clicks **My Listings** in sidebar (or is redirected here after creating a place). |
            | 2 | If they have **0 listings**, they see a friendly “Start your first place” panel. |
            | 3 | If they have listings, they see a **grid or table of cards** (one per place). |
            | 4 | They can **add new place**, edit an existing one, see inquiries, or open the calendar for a specific place. |
            | 5 | First-time create/edit uses the **lightweight 4-step flow** (Basics → Price → Extras → Ready to Publish). |
            
            **Entry from:**
            
            - Sidebar → *My Listings*
            - O1 Dashboard → “Manage Listings”
            - After finishing Step 4 of the wizard (redirect back here)
            
            **Exit to:**
            
            - WF-O1 Dashboard
            - WF-O3 Inquiries (filtered by a listing)
            - WF-O4 Calendar (filtered by a listing)
            
            ---
            
            ## **A3. UI Components (Page Layout)**
            
            ### **A3.1 Top Bar**
            
            - Page title: **My Listings**
            - Search box: “Search by address or place name”
            - Filter chips:
                - All · Active · Draft · Paused · Sold · Let Agreed
            - Button (primary): **Add New Place**
            
            ---
            
            ### **A3.2 Listing Cards / Table**
            
            Designer can choose **grid of cards** or **table with richer rows** (Dashfolio style).
            
            Each listing row/card shows:
            
            - Thumbnail image (first photo or placeholder)
            - Title: 12 King Street
            - Short address / area: Ilford · IG1
            - Chips:
                - **For Sale / For Rent**
                - Status: Active / Draft / Paused / Sold / Let Agreed
            - Mini stats (last 7 days):
                - Views: 241
                - Inquiries: 7 (4 verified)
                - Viewings: 2 upcoming
                - Offers / Applications: 1
            - Quick actions (buttons or icon row):
                - **Edit Listing**
                - **View Inquiries**
                - **Open Calendar**
                - **Duplicate**
                - **Pause / Resume**
                - **Delete** (in overflow menu, not as main CTA)
            
            ---
            
            ### **A3.3 First-Time Empty State (0 Listings)**
            
            If Owner has **no places yet**, replace list with:
            
            - Large card:
            
            > “Let’s list your first place”
            > 
            
            > "No agents. No fees. No catch."
            > 
            
            > CTA:
            > 
            > 
            > **Start Listing**
            > 
            
            > Subtext: “It takes a few minutes. You can add photos and documents later.”
            > 
            
            Click → opens **First-Time Listing Flow** (A4).
            
            ---
            
            ## **A4. First-Time Listing Flow (4 Steps, in a side-panel / modal)**
            
            > This is the
            > 
            > 
            > **lightweight “wizard”**
            > 
            
            **Progress bar (always visible):**
            
            > Step 1 — Basics → Step 2 — Price → Step 3 — Extras → Step 4 — Ready to Publish
            > 
            
            Designer: show as a simple horizontal bar with step labels and current step highlighted in **Yalla Yellow**.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4.1 Step 1 — Basics (Address & Type)**
            
            **Fields:**
            
            - (Pre-filled, read-only): Email (from login)
            - (Optional for MVP): First Name, Last Name
                
                > Microcopy: “You can add your details later in Settings.”
                > 
            - **Postcode**
                - UK: type → drop-down **address suggestions**
                - DE: fallback: manually type Street, House No., City, Postcode
            - **Full address** (resolved or manual)
            - **Listing type**: Sale / Rent
            - **Property type**: Flat / House / Maisonette / Other
            
            **UX:**
            
            - As soon as Owner saves Step 1, the system creates:
                - a **Draft** listing
                - a unique **Property ID** (see B3)
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4.2 Step 2 — Price**
            
            **If Sale:**
            
            - Currency: dropdown (£ / € initially)
            - **Asking price** (numeric)
            - Tenure: Freehold / Leasehold / Share of Freehold / Commonhold
            
            Microcopy:
            
            > “You can adjust the price anytime if interest is too high or low.”
            > 
            
            **If Rent:**
            
            - Currency: dropdown (£ / €)
            - **Rent per month**
            - **Deposit**
            - **Minimum term (months)**
            
            Labels auto-switch based on Sale vs Rent.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4.3 Step 3 — Extras (Optional)**
            
            Keep this light for MVP:
            
            - Beds (dropdown)
            - Baths (dropdown)
            - Short description (multi-line)
            - Photo upload area:
                - “Drag & drop or click to add photos”
                - Hint: “You can skip this for now, but listings with photos get more views.”
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4.4 Step 4 — Ready to Publish**
            
            Show a **review card**:
            
            - Address + small map snippet
            - Listing type (Sale / Rent)
            - Price or Rent per month
            - Status: Draft
            
            Buttons:
            
            - **Publish now** (if required fields met)
            - **Save as draft and finish later**
            
            After action:
            
            - Redirect back to **My Listings** list view with the new row highlighted.
            
            ---

            Use these in Figma:
            
            **Card Example (Sale)**

            > 
            
            > Active
            >

            >
