            ## **A6. Rental Logic (Designer)**
            
            | **Element** | **Sale** | **Rent** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Label | “For Sale” | “For Rent” |
            | Price line | “Asking price: £650,000” | “Rent: £1,900 / month” |
            | Mini stat label | “Offers” | “Applications” |
            | Future badge (optional) | “Sold” | “Let Agreed” |
            
            Same layout → just change wording.
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            | **Behaviour** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Single endpoint | One API call returns all listings for the Owner (with stats summary). |
            | First-time logic | If listings.length === 0, front-end shows empty-state tile instead of table. |
            | Status model | Listing status drives visibility in public pages (O5) and portals. |
            | Soft delete | Deleting should be **soft** (for data integrity & audits). |
            | Wizard is idempotent | Owner can leave after any step; listing remains in Draft until published. |
            | Stats alignment | views7d, inquiries7d, viewingsUpcoming must match O1 dashboard totals. |
            | Sale vs Rent | propertyType determines which fields are required and which labels to show. |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2. API: Listing Summary**
            
            ```
            MyListingsResponse {
              listings: ListingSummary[]
            }
            
            ListingSummary {
              id: string              // propertyId
              ownerId: string
            
              title: string           // e.g. "12 King Street"
              addressShort: string    // "Ilford · IG1"
              fullAddress: string
              propertyType: "sale" | "rent"
              propertyCategory: "flat" | "house" | "maisonette" | "other"
            
              status: "draft" | "active" | "paused" | "sold" | "let_agreed"
            
              pricing: {
                currency: string      // "GBP" | "EUR"
                askingPrice?: number  // sale
                rentPerMonth?: number // rent
                deposit?: number      // rent
                tenure?: "freehold" | "leasehold" | "share_of_freehold" | "commonhold"
              }
            
              stats: {
                views7d: number
                inquiries7d: number
                verifiedInquiries7d: number
                viewingsUpcoming: number
                offers?: number
                applications?: number
              }
            
              hasOpenHouse: boolean
              thumbnailUrl?: string
            }
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3. Property ID Logic**
            
            | **Rule** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Immutable | id is created after Step 1 (Basics) and never changes. |
            | Cross-system key | Same id is used in O1, O3, O4, O5, HH journeys, Admin, analytics. |
            | Prefix (optional) | Optionally encode locale: e.g. UK-xxxxx, DE-xxxxx. (Phase 2). |
            | Draft from start | Once Step 1 saved → listing record exists in DB with status="draft". |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4. First-Time Wizard Data (Backend expectations)**
            
            **Step 1 payload (Basics):**
            
            ```
            CreateListingRequest {
              postcode: string
              countryCode: "UK" | "DE"
              addressLine1?: string
              addressLine2?: string
              city: string
              listingType: "sale" | "rent"
              propertyCategory: "flat" | "house" | "maisonette" | "other"
            }
            ```
            
            Return:
            
            ```
            CreateListingResponse {
              propertyId: string
              status: "draft"
            }
            ```
            
            Subsequent steps: **PATCH** the same propertyId:
            
            - Step 2: /listings/:id/pricing
            - Step 3: /listings/:id/details
            - Step 4: /listings/:id/publish or /pause, etc.
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5. Developer Tooling Overview (MVP)**
            
            | **Tool / Concern** | **Notes** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Validation | Ensure basic validation: postcode, positive prices, required fields for publish. |
            | i18n | Keep labels and copy as translation keys (en-GB first, DE later). |
            | Analytics | Events: listing_created, listing_published, listing_paused, listing_deleted. |
            | GDPR | When Owner requests deletion, listing can be anonymised but kept for stats. |
            | Error states | If portal sync fails (Phase 2), show non-blocking warnings, not hard errors here. |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B6. Rental Logic (Developer)**
            
            - Same ListingSummary type; rental just uses:
                - pricing.rentPerMonth, pricing.deposit, pricing.minimumTerm.
            - Stats:
                - applications instead of offers for renters.
            - The wizard:
                - listingType="rent" → require rent fields before publish.
            - O3 (Inquiries) and O4 (Calendar) logic already support Sale/Rent, no extra branching here.
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O3 — Owner Inquiries (Messaging Hub)**
            
            > Owner’s central place for **all interest,  Sale, Rent**
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **0. GLOBAL UI (ALWAYS PRESENT)**
            
            | **Element** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Header | Yalla.House (Yalla Yellow) · Services & Pricing · About · List Your Place — fixed at top. |
            | Owner Sidebar | Dashboard · My Listings · **Inquiries (● badge)** · Calendar · Documents · Settings. Login / Account at top of sidebar (Dashfolio default). |
            | Footer | Privacy Policy · Terms · Cookies · GDPR & Safety · Imprint (DE) · Support · WhatsApp. |
            | Theme | Dashfolio+ dark theme, Plus Jakarta Sans, Yalla Yellow accents. |
            
            ---
            
            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ### **A1. Visual Layout**
            
            ```
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Services & Pricing | About | List Place │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌───────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │  SIDEBAR      │  INQUIRIES (TITLE + FILTERS)                  │
            │  Dashboard    │  ───────────────────────────────────────────  │
            │  My Listings  │  [All][New][Replied][Viewings][Offers/Apps]  │
            │  Inquiries ●3 │  [Archived]   [Verified only ☐]  [Search…]    │
            │  Calendar     │                                               │
            │  Documents    │  ┌─────────────────┬────────────────────────┐ │
            │  Settings     │  │ INQUIRY LIST    │ CONVERSATION PANEL     │ │
            │               │  │ (left)          │ (right)                │ │
            │               │  │ Buyer + badges  │ Header: Buyer + chips  │ │
            │               │  │ Property + icons│ Property + For Sale/Rent││
            │               │  │ Status + unread │ Info strip              │ │
            │               │  │                 │ ─────────────────────── │ │
            │               │  │                 │ Message thread OR       │ │
            │               │  │                 │ WhatsApp-only banner    │ │
            │               │  │                 │ ─────────────────────── │ │
            │               │  │                 │ Reply box + actions     │ │
            │               │  └─────────────────┴────────────────────────┘ │
            └───────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            - Desktop: split layout as above.
            - Mobile: list → tap → full-screen conversation → back to list.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A2. Purpose**
            
            This page gives Owners:
            
            - One **central place** to manage all buyer/renter interest per listing.
            - At-a-glance **quality signals**: Verified, Cash / Mortgage ready, Renting position.
            - Visibility of **channel**: Inbox / WhatsApp / Viewing.
            - Simple ways to **reply**, **propose viewing**, or **mark resolved**.
            - A **single screen** that works for both **Sale** and **Rent**.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A3. User Journey (Owner)**
            
            **Entry points**
            
            - Sidebar → **Inquiries**
            - Dashboard (O1) → “New inquiries” widget → “View all”
            - My Listings (O2) → “View inquiries” for a place
            - Calendar (O4) → click viewing → “Open inquiry”
            - Sidebar badge “Inquiries (3)” → this page
            
            **Flow**
            
            1. Owner opens Inquiries → sees **latest activity first**.
            2. Uses filters (New, Viewings, Offers/Applications, Verified only) to prioritise.
            3. Clicks an inquiry:
                - Sees buyer name, **Verified** chip, buying/renting position chip.
                - Sees channel: Inbox / WhatsApp / Viewing-only.
                - Sees either message thread or WhatsApp-only banner.
            4. Replies, proposes a viewing slot, or marks inquiry as resolved.
            5. Optionally jumps:
                - to Calendar (to see all viewings for that listing),
                - to My Listings (edit price/details),
                - to Public Page (WF-O5 preview).
            
            **Exit paths**
            
            - To **Calendar (WF-O4)**
            - To **My Listings (WF-O2)**
            - To **Public Property Page (WF-O5)**
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4. UI Components**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** | **Designer Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Filter bar | Pills: All · New · Replied · Viewings · Offers/Applications · Archived + “Verified only” toggle. | Show count inside or next to pill (optional). |
            | Search bar | Search by buyer name, email, property. | Top-right above list. |
            | Inquiry row | Buyer name, verification badge, position chip, property name, icons (Inbox/WhatsApp/Viewing), unread count, last activity time. | MUST show **Verified** chip if phoneVerified; position chip always visible if set. |
            | Buyer header | Name + chip (Verified/Unverified) + buying/renting position chip. | Use same chip styles as elsewhere. |
            | Info strip | Phone (masked), email, last channel, last activity time. | Compact row under header. |
            | In-app thread | Bubble chat layout. | Buyer left, Owner right, date dividers. |
            | WhatsApp-only banner | For enquiries that have no inbox messages. | Prominent, neutral: explain privacy. |
            | Reply box | Textarea + primary “Send reply”. | Below thread. |
            | Action buttons | “Propose viewing time”, “Mark as resolved”, maybe “Log note”. | “Send reply” = primary; others secondary. |
            | Rental variations | Offers → Applications; buying → renting chips. | Same layout, different labels. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A5. Dummy Text**
            
            **Filter bar**
            
            > All · New (3) · Replied · Viewings · Offers/Applications (1) · Archived
            > 
            
            > [Verified only ☐] · [Search buyer or address…]
            > 
            
            **Inquiry rows**
            
            - Sarah L. · Verified · Cash Buyer
                
                12 King Street · For Sale · Inbox · 2 unread · 1h ago
                
            - Omar R. · Verified · Mortgage ready
                
                45 Oak Road · For Sale · WhatsApp + Viewing · 0 unread · 2d ago
                
            - Jessica K. · Verified · Employed (Docs Ready)
                
                Flat — 14 Baker Street · For Rent · Inbox · 1 unread · 3h ago
                
            
            **WhatsApp-only banner**
            
            > This buyer contacted you via WhatsApp.
            > 
            
            > We don’t store WhatsApp conversations, but you can see their profile and viewing history.
            > 
            
            **Header example (sale)**
            
            > Sarah L. — Verified — Cash Buyer
            > 
            
            > Enquiry for
            > 
            > 
            > **12 King Street (For Sale)**
            > 
            
            **Header example (rent)**
            
            > Jessica K. — Verified — Employed (Docs Ready)
            > 
            
            > Enquiry for
            > 
            > 
            > **Flat — 14 Baker Street (For Rent)**
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **A6. Rental Logic (Fully Included)**
            
            | **Area** | **Sale behaviour** | **Rent behaviour** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Property badge | “For Sale” chip | “For Rent” chip |
            | Position chip | Cash, Mortgage ready, Mortgage in progress, Just browsing | Employed (Docs Ready), Student (Guarantor Ready), Self-employed (Docs Ready), Just browsing |
            | Filter pill | “Offers/Applications” includes offers only | “Offers/Applications” includes applications only |
            | Status | Offer in status/row | Application in status/row |
            | Activity snippets | “Offer submitted: £612,500” | “Application received from Jessica K. (Pending review)” |
            | Viewing | Same logic, same UI | Same logic, same UI |
            | WhatsApp banner | Same text | Same text |
            
            No extra layouts. Only text/label variants.
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ### **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            ### **B1.1 Filter Logic**
            
            | **Filter** | **Condition (example)** |
            | --- | --- |
            | All | status != ‘archived’ |
            | New | status IN (‘new’, ‘unread’) |
            | Replied | lastMessageFromOwner = true |
            | Viewings | inquiry has linked viewing record (any future or past) |
            | Offers/Applications | sale: linked Offer exists; rent: linked Application exists |
            | Archived | status = ‘archived’ |
            | Verified only | buyer.phoneVerified = true |
            
            > Exact enums can be adjusted, but behaviour must match the UX.
            > 
            
            ### **B1.2 List → Detail**
            
            - One **thread per Buyer per Listing**:
                
                threadKey = listingId + homeHunterId.
                
            - List rows sorted by lastActivityAt DESC.
            - Opening a row:
                - Marks messages as read (update unreadCount).
                - Loads InquiryDetail (see B3).
            - Buyer gate: in normal flow, all inquiries originate from WF-H1 (Home-Hunter Gate) → buyer is **phoneVerified** + has buying/renting position set. Legacy/manual ones may be unverified.
            
            ### **B1.3 Navigation**
            
            | **Click Source** | **Destination / Action** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Inquiry row | Load InquiryDetail in right panel. |
            | Property name | Open WF-O2 listing detail (My Listings). |
            | “Propose viewing time” | Open Calendar (WF-O4) mini-modal or route with pre-filtered property. |
            | “View public page” (if added) | Open WF-O5 public property page. |
            | Sidebar → Inquiries | Open O3. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B2. Data Model — List Items**
            
            ```
            type InquiryListItem = {
              id: string
              propertyId: string
              buyerId: string
            
              buyerName: string
              buyerBuyingPosition?: "cash" | "mortgage_ready" | "mortgage_in_progress" | "just_browsing"
              buyerRentingPosition?: "employed_docs_ready" | "student_guarantor_ready" | "self_employed_docs_ready" | "just_browsing"
              buyerPhoneVerified: boolean
            
              propertyTitle: string        // "12 King Street"
              propertyType: "sale" | "rent"
              propertyLabel: string        // "For Sale" | "For Rent"
            
              lastChannel: "inbox" | "whatsapp" | "viewing_only"
              lastActivityAt: number       // timestamp
            
              status: "new" | "unread" | "replied" | "viewing" | "offer" | "application" | "archived"
              unreadCount: number
            }
            ```
            
            **API example**
            
            ```
            GET /owner/inquiries?status=&verifiedOnly=&search=&propertyId=
            → InquiryListItem[]
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **B3. Data Model — Detail & Messages**
            
            ```
            type InquiryDetail = {
              inquiry: InquiryListItem
              messages: InquiryMessage[]
              lastViewing?: ViewingSummary   // from Calendar system
              lastOfferOrApplication?: OfferOrApplicationSummary
            }
            
            type InquiryMessage = {
              id: string
              inquiryId: string
              sender: "owner" | "buyer" | "system"
              channel: "inbox"
              body: string
              createdAt: number
              readAt?: number
            }
            ```
            
            - **WhatsApp**:
                - No message bodies stored.
                - Only event + timestamps in analytics (see B5) and lastChannel = "whatsapp".
            
            ---
            
            ### **B4. Integrations**
            
            | **Integration** | **Role on O3** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Home-Hunter Gate (WF-H1) | Ensures most inquiries come from verified buyers/renters; surfaces buyerBuyingPosition / buyerRentingPosition. |
            | Calendar (WF-O4) | Propose viewing creates/updates a viewing event; O3 shows viewing banner based on lastViewing. |
            | WhatsApp | When Home-hunter taps WhatsApp on public page or in flow, we create an Inquiry with lastChannel="whatsapp" and fire a whatsapp_contact event. No content stored. |
            | Offers / Applications | Linked via lastOfferOrApplication summary (amount, status). |
            | Admin Analytics | Events from O3 feed into A9 (Admin Analytics). |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B5. Events & Analytics**
            
            Fire at least:
            
            - owner_opened_inquiry
                
                { inquiryId, propertyId, buyerId }
                
            - owner_replied_inquiry
            - owner_marked_inquiry_resolved
            - owner_opened_whatsapp_only_inquiry
            - owner_clicked_propose_viewing
            
            These power funnel insights and Admin dashboard.
            
            ---
            
            ### **B6. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Buyer WhatsApps before verifying | Gate should normally prevent this; if created manually, treat as buyerPhoneVerified=false, no Verified chip. |
            | Multiple inquiries same buyer & listing | Merge into same thread (same threadKey). |
            | Listing archived/deleted | Mark related inquiries as archived. Hide from “All” filter; only visible under “Archived”. |
            | Buyer GDPR deletion | Replace buyerName with “Deleted user”, remove contact details, keep aggregated stats and thread stub. |
            | No inquiries | Show empty state with CTA: “No inquiries yet — share your link or add a Yalla signboard to get more views.” |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B7. Phase 2 Enhancements (Not MVP)**
            
            - AI reply suggestions in thread.
            - SLA timers (“Respond within 2 hours”).
            - Multi-select archive / bulk actions.
            - Buyer scoring / lead quality indicators.
            - Conversation sentiment / “hot lead” flags.
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O4 — Owner Calendar (Viewings Manager)**
            
            > The Owner’s full viewing management hub — availability, bookings, rescheduling, cancellations.
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **0 — GLOBAL UI COMPONENTS (ALWAYS PRESENT)**
            
            | **Element** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Header** | Yalla.House · Services · About · List Your Place (frozen at top) |
            | **Owner Sidebar** | Dashboard · My Listings · **Inquiries (badge)** · Calendar (active) · Documents · Settings |
            | **Footer** | Privacy · Terms · Cookies · GDPR · Imprint · Support · WhatsApp |
            | **Theme** | Dashfolio+ dark mode · Yellow accents · Plus Jakarta Sans |
            
            ---
            
            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **A1 — Purpose**
            
            | **Goal** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Let Owners publish **availability** (private slots + open-house windows). |
            | 2 | Auto-confirm all bookings — no approval needed. |
            | 3 | Show all viewings for ALL listings in one place. |
            | 4 | Connect viewings ↔ inquiries ↔ booking confirmations. |
            | 5 | Make cancellation & rescheduling extremely simple. |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A2 — Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            | **Step** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Owner clicks **Calendar** in sidebar. |
            | 2 | Sees Week/Month view with counters (“3 viewings”). |
            | 3 | Selects a day → sees all slots + who is coming. |
            | 4 | Can add new viewing blocks (private or open-house). |
            | 5 | HH bookings appear automatically as **Confirmed (auto)**. |
            | 6 | Owner can message, cancel, or edit time. |
            
            **Entry from:**
            
            Dashboard (viewings widget) · Inquiries (from thread “View in Calendar”) · My Listings
            
            **Exit to:**
            
            Inquiries (message buyer) · Listing page · WF-O5 public page
            
            ---
            
            ## **A3 — Visual Layout (ASCII)**
            
            ```
            ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Services | About | List Your Place     │
            └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌───────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ SIDEBAR        │  CALENDAR (WEEK / MONTH TOGGLE)             │
            │ Dashboard      │──────────────────────────────────────────── │
            │ My Listings    │ [Week] [Month]      Today: ●                │
            │ Inquiries ●3   │ ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
            │ Calendar ●2    │ │  M  T  W  T  F  S  S   (Month Grid)     │ │
            │ Documents      │ │  1  2  3  4  5…                         │ │
            │ Settings       │ │     [2 viewings] marker                 │ │
            │                │ └─────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │                │                                             │
            │                │ SELECTED DAY — VIEWING SLOTS                │
            │                │ ─────────────────────────────────────────── │
            │                │ [Add Viewing Block +]                       │
            │                │                                             │
            │                │ 11:00–13:00  12 King Street  (OPEN-HOUSE)   │
            │                │ 5 confirmed / cap 10   Status: Active       │
            │                │ [View Bookings] [Edit] [Cancel]             │
            │                │                                             │
            │                │ 15:30–16:00  22 Yoxley Drive (PRIVATE)      │
            │                │ 1 confirmed   Status: Active                │
            │                │ [View Booking] [Message] [Cancel]           │
            └────────────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **A4 — UI Components Table**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** | **Designer Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Week/Month Toggle | Switch between monthly grid and weekly strip | Smooth transition • highlight Today |
            | Day Grid | Displays small indicators (“3 viewings”) | Minimal markers; dot or number only |
            | Slot List | All slots for selected day | Open-house & private use same style (label-based only) |
            | Slot Card | Time · Address · Type chip · Status | No colour distinction except labels |
            | Capacity Bar | For open-house slots with capacity >1 | Small horizontal bar or text “5/10 confirmed” |
            | Slot Actions | View, Message, Edit, Cancel | Right-aligned buttons |
            | Add Viewing Block Modal | Fields: Listing, Type, Date, Start/End, Capacity, Note | Clean and simple |
            | Slot Detail Modal | Buyer list with badges & contact | Same UI for sale & rent |
            | Auto Confirm Badge | “Confirmed (auto)” | Green tick icon |
            | Google Calendar Tile | (Optional) small block showing sync status | Not interactive in MVP |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A5 — Dummy Content (for Designer)**
            
            **Calendar Month Example**
            
            - Tue 9 Apr — “2 viewings”
            - Sat 12 Apr — “3 viewings”
            - Sun 13 Apr — “0 viewings”
            
            **Selected Day**
            
            ```
            11:00–13:00 — 12 King Street (OPEN-HOUSE)
            5 confirmed / cap 10 — Status: Active
            Buttons: View Bookings | Edit Slot | Cancel Slot
            ```
            
            **Private Viewing**
            
            ```
            15:30–16:00 — 22 Yoxley Drive (PRIVATE)
            1 confirmed — Status: Active
            Buttons: View Booking | Message | Cancel
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B1 — Behaviour & Logic**
            
            ### **B1.1 Slot Types**
            
            | **Type** | **Rules** |
            | --- | --- |
            | PRIVATE | Capacity = 1 • Only 1 booking allowed |
            | OPEN-HOUSE | Capacity = N (default 10) • Many bookings allowed |
            
            ### **B1.2 Booking Logic (Critical)**
            
            | **Behaviour** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Auto-confirm ALWAYS | No approval step. Creating a booking = status: “confirmed”. |
            | System message insertion | Insert into inquiry_thread: “Viewing confirmed: [date/time] ([open-house/private]).” |
            | “Confirmed (auto)” label | Required in all booking displays. |
            | Messaging | Owner can message HH from within O4 via O3 thread. |
            
            ### **B1.3 Cancellation**
            
            | **Trigger** | **Result** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Owner cancels slot | Slot.status = “cancelled”; all bookings.status = “cancelled”; WhatsApp + email notifications sent |
            | HH cancels (Phase 2) | Free capacity reopens |
            
            ### **B1.4 Rescheduling (Edit slot)**
            
            - PATCH updates startTime/endTime.
            - System message inserted:
                
                > “Viewing updated: [new date/time]”
                > 
            - Notify HH via WhatsApp + email.
            
            ### **B1.5 Data flow integration**
            
            WF-O4 must sync with:
            
            - WF-O3 (threads)
            - WF-H1 (booking creation)
            - WF-O1 (viewings KPIs)
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2 — Data Model Requirements**
            
            ### **viewing_slots**
            
            ```
            slotID: string
            ownerID: string
            placeID: string
            slotType: "PRIVATE" | "OPEN_HOUSE"
            startTime: datetime
            endTime: datetime
            capacity: number
            status: "active" | "full" | "cancelled"
            note?: string
            ```
            
            ### **viewing_bookings**
            
            ```
            bookingID: string
            slotID: string
            hunterID: string
            status: "confirmed" | "cancelled" | "no_show" | "attended"
            ```
            
            ### **Linkage**
            
            - Each booking links back to inquiry_thread using (placeID + hunterID).
            - All events generate ActivityEvent for Owner Dashboard + Admin A9.
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3 — Integrations**
            
            | **Integration** | **Usage** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **WhatsApp** | Confirmation, cancellation, reminders (no threads saved) |
            | **Email** | Backup notifications |
            | **Google Calendar (one-way)** | Push: slot created / updated / cancelled |
            | **Analytics** | Events: slot_created · booking_auto_confirmed · slot_cancelled |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4 — Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Buyer not verified | Impossible — gate in WF-H1 blocks before booking. |
            | Over-capacity open-house | Reject booking with 409 FULL. |
            | Private slot full | Reject new booking. |
            | Slot deleted | All bookings cancelled + messages sent. |
            | Time overlap | No restriction — owner responsibility (MVP). |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5 — Phase 2 Enhancements**
            
            - Mark viewing attendance (attended/no-show)
            - Auto-assign optimism score to buyer
            - Suggest optimal open-house times (AI)
            - Owner can export calendar
            - Multi-day open-house window
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O5 — Owner Public Property Page  Preview + Visitor View)**
            
            > WF-O5 is the **public property page “Arrange a Visit”** It also shows **“Message Owner”**
            > 
            
            This is the **most important public-facing page** – ~90% of traffic comes here from:
            
            - Rightmove / Zoopla
            - WhatsApp viewing links
            - QR sign outside the house
            - Social shares
            - Owner sending the link directly
            
            **Main conversion goals:**
            
            - Book a **viewing**
            - Send an **inquiry**
            - Create an **account**
            - Eventually make an **offer/application** (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            ## **0. Global UI Rules (O5)**
            
            | **Element** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Header | Always visible: Yalla.House (yellow) · Services & Pricing · About · List Your Place |
            | Sidebar | **Never shown** on O5 (even for Owners). Owner sees a small preview ribbon instead. |
            | Footer | Privacy · Terms · Cookie · GDPR & Safety · Imprint (DE) · Support · WhatsApp |
            | Theme | Dark Dashfolio+ theme, Yalla Yellow CTAs, same font/spacing system as rest of app. |
            | Address | For MVP: **full address shown** on public page (no hiding). |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ### **A1. Purpose**
            
            | **Goal** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 | Be as clear and clean as a Rightmove listing, but simpler. |
            | 2 | Make **“Arrange a Visit”** the obvious next step (primary CTA). |
            | 3 | Let logged-in HHs **Message Owner** and later save / make offers. |
            | 4 | Work for **sale & rent** without separate designs. |
            | 5 | Double as an **Owner Preview** so they can sanity-check their listing. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A2. User Journeys**
            
            ### **Visitor / Home-Hunter (no owner account)**
            
            **Entry:**
            
            - Rightmove/Zoopla link → /place/{slug}?source=rightmove
            - QR sign link → ?source=qrcode
            - WhatsApp link → ?source=whatsapp
            - Direct share by Owner → ?source=direct
            - Yalla.House search (later/Phase 2)
            
            **Flow:**
            
            1. Lands on O5, sees **photos + price + key info + CTAs**.
            2. Scrolls through:
                - photos, description, docs, map
            3. Acts by:
                - clicking **Arrange a Visit** → buyer gate + slot picker (WF-H1)
                - or **Message Owner** → login/HH gate → messaging (WF-H2 / WF-O3 pair)
            4. After booking:
                - “Viewing confirmed” message, plus WhatsApp/email confirmation.
            
            ### **Owner Preview**
            
            - Enters from **WF-O2 → “Preview public page”**.
            - Sees **exact same layout as visitors** + small ribbon:
            
            > “You are viewing your public page. [Edit listing]”
            > 
            - No sidebar, no extra admin clutter.
            
            ---
            
            ### **A3. Visual Layout (ASCII)**
            
            ```
            ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Services & Pricing | About | List… │
            └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            (Owner preview ONLY adds a small ribbon at the very top/bottom)
            
            ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │  Breadcrumb: Home > London > IG1 > 12 King Street       │
            │                                                          │
            │  ┌─────────────────────────────┬───────────────────────┐ │
            │  │ PHOTO CAROUSEL              │  KEY INFO & CTAs     │ │
            │  │ [large hero image]          │                       │ │
            │  │ [thumbs below on desktop]   │  £615,000 (For Sale)  │ │
            │  │  swipe on mobile            │  3 bed · 2 bath ·     │ │
            │  │                              │ 110 m² · Freehold     │ │
            │  └─────────────────────────────┴───────────────────────┘ │
            │                                                          │
            │  [PRIMARY CTA] Arrange a Visit                           │
            │  [SECONDARY CTA] Message Owner (login required)         │
            │                                                          │
            │  ───── Description ───────────────────────────────────  │
            │  • Bullet highlights                                     │
            │    Long paragraph description                            │
            │                                                          │
            │  ───── Tabs: Details | Floorplan | Docs & EPC | Map ─── │
            │  [Details]  → beds/baths/size/tenure / rental terms      │
            │  [Floorplan] → inline image/PDF                          │
            │  [Docs & EPC] → EPC, other docs, survey badge            │
            │  [Map & Area] → map embed + text                         │
            │                                                          │
            │  (Optional) Survey badge:                                │
            │  "Independent survey available – unlock after viewing”   │
            └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            (Mobile: sticky bottom bar)
            [ £615,000 ]  [ Arrange a Visit ]  [ Message Owner ]
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **A4. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use dark Dashfolio+ theme; don’t invent new components.
            - **Hierarchy:**
                1. Photos
                2. Price + key facts
                3. Arrange a Visit CTA
            - All CTAs = **Yalla Yellow**.
            - Sidebar hidden on this page.
            - **Mobile-first:**
                - Sticky bar at bottom with price and the two CTAs.
            - Show “survey available” banner if we have a survey for this place (Phase 2 unlock).
            
            ---
            
            ### **A5. UI Components (Table)**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** | **Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Breadcrumb | Home > City > Area > Short address | Small, above hero |
            | Photo Carousel | 1 big image + thumbnails (desktop), swipe (mobile) | Use existing Dashfolio image gallery if possible |
            | Price Block | Big price or rent/month + “For Sale / For Rent” chip | Rental adds deposit & min term under price |
            | Key Facts Row | Beds · Baths · Size · Tenure (sale) / Furnishing (rent) | Use icons for bed/bath |
            | Status Badge | Live / Under Offer / Sold / Let agreed (small pill) | Top-right of price block |
            | Primary CTA | Arrange a Visit | Yalla Yellow |
            | Secondary CTA | Message Owner | Outline button, lock icon if logged out |
            | Description | Bullet highlights + long paragraph | Owner-supplied copy |
            | Tabs | Details · Floorplan · Docs & EPC · Map & Area | Single tab component |
            | Docs List | Floorplan, EPC, brochure, other docs | Show type icon + title |
            | Map Block | Static/embedded map + area text | Use lat/lng if available |
            | Survey Badge | “Independent survey available” strip | Only if surveyAvailable=true |
            | Bottom CTA | Full-width “Ready to see this place?” + Arrange button | Repeat of main CTA for scrollers |
            
            ---
            
            ### **A6. Dummy Text & Microcopy**
            
            **Key Info (Sale)**
            
            £650,000 · 3 bed · 2 bath · 110 m² · Freehold
            
            **Key Info (Rent)**
            
            £2,200 pcm · 3 bed · 2 bath · 110 m² · Min term 12 months · Deposit £2,300
            
            **Highlights (bullets)**
            
            - Quiet residential street, 5 minutes from the station
            - Large south-facing garden with mature trees
            - Recently renovated kitchen and bathrooms
            
            **Description**
            
            > A bright and spacious three-bedroom house on King Street with a modern kitchen, generous living space and a south-facing garden. Perfect for families or home-workers, with excellent transport links into central London.
            > 
            
            **Arrange a Visit (hover):**
            
            > “Pick a time that works for you – instant confirmation.”
            > 
            
            **Message Owner (logged out):**
            
            > “Log in or create a free account to message the owner.”
            > 
            
            **Docs empty text:**
            
            > “The owner hasn’t uploaded documents yet. They may share them after your viewing.”
            > 
            
            **Survey banner (if available):**
            
            > “🔍 Independent survey available – can be shared after your viewing.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **A7. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            | **Area** | **Sale** | **Rent** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Price text | £615,000 | £2,200 / month |
            | Label chip | “For Sale” | “For Rent” |
            | Extra facts | Tenure (freehold/leasehold), chain-free (optional) | Furnished/Unfurnished, deposit, min term |
            | Docs | EPC, floorplan, brochure | EPC, floorplan, draft tenancy (if uploaded) |
            | CTAs | Same CTAs, same behaviour | Same CTAs, same behaviour |
            
            No second layout. Just different labels.
            
            ---
            
            ## **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ### **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            ### **B1.1 Route & Visibility**
            
            - Public route: /place/{placeSlug}
            - Backend resolves slug → placeID.
            - If status != live:
                - Public (anonymous) = 404 or “Listing not available”.
                - Owner (logged in as ownerID) = **preview mode** with ribbon:
            
            > “You are viewing your public page. [Edit listing]”
            > 
            - Sidebar **never** appears here (even for Owner).
            
            ---
            
            ### **B1.2 CTAs & Buyer Gate**
            
            **Arrange a Visit**
            
            - When clicked:
                - If **not logged in as HH**:
                    - Open WF-H1 modal/flow:
                        - collect phone, verify, buying/renting position
                        - then show available viewing slots for this place.
                - If **HH logged in & verified**:
                    - Go directly to slots picker (from viewing_slots).
            - If there are **no active slots**:
                - Button label changes to **“Request a Viewing”**.
                - WF-H1 opens in **“request a slot”** mode (no slot list, just preferences).
            - On successful booking:
                - Create viewing_booking (status = confirmed).
                - Trigger WhatsApp/email to HH and calendar entry for Owner.
                - Write system message into inquiry thread:
                    
                    > “Viewing booked and confirmed: [date/time] (Open house / Private).”
                    > 
            
            **Message Owner**
            
            - When clicked:
                - If **not logged in** → Auth gate (create HH account).
                - Create/find inquiry_thread (placeID + homeHunterID).
                - Redirect HH to Inbox (WF-H2) or show inline widget (Phase 2).
            - Owner side sees same thread in WF-O3.
            
            ---
            
            ### **B1.3 Source Tracking**
            
            - Read source or UTM params on page load:
                - rightmove, zoopla, qrcode, whatsapp, direct, yalla, default unknown.
            - Persist in a short-lived visitor/session store (cookie/localStorage).
            - Attach source to:
                - page view metric (for O1 + A9)
                - created inquiries
                - created bookings.
            
            ---
            
            ### **B2. Data Model (Public Listing View)**
            
            A simplified **read model** for WF-O5:
            
            ```
            PublicListingView {
              placeId: string
              ownerId: string
              slug: string
            
              status: "draft" | "live" | "under_offer" | "sold" | "let_agreed"
              listingType: "sale" | "rent"
            
              // Address / location
              addressFull: string
              addressShort: string   // e.g. "Ilford, London"
              city: string
              postcode: string
              country: string
              lat?: number
              lng?: number
            
              // Pricing & terms
              price: number          // sale price or rent pcm
              currency: "GBP" | "EUR" // etc.
              depositAmount?: number
              minTermMonths?: number
              tenure?: "freehold" | "leasehold" | "share_of_freehold" | "commonhold"
            
              // Key facts
              beds: number
              baths: number
              sizeSqm?: number
              sizeSqft?: number
              epcRating?: string     // "A"–"G"
              propertyType: "flat" | "house" | "maisonette" | "other"
            
              // Media
              photos: string[]       // ordered, first used as hero
              floorplans: string[]
              docs: {
                type: "epc" | "brochure" | "tenancy" | "other"
                label: string
                url: string
              }[]
            
              // Content
              headline?: string
              highlights: string[]
              description: string
            
              // Flags
              surveyAvailable?: boolean
            }
            ```
            
            This can be derived from underlying tables like places, media, documents, surveys, etc. (your existing spec lists those in more detail – this is the condensed “view model” the frontend needs).
            
            ---
            
            ### **B3. Viewing Slots & Availability**
            
            WF-O5 doesn’t manage slots, but it needs to know **whether slots exist**:
            
            - Query viewing_slots where:
                - placeId = this.placeId
                - status = "active"
                - startTime > now
                - and (slotType = "PRIVATE" capacity not reached) or (slotType = "OPEN_HOUSE" and bookings < capacity)
            
            Frontend logic:
            
            - If ≥ 1 active slot:
                - CTA label = **“Arrange a Visit”**.
            - If 0 active slots:
                - CTA label = **“Request a Viewing”**.
                - WF-H1 opens “request” variant (collect preferred time window instead of choosing a slot).
            
            ---
            
            ### **B4. Inquiry Logic**
            
            - “Message Owner” creates or reuses an inquiry_thread for (placeId, homeHunterId).
            - For MVP:
                - allow a **guest inquiry** (no login), but:
                    - strongly nudge user to create an account afterwards to track everything.
            - Thread structure reuses WF-O3 **Unified Message Model** (no new schema).
            
            ---
            
            ### **B5. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Listing not live | 404 for public, Owner gets preview with ribbon. |
            | No photos | Show placeholder hero image + text: “Photos coming soon.” |
            | No docs / EPC | Docs tab shows helper text, no errors. |
            | No lat/lng | Hide map tab or show “Area info not available yet.” |
            | HH not verified | Arrange/View flows enforce WF-H1 verification step. |
            | Owner changes slug | Slug change redirects from old URL → new canonical; placeId remains stable. |
            
            ---
            
            ### **B6. KPIs (fed into O1 & Admin A9)**
            
            WF-O5 emits events for:
            
            - public_place_view (with placeId, source)
            - cta_arrange_visit_click
            - cta_message_owner_click
            - public_docs_view (doc type)
            - survey_banner_view / survey_unlock_click (Phase 2)
            
            These are later aggregated into:
            
            - Public page views
            - CTA conversion rate (views → bookings/inquiries)
            - Document view rate
            - Survey interest
            
            ---
            
            ### **B7. Phase 2 Ideas (Flagged, Not Required)**
            
            - Show “X people viewed this in the last 7 days” on page.
            - “Save this place” (needs HH login + favourites model).
            - “Similar properties nearby”.
            - Inline chat widget at bottom (“Ask a quick question”).
            - Multi-language content variants.
            - Optional “show area only” instead of full address (for sensitive sellers).
            
            ---
            
    
    ---
    
    - **🧩 WF-H1 - H5 Wireframes & UX (Home-hunter)** (searching / booking / offering/ documents)

            >

            > ✔ Upcoming Viewings

            > 
            > ✔ Suggested Listings (Phase 2)
            >

            >

            >

            >

            > - Booking confirmation
            > - After verifying phone
            > - After sending an inquiry
            > - After “Save place” action

            > - Bookings (WF-H3)

            > - Offers/Applications (WF-H5)
            > - Profile/Settings (Unified account)
            >

            > 
            > 1. HH logs in → sees dashboard.
            > 2. Sees upcoming viewings and messages immediately.
            > 3. Presses “Continue booking” or “Message Owner”.
            > 4. Continues with search, viewing booking, or offer/application.

            > | Messages Preview | Last 1–2 inbox messages | Clicking opens WF-H2 |

            > | Mobile Sticky CTA | “Book Viewing” | Rounded bar |

            > # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            > 
            > | **Behaviour** | **Description** |
            > | --- | --- |
            > | Data Scope | Dashboard only uses HH’s own data. |
            > | Upcoming viewings | Query viewing_bookings WHERE hunterID = me AND startTime>now AND status=confirmed. |
            > | Messages preview | Last message in each active inquiry thread. |
            > | Saved places | From saved_places table. |
            > | Status box | Read from HH profile: phoneVerified + buyingPosition/rentingPosition. |
            > | CMP | Must derive viewing type (private/open house) via slotType. |
            > | Ordering | Upcoming viewings sorted ASC, messages sorted DESC. |
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **B2. API / Data Model**
            > 
            > ### **homeHunterDashboardData**
            > 
            > ### **(example shape)**
            > 
            > ```
            > {
            >   "kpis": {
            >     "upcomingViewings": 2,
            >     "messagesUnread": 1,
            >     "savedPlaces": 4
            >   },
            >   "viewings": [
            >      { "slotID": "...", "placeID": "...", "type": "OPEN_HOUSE", "start": "...", "end": "...", "addressShort": "12 King Street" }
            >   ],
            >   "messages": [
            >      { "threadId": "...", "placeID": "...", "buyer": "me", "ownerName": "Sarah", "lastMessage": "See you Saturday..." }
            >   ],
            >   "savedPlaces": [
            >     { "placeID": "...", "photo": "...", "price": 650000, "area": "Dalston", "newSlots": true }
            >   ],
            >   "status": {
            >     "phoneVerified": true,
            >     "position": "mortgage_ready"
            >   }
            > }
            > ```
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **B3. Integrations**
            > 
            > | **Integration** | **How it’s used in H1** |
            > | --- | --- |
            > | WhatsApp | Messages may originate from WhatsApp, but preview shows only Yalla inbox content. |
            > | Calendar | Viewings list pulled from viewing_bookings. |
            > | Booking flow (H1→O4) | When clicking a viewing or CTA → open WF-H3 or WF-H1 depending on context. |
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **B4. Edge Cases**
            > 
            > | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            > | --- | --- |
            > | No viewings | Show: “You have no upcoming viewings” + CTA “Explore listings”. |
            > | No messages | Show placeholder. |
            > | HH not verified | Status box shows: “Verify your phone to book viewings faster”. |
            > | HH has no saved places | Hide section until they save something. |
            > | HH with rental properties | All logic identical except position chips. |
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **B5. Phase 2 Notes (Designer hides for MVP)**
            > 
            > | **Feature** | **Description** |
            > | --- | --- |
            > | Suggested listings | Built using user behaviour + area detection. |
            > | Offer/Application tracker | H5 becomes more sophisticated. |
            > | AI “Best slots” recommendation | Suggest times based on peak availability. |
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## B6. **Relation to Buyer Gate & Booking Flow**
            > 
            > **What H1 does not do**
            > 
            > - H1 is **not** the place where the Buyer Gate or booking logic actually runs.
            > - It only **shows the current status** of the Home-Hunter:
            >     - Are they **verified**?
            >     - What is their **buying / renting position**?
            >     - What viewings and messages already exist?
            > 
            > **Status box behaviour (Dashboard)**
            > 
            > - If phoneVerified = false
            >     - Status panel shows something like:
            >         - “Phone verification: Not completed”
            >         - Button: **Verify my phone**
            >     - That button opens the **global Buyer Gate modal** (the 3-step flow: profile → OTP → success).
            > - If phoneVerified = true
            >     - Status panel shows:
            >         - “Phone verification: ✅ Verified”
            >         - “Position: Cash / Mortgage ready / …”
            >     - Booking / messaging CTAs on property pages and other screens work **without extra friction**.
            > 
            > **Where the real actions happen**
            > 
            > - **Buyer Gate modal** is a **shared component** used from:
            >     - WF-O5 (Public Property Page) → “Arrange a Visit”, “Message Owner”, “WhatsApp”
            >     - WF-H2 (Inbox) → first reply if unverified
            >     - WF-H3 (Bookings) → request change/cancel if unverified
            > - **Booking creation & confirmation** are handled by:
            >     - WF-O5 (first booking step)
            >     - WF-H3 (Bookings / manage viewings)
            >     - WF-O4 (Owner Calendar for availability & rules)
            > 
            > **What H1 summarises**
            > 
            > H1 only **aggregates and displays**:
            > 
            > - Upcoming viewings (from viewing_bookings)
            > - Messages / new replies (from inquiry threads)
            > - Saved places (from HH saved list)
            > - Status (verification + buying / renting position, funnel stage)
            
        - **🧩 WF-H2 — Home-Hunter Home Hunter Inbox (Messaging Hub)**
            
            **Home-Hunter Workspace for messages, questions, and property interactions**
            
            ---
            
            # **0. GLOBAL UI COMPONENTS (REQUIRED)**
            
            These appear on **every** Home-Hunter screen.
            
            | **Element** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Header | Yalla.House (logo), Services, About, Saved Places, Dashboard, Inbox (active), Profile |
            | HH Sidebar | Dashboard · Inbox (badge) · Bookings · Saved Places · Offers/Applications · Documents · Settings |
            | Footer | Privacy Policy · Terms · Cookies · Support · Imprint |
            | Theme | Dashfolio+ dark theme + Yalla Yellow highlights |
            
            ---
            
            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **A1. Visual Layout (Wireframe Representation)**
            
            ```
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Yalla.House | Saved | Dashboard | Inbox ●3 | Profile  │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌───────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │  HH SIDEBAR    │  INBOX — Conversations                        │
            │  Dashboard     │  ───────────────────────────────────────────  │
            │  Inbox ●3      │  Left: Conversation List                      │
            │  Bookings      │  Right: Conversation Window                   │
            │  Saved Places  │                                               │
            │  Offers/App    │  RIGHT PANEL:                                 │
            │  Documents     │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
            │  Settings      │  │ Header: Property + Address/Alias        │  │
            │                │  │ Owner Label: “Owner of {StreetName}”    │  │
            │                │  │ Messages Thread                         │  │
            │                │  │                                          │  │
            │                │  │  CTA Row:                               │  │
            │                │  │  [ Arrange Visit ] [ Make Offer ]       │  │
            │                │  │  [ View Listing ]                      │  │
            │                │  │                                          │  │
            │                │  │ Message Input Box + Send                │  │
            │                │  └─────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
            └────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **A2. Purpose**
            
            Give Home-Hunters a **central communication hub** with Owners that:
            
            - Replaces WhatsApp/email fragmentation
            - Keeps all messages tied to **each property**
            - Helps them **book a viewing** or **make an offer** from within chat
            - Maintains **GDPR-safe masking** for Owner and HH identities
            - Works perfectly on mobile & desktop
            - Encourages **conversion** from chat → viewing → offer/application
            
            ---
            
            ## **A3. Home-Hunter Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            **Entry points:**
            
            - Sidebar → *Inbox*
            - After Buyer Gate (WF-H1) → direct to thread
            - From Property Page → “Message Owner”
            - From Bookings → “Message Owner”
            - From Offers → “Ask a question”
            
            **Flow:**
            
            1. HH sees left-side list of conversation threads.
            2. Opens a thread → sees message history with owner.
            3. Uses CTA row:
                - **Arrange a Visit**
                - **Make an Offer** (sale)
                - **Apply to Rent** (rent)
                - **View Listing**
            4. Sends message using the input box.
            5. Sees Owner replies (all masked identities).
            
            **Exit paths:**
            
            - To WF-H3 Bookings
            - To WF-H4 Saved Places
            - To WF-O5 Public Property Page
            
            ---
            
            ## **A4. UI Components (Table)**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** | **Designer Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Conversation List | Thumbnail, address (masked), owner label, timestamp, unread badge | Use pill badges (Yalla Yellow) |
            | Conversation Window | Full thread + CTAs + message input | Should feel like WhatsApp/iMessage |
            | CTA Row | Arrange Visit / Make Offer / View Listing | Always visible under thread |
            | Message Bubbles | HH right, Owner left | Neutral colours, subtle styling |
            | Owner Identity Mask | “Owner of 12 King Street” (never real name) | Required for GDPR & platform trust |
            | Property Header | Photo + address/alias + For Sale/For Rent chip | Reuse WF-O5 styling |
            | Mobile Drawer | Conversation list collapsible into top drawer | High mobile usage |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A5. Dummy Text (use in design)**
            
            **Conversation list example:**
            
            ```
            12 King Street (For Sale)     ● 2 new
            Owner replied 1h ago
            ```
            
            **Conversation content example:**
            
            ```
            Owner: Hi, yes the property is available.
            You: Great, is Saturday okay?
            Owner: Yes, 11:00 works — you can book via the button below.
            ```
            
            CTA row:
            
            ```
            [ Arrange a Visit ]  [ Make an Offer ]  [ View Listing ]
            ```
            
            Rental version CTA:
            
            ```
            [ Arrange a Visit ]  [ Apply to Rent ]  [ View Listing ]
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **A6. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            | **Sale Mode** | **Rent Mode** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Make Offer CTA | Apply to Rent CTA |
            | Buying Position (Cash/Mortgage) | Renting Position (Employed/Student) |
            | Offer thread | Application thread |
            | Place labelled “For Sale” | Place labelled “For Rent” |
            
            No layout changes — only labels swap automatically.
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            | **Behaviour** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | 1 Thread per HH + Listing | Key rule: threadKey = listingId + homeHunterId |
            | Sorting | Descending by lastActivityAt |
            | Unread count | Count messages where receiver = HH and read=false |
            | GDPR masking | Owner = “Owner of ”, HH = full name only |
            | CTA Behaviour | Always available unless listing is archived |
            | Visiting | CTA → open WF-H1 booking flow |
            | Offers/Applications | CTA → opens WF-H5 (offers/applications) |
            | Auto-link to Booking | If booking exists → highlight upcoming visit inside thread |
            | Thread Merging | If HH sends WhatsApp before inbox, still merge to single inquiry |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2. Data Model Requirements**
            
            **Threads Table**
            
            ```
            threadId
            listingId
            ownerId
            homeHunterId
            lastActivityAt
            status (active / archived / offer_made / application_made)
            unreadCount
            ```
            
            **Messages Table**
            
            ```
            messageId
            threadId
            sender (owner|hh|system)
            body
            createdAt
            readAt
            ```
            
            **HomeHunter Model**
            
            (Referenced only)
            
            ```
            hhId
            name
            phone (masked)
            phoneVerified
            buyingPosition OR rentingPosition
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3. Integrations (Description)**
            
            | **Integration** | **Use** |
            | --- | --- |
            | WF-H1 Buyer Gate | Messaging locked until HH verifies phone |
            | WF-O3 Owner Inquiries | Thread updates sync to Owner’s side |
            | WF-O4 Calendar | “Arrange Visit” CTA → slot selector |
            | WF-H5 Offers | “Make Offer / Apply” CTA → offers/applications |
            | WhatsApp (twilio) | Notification only, not messaging storage |
            | Email | Notification only |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Expected Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Owner archived listing | Thread auto-archived |
            | HH deleted account | Thread anonymised (GDPR), messages preserved |
            | WhatsApp contact before Buyer Gate | Force gate before inbox unlock |
            | Multiple listings with same owner | Separate threads per listing |
            | Owner changes address privacy | Display alias instead of full street address |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5. Phase 2 Notes**
            
            - Attachments (photos/documents)
            - AI auto-reply / suggested answers
            - Read receipts shown to HH
            - Offer negotiation thread inside chat
            - Voice notes
            - Image sharing
            - Owner identity unmasking after offer accepted
            
            ---
            
            ## **B6. KPI Definitions**
            
            | **KPI** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Response Rate | % owner replies within 24h |
            | Time to First Response | Avg delay before owner replies |
            | Conversion to Viewing | % of conversations → viewing booked |
            | Conversion to Offer | % → offer/application submitted |
            | Message Volume | # of messages per listing |
            
            These feed Admin Analytics (A9) & Owner Dashboard (O1).
            
            ---
            
            ## **B7. Conversion Funnel**
            
            ```
            Conversation Opened
               ↓
            First Message Sent
               ↓
            Owner Replies
               ↓
            CTA Buttons Displayed
               ↓
            Viewing Booked / Offer Made
               ↓
            Confirmation
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B8. ID & Security Logic**
            
            - HH never sees owner’s phone/email
            - Owner never sees HH phone/email (until offer accepted)
            - threadId always unique per (listingId + homeHunterId)
            - All messages stored with immutable timestamps
            - Deletion = soft delete (visibility flag)
            
            ---
            
            ## **B9. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - WebSockets or 15s polling
            - Twilio WhatsApp notifications
            - Email sender
            - Thread merging resolver
            - Rate limiting & abuse protection (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            # **📌 READY FOR NOTION**
            
            This version is:
            
            - Fully merged
            - Fully consistent with WF-O1/O2/O3
            - Includes Visual Layout, Designer & Developer tables, Rental logic, Funnel, KPIs
            - All masking rules preserved
            - CTA row added
            - Inbox → Viewing/Offer flows clearly defined

        - **🧩 WF-H3 — Home-Hunter My Bookings (Viewings Manager)**
            
            **Status: FULLY UPDATED + FULLY MERGED with old version — nothing missing**

            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **A1. Visual Layout**
            
            ```
            ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HEADER: Dashboard • Inbox • Bookings (active) • Saved Places  │
            └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌───────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ HH SIDEBAR    │  H3 — My Bookings (Home-Hunter Viewings)      │
            │ Dashboard     │  Filters: Upcoming | Past | Cancelled         │
            │ Inbox         │                                                │
            │ Bookings ●    │  VIEWING CARDS                                │
            │ Saved Places  │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
            │ Offers/App    │  │ Photo • Address • Price                   │ │
            │ Documents     │  │ Viewing Date & Type                       │ │
            │ Settings      │  │ Chips: ✔ Confirmed / Past / Cancelled     │ │
            │               │  │ Buttons: View Details / Message Owner      │ │
            │               │  │ Add to Calendar / Cancel Viewing          │ │
            │               │  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
            │               │                                                │
            │               │ Empty State for each filter                    │
            └───────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            Mobile:
            
            - Date headers
            - Vertical cards
            - Swipe left for quick actions (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            ## **A2. Purpose**
            
            - Give Home-Hunters a **clean viewing schedule**.
            - Reduce no-shows.
            - Keep them engaged after viewing (offers/surveys).
            - Provide quick access to messaging & rescheduling.
            
            ---
            
            ## **A3. HH Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            1. Books a viewing via WF-H1
            2. Receives WhatsApp + Email confirmation
            3. Lands here to check all upcoming and past viewings
            4. Uses this page to:
                - get directions
                - message the owner
                - cancel/reschedule (Phase 2)
                - make an offer after viewing
            
            WF-H3 is the **Home-Hunter’s personal appointment diary**.
            
            ---
            
            ## **A4. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - “When is my next viewing?”
            - “Where do I go?”
            - “Is it open-house or private?”
            - “Can I message the owner?”
            - “Can I cancel?”
            - “What have I already viewed?”
            - “Should I make an offer?”
            
            ---
            
            ## **A5. UI Component List**
            
            | **Component** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Filter bar | Upcoming · Past · Cancelled |
            | Date headers | “Sat 12 April” |
            | Viewing card | Photo + info + CTA actions |
            | Status chips | ✔ Confirmed · Past · Cancelled |
            | Buttons | View Details · Message Owner · Add to Calendar · Cancel Viewing |
            | Empty states | Different for each filter |
            | Swipe actions | Cancel / Message (Phase 2) |
            | Map link | Optional: open Google Maps |
            
            ---
            
            ## **A6. Viewing Card Layout**
            
            **Top Section**
            
            - Preview photo
            - Full address (revealed after booking)
            - Price (sale or rent)
            - Beds · Size

            - Slot information:
                - **Sat 12 Apr · 11:00–13:00**
                - OPEN-HOUSE / PRIVATE VIEWING
            - Status Chip
                - ✔ Confirmed
                - Past Viewing
                - Cancelled

            - [View Details] → WF-O5
            - [Message Owner] → WF-H2

            ## **A8. Cancelled Viewings**

            - Greyed-out

            - If cancelled by HH → “Cancelled by You”

            > 
            
            >

            >

            >

            > “You have no cancelled viewings.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **A10. Rental Logic**
            
            - Price → rent/month
            - After viewing, nudges use “Apply to Rent”
            - Optional: Minimum term + deposit
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            | **Condition** | **Category** |
            | --- | --- |
            | now < startTime | Upcoming |
            | now > endTime | Past |
            | status = cancelled | Cancelled |
            
            Viewing timeline is consistent with WF-O4 data.
            
            **Open-house logic**
            
            - Multiple bookings allowed
            - Cancellation decreases participant count
            
            **Private slot logic**
            
            - Only one HH
            - If HH cancels → slot becomes available to others
            
            **Address reveal**
            
            - Address only shown after booking
            - Before booking → area only
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2. Data Model Requirements**
            
            **Booking object**
            
            ```
            Booking {
              bookingID: string
              placeID: string
              ownerID: string
              homeHunterID: string
              slotID: string
              slotType: "OPEN_HOUSE" | "PRIVATE"
              startTime: number
              endTime: number
              status: "confirmed" | "cancelled" | "past"
              cancellationReason?: string
            }
            ```
            
            **Place summary**
            
            ```
            PlaceSummary {
              previewPhoto
              addressShort
              addressFull
              price or rent
              beds
              sizeSqm
            }
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3. API Endpoints**
            
            - GET /hh/viewings
            - POST /viewing/cancel
            - POST /viewing/reschedule (Phase 2)
            
            Notifications:
            
            - Cancel → Owner
            - Reschedule → Owner (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4. Integrations**
            
            | **System** | **Use** |
            | --- | --- |
            | WF-H2 | Messaging owner |
            | WF-O5 | Property details |
            | WF-H1 | Book/reschedule flow |
            | O4 Calendar sync | Reflect booking status |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Edge Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Slot cancelled by owner | Move to Cancelled with “Cancelled by Owner” |
            | Overlapping reschedule | Block (Phase 2) |
            | Owner changes slot time | Auto-update booking + notify HH |
            | HH deletes account | Bookings anonymised for analytics |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B6. KPI Definitions**
            
            - Attendance rate
            - Cancelation rate
            - Average time booking → viewing
            - Repeat viewings per HH
            - Offer rate after viewing (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            ## **B7. Funnel**
            
            ```
            Booking Confirmed (H1)
                  ↓
            My Bookings (H3)
                  ↓
            Viewing Completed
                  ↓
            Survey Unlocked (optional)
                  ↓
            Offer / Application
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B8. ID Logic**
            
            - bookingID
            - placeID
            - slotID
            - hhID
            - ownerID
            - calendarEventID
            
            ---
            
            ## **B9. Tooling Overview**
            
            - Link bookings ↔ view_slots
            - Link bookings ↔ places
            - WhatsApp integration for reminders
            - .ics generator
            - Google Calendar link generator

            **WF-H4 — My Saved Places**

            # **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            ### **Saved Card Should Display:**
            
            - Saved status
            - Viewing status (from O4 Calendar → confirmed / past / cancelled)
            - Unread messages count
            - Survey status
            - Offer/application status
            - Next viewing slot
            
            ### **Actions Trigger:**
            
            - Save/Unsave → SavedPlaces table
            - Arrange Viewing → WF-H1
            - Messaging → thread open in H2
            - Survey → S6/S7
            - Offer/Application → H5
            
            ### **Sorting Server-Side**
            
            To handle 100+ saved places cleanly.
            
            ---
            
            # **B2. Data Model Requirements**
            
            pull from:
            
            **SavedPlaces Table**
            
            - savedPlaceID
            - hhID
            - placeID
            - savedAt
            
            **Places Table**
            
            - addressShort / full
            - price or rent
            - beds / size
            - previewPhoto
            
            **ViewingsBooking Table**
            
            - bookingID
            - date/time
            - status
            
            **Messages Table**
            
            - unreadCount
            
            **Surveys Table**
            
            - surveyStatus
            
            **Offers Table (Phase 2)**
            
            - status (pending / accepted / rejected)

            # **B3. Integrations**
            
            - Airtable (SavedPlaces, Places, Viewings, Surveys)
            - Twilio WhatsApp (for booking confirmations)
            - Email provider (notifications)
            - Calendar links (.ics)
