            # **B4. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Saved place becomes **unavailable** | Show “Unavailable” chip + disable CTA |
            | Owner deletes listing | Grey out card, allow “Remove” |
            | HH unsaves place | Remove instantly from list |
            | Viewing cancelled by owner | Show “Cancelled” chip + reschedule CTA |
            | HH has 0 saved places | Show empty state |

            # **A1. Purpose**
            
            - Provide a **simple, guided, transparent** offer/application workflow.
            - Prevent confusion across WhatsApp/email.
            - Show clear **status timeline** so HH always knows “what’s happening next”.
            - Keep all negotiations inside Yalla House.
            
            ---
            
            # **A2. What This Page Must Solve**
            
            - “What is the status of my offer?”
            - “Has the owner seen it?”
            - “What documents do I need?”
            - “Can I negotiate?”
            - “Can I withdraw?”
            - “Where can I message the owner about this?”
            
            ---
            
            # **A3. UI Components (Merged Version from New + Old)**
            
            | **Component** | **Included** | **Reason** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Offer/Application Cards | ✅ | In old + new |
            | Status Chips incl. “Viewed”, “Counter-offer” | ✅ **ADDED BACK** | Missing in new |
            | Status Timeline | ✅ **ADDED BACK** | Old version had it |
            | Document Upload Zones | ✅ | In old |
            | Offer Detail Page | ✅ **ADDED BACK** | Old version |
            | Application Detail Page | ✅ | Old version |
            | Viewing prerequisite nudge | ✅ **ADDED BACK** | “Offers from viewers prioritised” |
            | Sticky mobile bar | ✅ **ADDED BACK** | Old version |
            | Filters (Active/Accepted/Declined/Drafts) | ✅ | In old |
            | Sale vs Rent segmentation | ✅ | In both |
            | Counter-offer support (Phase 2) | ✅ | Old version |
            
            ---
            
            # **A4. Designer Notes**
            
            - Use **mobile-first timeline scroll** (Airbnb-style).
            - Timeline uses: grey dots (pending), green (completed), red (declined).
            - Document upload boxes must feel **secure** and **official**.
            - Sticky mobile action bar appears **after** offer submission.
            - Separate **Offer Detail Page** and **Application Detail Page** need full-width modals.
            - For rent, highlight **ID / Payslips / References** visually.
            
            ---
            
            # **A5. Dummy Microcopy**
            
            - “Offers from verified viewers are prioritised.”
            - “Upload proof of funds to strengthen your offer.”
            - “Your application is being reviewed.”
            - “Owner viewed your offer.”
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            # **B1. Behaviour & Logic (Merged)**
            
            ### **Draft → Submit → Viewed → Counter → Accepted/Declined**
            
            All states must be stored.
            
            ### **Sale:**
            
            - Must store **offerAmount**, docs, notes.
            
            ### **Rent:**
            
            - Must store **application form fields** + required docs.
            
            ### **Viewing prerequisite:**
            
            If HH did **not view**, show banner:
            
            > “Offers from viewers are prioritised.”
            > 
            
            ### **After submission:**
            
            - Create system message in O3/H2.
            - Notify owner via WhatsApp/email.
            - Lock editing except uploading new docs.
            
            ### **Counter-offer:**
            
            (Phase 2, but shown in timeline.)
            
            ---
            
            # **B2. Data Model Additions (from older spec)**
            
            ### **Status timeline events**
            
            ```
            timelineEvents[] = [
              { type:"submitted", timestamp },
              { type:"viewed_by_owner", timestamp },
              { type:"counter_offer", data, timestamp },
              { type:"accepted", timestamp },
              { type:"declined", timestamp }
            ]
            ```
            
            ### **Rental fields**
            
            ```
            employmentStatus
            householdIncome
            moveInDate
            references[]
            ```
            
            ### **Sale fields**
            
            ```
            proofOfFundsDoc
            mortgageInPrincipleDoc
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **B3. API Endpoints (merged)**
            
            - POST /offer/create
            - POST /offer/submit
            - POST /offer/update
            - POST /offer/upload-document
            - GET /hh/offers
            - GET /owner/offers
            - PATCH /offer/withdraw
            
            ---
            
            # **B4. Edge Cases (old spec restored)**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Owner views offer | timeline event: “viewed_by_owner” |
            | Counter-offer issued | store new amount, notify HH |
            | Owner accepts | show “Next steps” panel |
            | Owner declines | show “Explore other places” |
            | HH withdraws | timeline event + grey status |
            | Listing removed | card disabled |
            
            ---
            
            # **B5. KPIs (combined)**
            
            - Offers per viewing
            - Offer acceptance rate
            - Rental application completion rate
            - Document upload completion rate
            - Time HH waits for decision
            - Counter-offers frequency
            
            ---
            
            # **B6. Funnel (Merged)**
            
            ```
            Viewing Attended
                ↓
            Offer/Application Created
                ↓
            Docs Uploaded
                ↓
            Owner Viewed
                ↓
            (Option) Counter-offer
                ↓
            Accepted / Declined
                ↓
            Legal / Referencing
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **B7. ID Logic**
            
            These IDs drive the offer/application lifecycle:
            
            ### **Primary Entities**
            
            | **ID** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **offerID** | Unique offer/application record |
            | **hhID** | Home-Hunter submitting the offer |
            | **ownerID** | Owner receiving the offer |
            | **placeID** | Property the offer relates to |
            | **bookingID** | Viewing record for eligibility / context |
            | **conversationID** | Associated message thread in H2/O3 |
            | **timelineEventID** | Each event in the offer timeline |
            | **docID** | Each uploaded document (POF, ID, Payslips) |
            
            ### **Status Object**
            
            ```
            {
              "status": "submitted | viewed | counter | accepted | rejected",
              "submittedAt": "...",
              "viewedAt": "...",
              "responseAt": "...",
              "counterDetails": { "amount": "...", "note": "..." }
            }
            ```
            
            ### **Document Attachment Object**
            
            ```
            {
              "docID": "...",
              "type": "proofOfFunds | ID | mortgagePrinciple | payslip | reference",
              "uploadedAt": "...",
              "url": "..."
            }
            ```
            
            ### **Identity Logic Rules**
            
            - **offerID** stays the same for all updates.
            - **Home-Hunter identity must be verified** (from Buyer Gate).
            - **Owner never sees HH phone/email** until acceptance unless both mutually agree (Phase 2).
            - If HH upgrades to full account later → seamlessly merge with tempAccountToken.
            
            **GDPR Note:**
            
            Messages + offer documents cannot be deleted by HH once submitted, only hidden from UI.
            
            ---
            
            # **B8. Tooling Overview (Complete)**
            
            ### **Databases (Airtable / Postgres Later)**
            
            - **Offers** table
            - **Places**
            - **HHAccounts**
            - **OwnerAccounts**
            - **Bookings**
            - **Documents** (attachments)
            - **Messages** (integration with H2/O3)
            
            ### **Integrations**
            
            | **Tool** | **Usage** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Twilio** | WhatsApp notifications for: submission, owner viewed, responses |
            | **SendGrid** | Email confirmations |
            | **Stripe (Phase 2)** | Holding deposits (rent) / reservation fee (sale) |
            | **PDF generation service** | Auto-generate Offer Summary PDF |
            | **Framer** | Designer layout (CTAs, timeline, mobile behaviour) |
            
            ### **Triggers**
            
            - When HH submits →
                - System message in inbox
                - WhatsApp + Email to owner
                - Timeline event created
            - When Owner responds →
                - Update timeline
                - Notify HH
                - Sync inbox with auto-message
            
            ### **Validation**
            
            - Cannot submit incomplete offer
            - Cannot overwrite accepted offer
            - Cannot submit second offer → instead “Improve Offer” (Phase 2)

            |---------------------------------------------------------|

            # **A — DESIGNER SECTION**
            
            ## **Page Name**
            
            **WF-H6 — Surveys Hub**
            
            ## **Purpose**
            
            Give Home-Hunters one place to **view, buy, request, compare** and **re-open** condition reports across all properties they are tracking.
            
            This page drives:
            
            - **Offer quality**
            - **Confidence**
            - **Reduced wasted viewings**
            - **Paid survey revenue**
            
            ---
            
            ## **User Journey (HH)**
            
            ```
            Public Page (WF-O5)
                ↓ sees "Survey Available"
            H3 Saved Places
                ↓ clicks survey badge
            H6 Surveys Hub
                ↓ Unlock / Request / View Survey
            H5 Offer
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **UI COMPONENT LIST**
            
            ### **1. Header Block**
            
            - Title: **Your Surveys**
            - Subtext: *“Independent condition reports for informed decisions.”*
            - Filters bar:
                - All
                - **Available**
                - **Purchased**
                - **Requested**
                - **Completed**
            
            ### **2. Survey Cards**
            
            Each card includes:
            
            **Top row**
            
            - Property thumbnail
            - AddressFull or addressShort
            - Price / Rent
            - Beds / Size
            
            **Survey Status Chip (5 STATES)**
            
            - 🔓 **Available**
            - 💰 **Purchased**
            - 🛠 **Requested (Pending)**
            - ✔ **Completed (PDF ready)**
            - ⛔ **Not available**
            
            **Origin Badge**
            
            - Provided by Owner
            - Uploaded by Home-Hunter
            - Uploaded by Another Buyer
            
            **Summary (metadata preview)**
            
            Short summary from survey file or metadata:
            
            > “General condition sound. Minor damp in rear wall.”
            > 
            
            **CTAs based on state**
            
            - Available → **[Unlock Survey for £X]**
            - Purchased → **[View Survey]**
            - Requested → **[Cancel Request]**, **[Message Owner]**
            - Completed → **[View Survey]**
            - None → **[Ask Owner]**, triggering H2 inbox
            
            ---
            
            ## **Survey Detail Modal (Designer Spec)**
            
            Contains:
            
            - Hero: Photo + address
            - Toolbar buttons:
                - [Open PDF]
                - [Download]
                - [View Place]
            - Metadata block:
                - Surveyor name
                - Survey date
                - Survey type (HomeBuyer / Level 2 / Structural)
                - Uploaded by (Owner / HH)
                - Version
                - Price (if applicable)
            - Summary box:
                - Top issues (text)
            - Optional (Phase 2):
                - AI Highlights
                - Repair cost estimates
            
            ---
            
            ## **Dummy Text**
            
            **Title:** “Your Surveys”
            
            **Card summary:**
            
            > “3-bed terraced house. Generally sound. Damp noted behind kitchen wall.”
            > 
            
            **CTA examples**
            
            - “Unlock Survey for £29”
            - “View Survey”
            - “Request Survey”
            
            ---
            
            ## **Rental Logic**
            
            For rentals use same layout but wording can include:
            
            - HMO certificates
            - Gas/Electric reports
            - Safety findings
            - Noise / damp findings
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            ### **Survey Visibility Rules**
            
            - Only **approved** surveys visible.
            - Summary visible **even if locked**.
            - Full PDF only accessible to:
                - HH who purchased
                - HH who requested → when completed
                - HH who uploaded it
            
            ### **Survey States Logic**
            
            ```
            IF survey exists AND hh owns (purchase OR uploader)
                → OWNED
            ELSE IF survey exists AND is purchasable
                → AVAILABLE
            ELSE IF survey requested by hh AND pending
                → REQUESTED
            ELSE IF survey requested AND admin uploaded completed PDF
                → COMPLETED
            ELSE
                → NONE (Ask Owner)
            ```
            
            ### **Request Workflow**
            
            - HH clicks **Request Survey**
            - Creates surveyRequests record with:
                - status = pending
                - hhID, placeID, ownerID
            - Owner notified via O3 & email
            - Admin uploads PDF → marks as completed
            - HH receives:
                - WhatsApp
                - Email
                - In-app alert
            - Survey becomes **Completed** and **Unlocked**
            
            ### **Payment Logic**
            
            - Stripe Checkout Session created → returns URL
            - On successful payment:
                - Create surveyPurchases entry
                - Unlock file access
                - Update UI to “Owned”
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2. Data Model Requirements**
            
            ### **Table: surveys**
            
            - surveyID
            - placeID
            - origin (owner / hh / other_hh)
            - status (pending_review, approved, rejected)
            - shortTitle
            - summary
            - fileURL
            - price
            - currency
            - surveyType
            - surveyorName
            - createdBy
            - createdAt
            - version
            - isPublicOnPage
            
            ### **Table: surveyPurchases**
            
            - purchaseID
            - hhID
            - surveyID
            - placeID
            - purchasedAt
            - pricePaid
            - version
            
            ### **Table: surveyRequests**
            
            - requestID
            - hhID
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - status (pending, in_progress, completed)
            - surveyPDFurl (if completed)
            - completedAt
            - adminNotes
            
            ### **HH Logic**
            
            - ownershipStatus derived from:
                - purchase
                - request completion
                - uploader
                - availability
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3. Integrations (Description)**
            
            ### **Payments**
            
            - Stripe Checkout for paid surveys.
            - Success redirect → H6 with “Owned” chip.
            
            ### **Messaging**
            
            - “Ask Owner” → opens H2 inbox thread.
            - “Survey Request Created” → owner & admin notifications.
            
            ### **File Storage**
            
            - Airtable attachments (MVP)
            - Optional S3 in Phase 2
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4. Edge Cases**
            
            - Survey deleted by Owner → HH who purchased retains PDF access.
            - Owner uploads new version → versioning used.
            - HH tries to buy twice → prevent duplicate purchases.
            - HH without account (temp) → must complete buyer gate before purchase.
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5. Phase 2 Notes**
            
            - AI-generated “Top issues”
            - Cost estimates
            - Multi-version comparison
            - Share with solicitor / broker
            - Owner-paid surveys (subsidised or free-to-unlock)
            
            ---
            
            ## **B6. KPI Definitions**
            
            - Survey availability rate
            - Purchase rate
            - Request → completion time
            - Survey → offer conversion rate
            - Revenue per listing
            - Owner vs HH-uploaded survey ratios
            
            ---
            
            ## **B7. Funnel**
            
            ```
            Saved Place / Viewing
                    ↓
            Survey Badge Seen (H3 or O5)
                    ↓
            WF-H6 — Surveys Hub
               ↓        ↓          ↓
            Unlock   Request    View Survey
                    (pending)
                    ↓
            Completed
                    ↓
            Better-Informed Offer (H5)
                    ↓
            Owner Response
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B8. ID Logic**
            
            - surveyID
            - placeID
            - hhID
            - surveyRequestID
            - surveyPurchaseID
            - ownerID
            - version

        - **ADMIN WIREFRAME LIST ( Logic)**
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A1 — Admin Dashboard (Command Center)**
            
            **Shows everything at a glance:**
            
            - Owners active / Places live
            - Home-hunters active
            - New viewings booked today
            - New inquiries today
            - New surveys uploaded / purchased
            - Integrations health (WhatsApp, Stripe, Calendar)
            - Revenue snapshot
            - Task count (from fulfillment queue)

            ### **WF-A2 — Owner Detail View**
            
            Admin sees everything about an owner:
            
            - Profile
            - Places listed
            - Performance stats
            - Tasks related to the owner
            - Subscription & billing status
            - Interactions timeline
            - Survey-related actions (if owner purchases surveys)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A3 — Home-Hunter Detail View**
            
            Admin sees:
            
            - HH identity
            - Viewings booked
            - Messages
            - Surveys purchased / uploaded
            - Offers (Phase 2)
            - Flags (fraud/behaviour)
            - Verifications (ID, address, funds)

            Now includes full logic for:
            
            - WhatsApp (Twilio)
            - Stripe
            - Email (Sendgrid)
            - Calendar Sync (Google)
            - Property Feeds (Rightmove, Zoopla)
            - QR tracking cold-start (signboard scans)
                
                **+ error messages + logs + timestamps**

            ### **WF-A5 — Tasks & Fulfillment**
            
            Rebuilt after your new logic.
            
            Tasks auto-created for:
            
            - Signboard orders
            - Photo/floorplan orders
            - EPC orders
            - Listing review / quality check
            - Owner support escalations
            - Survey validation
            - “Buyer flagged survey for review”
            
            This is the **“operations HQ”**.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A6 — Survey Marketplace Oversight (Rebuilt)**
            
            Now it supports:
            
            ### **OWNER SIDE**
            
            - Did the owner upload the survey?
            - Does it meet quality standards?
            - Is it approved by admin?
            - Has any HH bought it?
            
            ### **HOME-HUNTER SIDE**
            
            - HH purchases
            - HH uploads
            - Refund requests
            - Disputes
            - Survey reusability
            - % commission earned
            
            Huge value centre.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A7 — Support Inbox (Admin + Support Team)**
            
            Admin sees:
            
            - All owner + HH messages (not threads, but support tickets)
            - Auto-responses performance
            - Priority flags
            - Internal notes
            - Resolution workflow
            - SLA tracking
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A8 — Billing & Revenue Console**
            
            Tracks:
            
            - Owner subscription payments
            - Survey payments
            - Add-on services
            - Costs (Rightmove, Twilio, Stripe, photography vendors)
            - Revenue per place
            - Growth metrics
            - P&L preview (simple)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A9 — Analytics & Performance Dashboard**
            
            The “CEO mode” inside admin.
            
            Metrics:
            
            - Owner → HH conversion
            - Viewing → offer rate (later)
            - Survey marketplace revenue
            - Lead source performance
            - Territory performance (UK → DE → more)
            - Funnel breakdown
            - Churn
            - Cost-to-acquire (later)
            - Cost-to-operate per place

            ---
            
            ## **A2. Purpose (Designer Summary)**
            
            The Dashboard is the **central cockpit** for Admin to monitor:
            
            - System health
            - Marketplace activity
            - User actions (Owners & HH)
            - Integrations
            - Support issues
            - Operational tasks (EPC, surveys, signboards)
            
            Visual tone: calm, clean, control-tower minimalism.
            
            ---
            
            ## **A3. UI Components**
            
            ### **Top Section**
            
            - Title + sub-label
            - Optional small badge: *“Last updated: 2 minutes ago”*
            
            ### **KPI Cards**
            
            - Total Owners
            - Total Home-Hunters
            - System Health (color-coded)
            - Optional “Today’s Viewings” (attachable in Phase 2)
            
            ### **Activity Feed**
            
            - Scrollable panel
            - Items grouped by:
                - Owners
                - Home-Hunters
                - Listings
                - Bookings
                - Inquiries
                - Offers
                - Surveys
            
            ### **Alerts Panel**
            
            - Integration alerts
            - Support tickets
            - Task alerts (EPC pending, photo missing, etc.)
            - Listing issues
            - Verification issues (ID docs mismatched)
            
            ---
            
            # **B — DEVELOPER SECTION**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B1. Behaviour & Logic**
            
            | **Widget** | **Data Source** | **Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Owners Count | users.role=owner | cached |
            | HH Count | users.role=hh | cached |
            | System Health | integration_status | aggregated percentile |
            | Activity Feed | combined events table | DB view recommended |
            | Alerts | support_tickets, task_items, integration_logs | sort by priority |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B2. Data Model Requirements**
            
            ### **Tables Involved**
            
            - **users**
            - **places**
            - **inquiries**
            - **viewings**
            - **offers**
            - **surveys**
            - **survey_access / purchases**
            - **support_tickets**
            - **task_items**
            - **integration_status**
            - **integration_logs**
            - **event_log (recommended)**
            
            ### **Event Aggregation**
            
            Activity Feed should use a unified events table:
            
            ```
            eventID
            eventType (listing_created, booking, inquiry, offer, survey_uploaded)
            actorID
            ownerID / hhID
            placeID
            timestamp
            payload JSON
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **B3. APIs Needed**
            
            - GET /admin/dashboard
            - GET /admin/activity
            - GET /admin/alerts
            - GET /admin/integrations
            - GET /admin/tasks
            
            All endpoints must use **summary-mode** only (no heavy joins).
            
            ---
            
            ## **B4. Integrations (Health Checks)**
            
            Check every 5 minutes:
            
            | **Service** | **Check** | **Logic** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Stripe | webhook ping | if failed >3 |
            | WhatsApp (Twilio) | send test message | if timeout → warn |
            | Email | bounce rate | if >5% → warn |
            | Hosting | CPU/RAM | optional |
            
            Dashboard displays aggregated status:
            
            **🟢 OK • 🟠 Degraded • 🔴 Down**
            
            ---
            
            ## **B5. Security & Permissions**
            
            - Only admins with role=admin may access WF-A1
            - Logging is mandatory for:
                - Alert dismissals
                - Opening support tickets
                - Viewing integrations status
            
            ---
            
            ## **B6. Edge Cases**
            
            | **Case** | **Behaviour** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Zero users | Show blank-state welcome cards |
            | No integrations configured | System Health = grey “No integrations yet” |
            | DB partial outage | Show cached values + warning |
            | Cron delay | Timestamp badge turns orange |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B7. KPIs (Final Set)**
            
            | **KPI** | **Rationale** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Total Owners | Owner growth |
            | Total HH | Liquidity |
            | Listings Live | Inventory |
            | Viewings Today | Operational load |
            | Offers This Week | Market heat |
            | Survey Purchases | Revenue |
            | Unread Support Tickets | Admin pressure |
            | System Health Index (0–100) | Risk |
            
            ---
            
            ## **B8. Admin-Level Funnel**
            
            ```
            Owner Created
                  ↓
            Listing Drafted
                  ↓
            Listing Published
                  ↓
            Viewings
                  ↓
            Offers
                  ↓
            Accepted Deals (Phase 2)
            ```
            
            Admin dashboard shows % drop at each stage.
            
            ---
            
            ## **B9. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - Cron jobs
            - S3/Airtable attachments
            - Error logging middleware
            - Analytics pipeline (Mixpanel / Amplitude later)
            
            ---
            
            # **C — DUMMY CONTENT**

            Owners: 41 (+6 this week)

            • ⚠️ WhatsApp retrying (last error 2h ago)

            • 📩 3 new support messages
            • 🛠 EPC required for 12 Willow Lane
            ```

            │                              │                               │

            │ - Fraud suspicion            │   • Amount / status / date    │
            │ - Spam behavior              │                               │
            │ - Multiple failed KYC        │ Surveys:                      │
            │                              │   • Bought / Requested        │
            │ INTERNAL NOTES               │   • Uploaded (Owner)          │
            │ - Admin-only                 │                               │
            │                              │ Logs:                         │
            │ CONTROLS                     │   • Login history             │
            │ - Suspend user               │   • Device fingerprints       │
            │ - Reset verification         │   • Integration issues        │
            │ - GDPR Export / Delete       │                               │
            └──────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────┘
            ```

            # **C — PURPOSE (combined)**
            
            The admin must immediately understand:
            
            ### **“Who is this user and what have they done?”**
            
            For **Owners**:
            
            Listings → Viewings → Offers → Surveys → Tasks → KYC
            
            For **Home-Hunters**:
            
            Viewings → Offers → Surveys → Funnel → Messaging → Risk Score
            
            This page is the **single source of truth** for trust, behaviour, troubleshooting, and moderation.

            - Multiple failed KYC

            - No-show behaviour
            - Abuse reports from owners

            # **E — RIGHT COLUMN (MERGED TABS)**
            
            ## **TAB 1 — Activity Timeline**
            
            Shows last 20–50 events:
            
            - Created account
            - Viewed property
            - Saved property
            - Started conversation
            - Booked viewing
            - Cancelled viewing
            - Attended viewing
            - Submitted offer

                - Edited availability
                - Responded to offer

                - Purchased
                - Requested
                - Uploaded

            | Property | Status | Price/Rent | Views 7d | Inquiries | Viewings | Offers | Tasks |

            - **Inquiry Response Time**
            - **Overdue Tasks** (EPC, photos, documents)

            ### **Home-Hunter:**
            
            - Booked
            - Attended
            - Cancelled
            - No-show rate (🟢 <20% / 🟡 20–40% / 🔴 >40%)
            
            ### **Owner:**
            
            - All viewings across all listings
            - Auto-confirm vs manual
            - Conversion funnel

            - Surveys bought
            - Surveys requested
            - Surveys completed

            ### **Owner:**
            
            - Surveys uploaded
            - Survey sales (Phase 2)
            - Visibility toggle

            - Login history
            - Device fingerprints
            - IP regions
            - Integration failures
            - Message violations
            - Support tickets
            - Admin actions (audit log)

        - **🧩  WF-A3 — Admin Users List**
            
            **(Global table of all Owners + Home-Hunters)**
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist (Dashfolio+ / Complete)**
            
            ### **Style**
            
            - Dark theme (Dashfolio+)
            - Yalla Yellow for active tabs
            - Blue for information blocks (roles)
            - Red/Amber/Green status colours
            
            ### **Table UI**
            
            - Large data table
            - Sticky header
            - Scrollable right side
            - Two-column layout:
                - Left = sticky filter panel
                - Right = user table
            - Row hover highlights
            - **Row colour flags**:
                - 🔴 Light red background → suspicious/fraud flagged
                - 🟡 Light amber → verification pending too long
            
            ### **Filters (designer-visible chips)**
            
            - All / Owners / Home-Hunters
            - Status: Active / Suspended / Needs Verification
            - Funnel (HH): Viewed → Saved → Booked → Attended → Offered
            - KYC: Verified / Pending / Missing
            - Flags: Fraud / Spam / High-risk
            - Country filter
            - Joined date (range)
            - Last active (range)
            
            ### **Columns (designer spec)**
            
            | **Column** | **Details** |
            | --- | --- |
            | User | Avatar + Name + Email + Phone (masked) |
            | Role | 🟦 Owner / 🟨 HH |
            | Status | Active / Suspended / Pending |
            | Last Active | “2h ago” |
            | Funnel Stage (HH only) | Viewed/Saved/Booked/Offered |
            | Listings (Owner only) | Count |
            | Verification | ✔ Complete / ⚠ Missing |
            | Trust Score | Good / Medium / Risk |
            | Country | e.g. UK |
            | Actions | “Open → WF-A2” |
            
            ### **Empty State**
            
            > “No users match these filters. Try clearing filters.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist (Complete)**
            
            ### **Endpoint**
            
            GET /admin/users
            
            ### **Supported Features**
            
            - Pagination (cursor-based)
            - Filters:
                - role, status, funnel_stage, country, kyc, flags
            - Search:
                - name, email, phone partial, country
            - Sorting:
                - last active (default)
                - joined date
                - trust score
                - number of listings (owner)
                - number of offers (HH)
            - Role-based visibility (support staff cannot see internal notes/flags)
            
            ### **Security**
            
            - All access logged in admin_audit_log
            - RBAC enforcement (support vs full admin)
            
            ### **Performance**
            
            - Index fields: email, phone, role, last_active
            - TTFB < 150ms
            - Return lightweight user objects (no heavy listings)
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey (Short)**
            
            Use cases:
            
            - Find any user fast
            - Diagnose issues
            - Detect fraud
            - Filter Home-Hunters by funnel stage
            - Identify inactive users
            - Access A2 User Detail
            - View overall user health
            
            ---
            
            # **4. Page Position**
            
            ```
            A1 Dashboard
               ↓
            A3 Users List
               ↓ click row →
            A2 User Detail
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            A3 provides the **master directory** of all platform users.
            
            Admins should instantly see:
            
            - Who they are
            - What role they have
            - Their behaviour level
            - Their trust score
            - Their KYC status
            - Their progress in the HH funnel
            - Their activity levels
            
            This page powers compliance, customer support, fraud detection, and funnel insights.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Solves**
            
            - Centralised user management
            - Fraud detection
            - Support triage
            - Quick entry into deep profile (A2)
            - Activation journey monitoring
            - Owner + Home-Hunter segmentation
            - Cross-country moderation

            ---
            
        - **🧩  WF-A4 — Admin Integrations & Status**
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist (Dashfolio+ + Colour Rules)**
            
            | **Status** | **Colour** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | 🟢 Green | #2ECC71 | Fully operational |
            | 🟡 Amber | #F1C40F | Degraded / partial |
            | 🔴 Red | #E74C3C | Down / repeated errors |
            | 🔵 Blue | #3498DB | Informational sections |
            | ⚫ Dark Base | #161616 / #212121 | Background |
            | 🟡 Yalla Yellow | #ECE269 | Accents, headers, active filters |
            
            UI Structure:
            
            - System Overview Strip (4 big horizontal badges)
            - Grid of Integration Cards (3×3 responsive)
            - Service Detail Drawer
            - Error Log Panel (right column)
            - Buttons: Ping Now, Retry, Export Logs
            - Avoid clutter, focus on diagnosis clarity
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist (Merged + Expanded)**
            
            - Endpoint: /admin/integrations/status
            - Cron: Every 5 minutes ping all services
            - Fallback if service unreachable: degrade gracefully
            - Log severity levels (info/warn/error/critical)
            - Webhook queue (Stripe) must show:
                - delivered
                - failed
                - pending
                - retry count
            - Developer must save:
                - latency
                - last_success
                - last_error
                - root_cause
                - event count (24 hrs)
            - Permissions:
                - Admin: full control
                - Support: read-only
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey**
            
            Admin uses A4 to:
            
            - Detect outages *before* users complain
            - Diagnose booking issues (WA/email)
            - Validate new listings pushing to portals
            - Check survey purchase reliability (Stripe)
            - See cron failures (EPC tasks, reminders)
            - Retry stuck messages or webhook events
            
            Critical for platform stability.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Position)**
            
            ```
            Admin Login
             → A1 Dashboard
               → A4 Integrations (this page)
                 → A5 Support (if user impacted)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            To deliver a **centralised, real-time view** of:
            
            - All third-party APIs
            - Background job engine
            - Database health
            - Messaging channels
            - Payment systems
            - Portal feeds
            - File storage
            
            Admin must see instantly:
            
            > “Is the system healthy? Where is the failure?”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Stripe failures (survey purchases / refunds)
            - WhatsApp message delivery delays
            - Email confirmations not sent
            - Portal pushes failing (Rightmove/Zoopla)
            - Cron worker behind schedule
            - Webhooks stuck in retry loops
            - Storage or CDN issues
            - Outage detection
            - Latency spikes
            
            ---
            
            # **7. Designer: What to Build in Framer**
            
            ### **A) Page Header**
            
            **Integrations & System Status**
            
            “Live monitoring of connected services.”
            
            ---
            
            ### **B) System Overview Strip (Top Row)**
            
            4 large metrics:
            
            1. **Platform Health Score (0–100)**
            2. **Errors (last 24h)**
            3. **Active Services Count**
            4. **Background Jobs Health**
            
            Colour-coded via severity.
            
            ---
            
            ### **C) Services Grid (Main Area)**
            
            **1. Stripe (Payments)**
            
            - Status + latency
            - Webhook: delivered/failed/retries
            - Last charge
            - Root-cause if error
            - Button: *View Webhooks*
            
            **2. WhatsApp (Twilio)**
            
            - Delivery rate (%)
            - Failed messages
            - Queue size
            - Test Message button
            
            **3. Email (SendGrid/Resend)**
            
            - Bounce rate
            - Recent template errors
            - Latency
            - Test Email button
            
            **4. File Storage (Airtable/S3)**
            
            - Upload success %
            - Thumbnail generation issues
            - Quota status
            
            **5. Database**
            
            - Response time
            - Slow queries today
            - Storage level
            
            **6. Cron Engine**
            
            - Jobs scheduled
            - Jobs completed
            - Missed jobs
            - Last run timestamp
            
            **7. Webhooks**
            
            - Pending
            - Failed
            - Stuck
            - Retry queue
            
            **8. Rightmove (Phase 2)**
            
            - Last feed push
            - Errors
            - Next scheduled push
            
            **9. Zoopla (Phase 2)**
            
            - Same fields as Rightmove
            
            ---
            
            ### **D) Service Detail Drawer**
            
            Clicking a card expands:
            
            - Full metric list
            - Error history
            - Raw error messages
            - Root cause
            - Retry button
            - “Flush queue” (Admin only)
            
            ---
            
            ### **E) Error Log Sidebar**
            
            Scrollable table:
            
            | **Time** | **Service** | **Level** | **Message** | **Metadata** |
            | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
            
            Filters:
            
            - By service
            - By severity
            - Last 24h / 7d
            
            Buttons:
            
            - Export logs
            - Clear filters
            
            Severity-coloured rows.
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            Tables needed:
            
            - integration_status
            - integration_logs
            - webhook_logs
            - retry_queue
            - cron_status
            - portal_feed_logs
            
            Cron logic:
            
            - Ping all services → record results
            - Degrade service after 3 failures
            - Mark “Critical” after 5
            
            Queue logic:
            
            - Webhook retry up to 5 times
            - Twilio queue auto-clean after 24h
            - Cron must mark missed jobs
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Platform Health | Weighted score across all services |
            | Error Count (24h) | Failures across integrations |
            | API Latency | Avg response time in ms |
            | Delivery Rate | For WhatsApp + Email |
            | Webhook Success | Delivered / Total |
            | Portal Push Success | Rightmove/Zoopla feed reliability |
            | Cron Reliability | Jobs completed vs scheduled |
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Logic**
            
            A4 directly influences conversion by identifying:
            
            - Messaging delays → fewer bookings
            - Email failures → fewer confirmations
            - Portal feed errors → incorrect listing data
            - Stripe outages → failed survey purchases
            
            ---
            
            # **11. Integration ID Logic**
            
            - integration_id
            - service_key (stripe, whatsapp, email…)
            - status
            - last_ping
            - last_error
            - latency_ms
            - error_count
            - root_cause
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - /ping/stripe
            - /ping/email
            - /ping/whatsapp
            - /ping/cron
            - /ping/database
            - /ping/rightmove (Phase 2)
            - /ping/zoopla (Phase 2)
            - Test harness (Phase 2)
            - Admin audit logging

            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Ticket Lifecycle**
            
            - open → default
            - pending → waiting for user
            - resolved → admin closed
            - reopened → if user messages again
            
            ### **SLA Logic**
            
            - Define by priority
            - Shown as a countdown
            - When expired → auto tag red + email alert
            
            ### **Classification Logic (Phase 2)**
            
            - NLP auto-detects:
                
                “payment”, “cancel”, “booking”, “bug”, “survey”
                
            - Auto-route to correct category
            
            ### **Ingestion Inputs**
            
            - Inbound email → piping
            - Inbound WhatsApp → webhook
            - Owner contact form → API
            - HH contact → API
            
            ### **GDPR**
            
            - Log everything
            - Allow export on request
            - Mask sensitive info
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Avg. response time | Key support metric |
            | SLA breach rate | Critical red flag |
            | Tickets per user | Track frustration |
            | Category frequency | Helps improve product |
            | Reopen rate | Poor solution quality |
            | Resolution time | Support efficiency |
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Logic**
            
            Support impacts:
            
            - Owner → happier → completes onboarding faster
            - HH → clearer → books more viewings
            - Faster replies → more trust → higher conversion
            - Reduced friction → fewer churns

            TKT-YYYYMMDD-XXXX
            
            - Unique
            - Date-linked
            - Helps export/import

            # **8. DEVELOPER REQUIREMENTS (Merged)**
            
            ### **Triggers**
            
            MVP:
            
            - Manual create
            - Convert support ticket → task
            - Manual creation from integration error
            
            Phase 2:
            
            - Owner buys package → auto tasks
            - Error logs → auto-create tasks
            - Survey upload → verification task
            - Portal push failure → auto task
            - Viewing clash → auto task
            
            ### **SLA & Alerts**
            
            - Overdue = 🔴
            - Email/SMS notification to assignee
            - “New Tasks” badge in Admin nav
            
            ### **Audit Trail**
            
            Every change logged:
            
            - Who
            - What
            - When
            - Before/after state

            - Completion speed
            - Overdue rate
            - Tasks per category
            - Tasks per staff member
            - Tasks per Owner
            - Tasks created from errors
            
            ✔ All from old version.

            # **1. DESIGNER CHECKLIST (FINAL)**
            
            ### **Page Structure**
            
            Build a **three-section dashboard**:
            
            1. **Revenue KPI Band**
            2. **Tabbed Financial Tables**
            3. **Slide-out Payment/Invoice/Payout Detail Panel**

            - Dashfolio+ dark theme
            - Yalla Yellow (#ECE269) for:
                - Positive trend icons
                - Active tabs
                - “Pay Now”
                - “Download CSV”
            - Bordered KPI cards, clean spacing
            - No charts (MVP) → only KPI cards + tables
            
            ### **Tabs**

            - **Invoices**
            - **Payouts**
            - **Failed Payments (Dunning)**
            - **Forecast (Phase 2)**
            
            ### **Tables**
            
            Every table must support:
            
            - Sorting
            - Filtering
            - Pagination
            - Slide-out detail panel on row click
            
            ---
            
            # **2. DEVELOPER CHECKLIST (FINAL)**
            
            ### **Endpoints Needed**
            
            ```
            GET /admin/revenue/summary
            GET /admin/transactions
            GET /admin/invoices
            GET /admin/payouts
            GET /admin/dunning
            POST /admin/payouts/pay
            POST /admin/refund
            POST /admin/invoice/resend
            ```
            
            ### **Stripe Integration**
            
            - Pull:
                - invoices
                - subscriptions
                - one-off charges
                - payment failures
                - dunning attempts
                - webhook status
            
            ### **Survey Marketplace**
            
            - revenue = SUM(survey_purchases.amount)
            - payout = 50% to uploader (configurable)
            - payout logs
            - fee split tracking
            
            ### **Taskboard Integration (A6) — REQUIRED**
            
            - When Owner buys service:
                
                → auto-create A6 task (EPC/Photos/Floorplan/QR Sign)
                
            
            ### **Refund Handling**
            
            - Full + partial refunds
            - Record:
                - refund reason
                - initiator (Admin/User/Stripe)
            - Auto-generate negative transaction entry
            
            ### **Dunning Logic**
            
            - Track retry attempts (1/3, 2/3…)
            - Show next retry timestamp
            - Show failure cause:
                - Card expired
                - Insufficient funds
                - 3DS auth needed
            
            ### **Stripe Webhook Health**
            
            - Store last event timestamp
            - If > 5 min → mark as degraded
            
            ### **Slide-out Panel Includes**
            
            - Transaction details
            - Invoice details
            - Survey payout history
            - Buttons:
                - Refund (full/partial)
                - Pay Now (payout)
                - Resend receipt
                - Create Task

            # **9. KPI DEFINITIONS (FOUNDERS LEVEL)**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **MRR** | All active recurring subscriptions |
            | **One-off Revenue** | EPC, Photography, Floorplan, Signs |
            | **Marketplace Revenue** | Survey sales (platform share) |
            | **Pending Payouts** | Money owed to survey uploaders |
            | **ARPU (Owner)** | Avg revenue per Owner |
            | **ARPU (HH)** | Avg rev per HH |
            | **Failed Payments** | Count in dunning |
            | **Refund Rate** | Refunds ÷ total transactions |

              + marketplace_revenue
              - refunds
              - payouts

            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ LEGAL & COMPLIANCE                         │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ Privacy Policy URL      [ /legal/privacy ] │
            │ Terms of Service URL    [ /legal/terms   ] │
            │ Cookie Policy URL       [ /legal/cookies ] │
            │ GDPR & Safety URL       [ /legal/gdpr    ] │
            │ Imprint (DE only) URL   [ /legal/imprint-de ]│
            │                                             │
            │ Helper text: used in header/footer/emails.  │
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ ADVANCED / FEATURE FLAGS  (FOUNDER ONLY)   │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ [on ] Survey Marketplace Live              │
            │ [on ] WhatsApp Notifications               │
            │ [off] Rightmove Integration (Phase 2)      │
            │ [off] Zoopla Integration (Phase 2)         │
            │ [off] Rental Applications (Beta)           │
            │ [off] Invite-only Mode                     │
            │                                             │
            │ Short helper text beneath each toggle.      │
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ ORGANISATION INFO                          │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ Company Name             [ Yalla House Ltd ]│
            │ Registered Address       [ …              ]│
            │ VAT Number               [ …              ]│
            │ Bank / IBAN (for payouts)[ …              ]│
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ BRANDING                                   │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ Logo upload (file)                         │
            │ Favicon upload                             │
            │ Primary Colour: [ #ECE269 ] (Yalla Yellow) │
            │ Dark Theme: Dashfolio+ presets             │
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ SECURITY & AUDIT LOGS                      │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ Table of recent admin actions:             │
            │ Time | Admin | Action | Section            │
            │ e.g. “2025-01-04 10:21 – Tarek – changed   │
            │ pricing_defaults.owner_pro_monthly”        │
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            
            ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │ GDPR TOOLS                                 │
            ├────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │ [ Export User Data ]  (enter user/email)   │
            │ [ Delete User ]       (red, double confirm)│
            │ [ Pseudonymise User ]                      │
            │ Note: operations logged in gdpr_events.    │
            └────────────────────────────────────────────┘
            ```
            
            Tone: **clean, form-like, no graphs, no scary DevOps UI.**
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. DESIGNER CHECKLIST (MERGED)**
            
            - **Overall layout**
                - Simple, non-scary settings page.
                - Left sidebar with clear sections.
                - Main area shows **one section at a time** (not everything at once).
                - Use standard Dashfolio+ form elements: inputs, dropdowns, toggles.
            - **Visual rules**
                - Dark theme base, soft contrasts.
                - Yalla Yellow **only** for:
                    - Primary “Save / Apply” buttons.
                    - Important warnings (e.g. GDPR delete).
                    - Maybe active section in sidebar.
                - No charts, no graphs.
            - **Sections to include (exactly as in old spec, plus extensions):**
                - General
                - Roles & Permissions
                - Language & Regions
                - Pricing & Plans (high-level)
                - Integrations (Keys & IDs)
                - Legal & Compliance (URLs only)
                - Advanced / Feature Flags (Founder only)
                - Organisation Info
                - Branding
                - Security & Audit Logs
                - GDPR Tools
            - **Copy tone**
                - Clear helper text under each control.
                - Emphasise safety: “Does not affect existing invoices,” “Used only for…”, etc.
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. DEVELOPER CHECKLIST (MERGED)**
            
            System Settings must:
            
            - Be **role-protected**:
                - Only **Founder** and **Admin** see A9.
                - **Advanced / Feature Flags** = Founder-only.
            - Persist into a structured system_settings table (or similar) with:
                - settings_version_id
                - edited_by_admin_id
                - updated_at
            - Use **safe defaults** if any field missing.
            - Be ready for **multi-tenant/multi-region** later (settings scoped per environment/tenant).
            - Avoid “free text JSON chaos”: strongly-typed keys, validated on write.
            
            ### **Key endpoints**
            
            ```
            GET  /admin/settings          # read all (filtered by role)
            PATCH/POST /admin/settings    # update sections
            
            GET  /admin/settings/audit    # audit history
            POST /admin/settings/gdpr/export
            POST /admin/settings/gdpr/delete
            POST /admin/settings/gdpr/pseudonymise
            ```
            
            All changes → admin_audit_log.
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. ADMIN JOURNEY (SHORT)**
            
            Admin / Founder uses A9 to:
            
            - Set general defaults (country, currency, emails).
            - Understand & oversee roles (Founder, Admin, Support).
            - Configure **language & regions** (UK now, DE later).
            - Set **high-level pricing** (Owner Pro, survey split).
            - Manage **API keys** for Stripe, WhatsApp, email, address lookup, portal placeholders.
            - Link **legal pages** used in footer/emails.
            - Toggle **feature flags** as the platform grows (Phase 2).
            - Maintain **organisation info** & branding.
            - Check **security & audit logs**.
            - Perform **GDPR exports/deletions**.
            
            Support staff **never** see A9.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. PURPOSE**
            
            - Centralise all **platform configuration**.
            - Give Founders control **without** always calling devs.
            - Keep **roles, language, legal, integrations, pricing defaults** in one place.
            - Prepare cleanly for **Germany / multi-region** and future features.
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. WHAT THIS PAGE SHOULD SOLVE**
            
            - No “who has the Stripe key?” chaos.
            - No “pricing hard-coded in three places” madness.
            - Easy to **roll out DE** later.
            - Only the right people see sensitive settings.
            - Easier **audits and compliance** (GDPR, legal).
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. WHAT TO BUILD IN FRAMER (SECTION BY SECTION)**
            
            You already have the content above; from the old spec we *explicitly keep*:
            
            - **General** fields exactly as:
                - Platform Name
                - Default Country
                - Default Currency
                - Support Email
                - Support WhatsApp Link
            - **Roles & Permissions**
                - Readable list of roles + short descriptions.
                - MVP: no complex UI for permission editing – just view matrix & note: “Advanced role management – Phase 2.”
            - **Language & Regions**
                - Primary language/region.
                - Disabled toggle for DE with copy: “MVP: UK only. Later: Germany / multi-language copy management.”
            - **Pricing & Plans**
                - Owner Pro monthly price.
                - Survey marketplace split (percentage for uploader vs platform) – **logic only**.
            - **Integrations**
                - Masked keys + simple “Copy / Rotate” actions.
            - **Legal & Compliance**
                - Plain URL fields; used for header/footer/email link generation.
            - **Advanced / Feature Flags**
                - Read-only or Founder-only toggles for:
                    - Survey Marketplace Live
                    - DE Region Enabled
                    - Invite-only mode
                    - Viewing auto-confirm (if you want to bubble it up)
                    - Rentals Beta
            - **Security & GDPR**
                - Logs & basic tools, with strong warnings.
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. SETTINGS STORAGE EXAMPLE (MERGED JSON SHAPE)**
            
            ```
            {
              "platform_name": "Yalla.House",
              "default_country": "UK",
              "default_currency": "GBP",
              "support_email": "support@yalla.house",
              "support_whatsapp_url": "https://wa.me/...",
              "roles": ["founder", "admin", "support"],
              "pricing_defaults": {
                "owner_pro_monthly": 12,
                "survey_marketplace_split": 0.5
              },
              "integrations": {
                "stripe_public_key": "pk_live_***",
                "stripe_secret_key": "sk_live_***",
                "whatsapp_api_key": "***",
                "email_api_key": "***",
                "address_lookup_api_key": "***",
                "rightmove_api_key": null,
                "zoopla_api_key": null
              },
              "legal": {
                "privacy_url": "/legal/privacy",
                "terms_url": "/legal/terms",
                "cookie_url": "/legal/cookies",
                "gdpr_url": "/legal/gdpr",
                "imprint_url": "/legal/imprint-de"
              },
              "regions": {
                "primary_language": "en-UK",
                "primary_region": "UK",
                "de_enabled": false
              },
              "feature_flags": {
                "survey_marketplace": true,
                "whatsapp_notifications": true,
                "rightmove_integration": false,
                "zoopla_integration": false,
                "invite_only_mode": false,
                "rental_applications_beta": false
              }
            }
            ```
            
            Versioning + audit live *outside* this blob.
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. KPI / META METRICS (LIGHT)**
            
            - **Regions Enabled** = how many regions active (now 1).
            - **Languages Live** = number of languages.
            - **Active Integrations** = count of configured keys.
            - **Last Settings Change** = timestamp.
            - **Who Last Edited** = admin ID.
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. RENTAL LOGIC**
            
            Nothing here is sale vs rent specific, but:
            
            - Pricing & Plans may later gain **separate plans** for rent vs sale.
            - Legal URLs for DE may include **rental-specific** info (but that’s content, not config).
            - Feature flag rental_applications_beta controls related surfaces elsewhere.

            # **4) What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Reduce fear (“Is this legit?”)
            - Explain the “no agent” model with authority
            - Establish emotional connection
            - Show professionalism
            - Encourage conversion → “List Your Place” CTA
            
            ---
            
            # **5) What the Designer Should Build**
            
            - Strong hero headline
            - 3-value pillars
            - “How It Works” horizontally
            - Creator story (founder-friendly, light narrative)
            - Trust indicators (security + partners)
            - Single CTA: **List Your Place**
            - Footer stays fully visible
            
            ---
            
            # **6) Developer Requirements**
            
            - All text editable in CMS/Notion DB (so you can tweak copy later).
            - Responsive mobile-first layout.
            - Load images from /public/assets/about/ folder.
            - Hero animation optional (phase 2).
            - Ensure contact → WhatsApp is the same endpoint as global header.
            
            ---
            
            # **7) Dummy Content (Hybrid Tone)**
            
            ### **Hero Section**
            
            **About Yalla.House**
            
            *A smarter, simpler way to sell or rent your place — without agents.*
            
            Yalla.House was built from one idea:
            
            **Owners deserve a transparent, modern, and fair way to list their home.** 
            
            [ **List Your Place** ]
            
            ---
            
            ## **Our Mission**
            
            To give every owner the tools, support, and confidence to sell or rent their place—
            
            **without expensive commissions or complicated processes.**
            
            We combine:
            
            - intuitive software
            - verified services (EPCs, photos, floorplans)
            - modern communication
            - and transparency at every stage
            
            ---
            
            ## **How Yalla.House Works**
            
            **1. List Your Place**
            
            Add details in minutes. We guide you step-by-step.
            
            **2. Publish Everywhere**
            
            Your place appears on Yalla.House + partner platforms.
            
            **3. Manage Viewings & Offers**
            
            A clean dashboard for bookings, messages, and real interest.
            
            **4. Sell or Rent Without Commission**
            
            Keep your equity. Stay in control.
            
            ---

            ✔ No hidden fees, no commissions
            
            ✔ Clear dashboard for viewings & offers
            
            ✔ Optional services (photography, EPC, signs, floorplans)
            
            ✔ Transparent tracking: views, inquiries, conversions
            
            ✔ Friendly support via WhatsApp
            
            ---
            
            ## **We Are Not Estate Agents**
            
            Yalla.House is a **technology platform**, not an estate agency.
            
            We do not negotiate on your behalf or act as an intermediary.
            
            You remain in full control — always.
            
            ---
            
            ## **Our Story**
            
            Yalla.House was started after experiencing first-hand
            
            **how stressful and expensive selling a place can be.**
            
            We decided to build something different:
            
            A platform that empowers owners, reduces friction, and offers
            
            **the clarity we all wished existed**.
