            - **🧩WF-P4-L1 — Privacy Policy (Stand-Alone Page)**
                
                # **Yalla.House Privacy Policy**
                
                *Last updated: 2025*
                
                (Version 1.0 — suitable for MVP launch, UK + EU compliant)
                
                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                Welcome to **Yalla.House** (“we”, “us”, “our”).
                
                We provide a platform that helps Owners list places, Home-Hunters book viewings, send offers, communicate, and (optionally) access professional services.
                
                We take privacy extremely seriously. This Privacy Policy explains:
                
                - What personal data we collect
                - How and why we use it
                - When we share it
                - Your rights under GDPR
                - How to contact us
                
                If you have any questions, contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are (Data Controller)**
                
                **Yalla.House Ltd**
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: [Insert once formed]
                
                Registered Address: [Insert once formed]
                
                Email: **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                We are the **Data Controller** for all personal information processed through the platform.
                
                ---
                
                # **3. What Personal Data We Collect**
                
                We collect only the minimum necessary data for the platform to operate.
                
                ### **A. Account Data (Owner + Home-Hunter)**
                
                - Name
                - Email address
                - Phone number
                - Password (hashed — never readable by us)
                - Country
                - Login logs (IP truncated/anonymised)
                
                ### **B. Owner Data (when listing a place)**
                
                - Property address
                - Photos, floorplans, EPC
                - Listing details (price, type, description)
                - Availability for viewings
                - Messages exchanged with Home-Hunters
                
                ### **C. Home-Hunter Data (when interacting with listings)**
                
                - Viewing bookings
                - Buying position (cash / mortgage-ready / browsing)
                - Messages to Owners
                - Offers made
                - Uploaded documents (optional, for verified offers)
                
                ### **D. Surveys Marketplace Data**
                
                If participating:
                
                - Uploaded surveys
                - Survey purchase records
                - Payment history (processed by Stripe, not stored by us)
                
                ### **E. Usage Data (analytics-safe)**
                
                - Page interactions
                - Session counts
                - Device type (mobile/desktop)
                - Funnel performance (views → inquiries → viewings → offers)
                
                We do **not** use fingerprinting or invasive tracking.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. How We Use Personal Data**
                
                We use your personal data only for the following purposes:
                
                ### **Platform Functionality**
                
                - Create and manage user accounts
                - Display listings
                - Manage messages
                - Handle bookings
                - Facilitate offers
                
                ### **Payments**
                
                - Process payments through Stripe
                - Issue receipts and invoices
                
                ### **Security**
                
                - Prevent fraud
                - Detect unusual activity
                - Protect users and the platform
                
                ### **Communications**
                
                - Send booking confirmations
                - Send operational updates
                - Send reminders (viewing reminders, offer status, etc.)
                
                ### **Legal Compliance**
                
                - Accounting and tax requirements
                - Law enforcement requests (where legally required)
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Legal Basis for Processing**
                
                We process your data under the following bases:
                
                | **Purpose** | **Legal Basis (GDPR)** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Running your account, listings, bookings | Contract (Art. 6(1)(b)) |
                | Payments | Contract + Legal obligation |
                | Messaging | Legitimate interest |
                | Analytics | Legitimate interest (privacy-safe) |
                | Marketing emails (optional) | Consent |
                | Safety & fraud prevention | Legitimate interest |
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Sharing Your Data**
                
                We only share data with **essential service providers**:
                
                ### **A. Stripe (Payments)**
                
                - Processes subscription and service payments
                - We do NOT store card details
                
                ### **B. Twilio / WhatsApp**
                
                - Sends verification codes
                - Sends booking updates
                
                ### **C. Email Provider**
                
                - Sends confirmations and OTPs
                
                ### **D. Cloud Hosting (EU)**
                
                - Secure encrypted data storage
                
                ### **We NEVER:**
                
                ❌ Sell personal data
                
                ❌ Share data with advertisers
                
                ❌ Use third-party analytics that require personal data (e.g., Google Analytics with IP retention)
                
                ---
                
                # **7. International Transfers**
                
                If data leaves the UK/EU (rare), it is protected by:
                
                - Standard Contractual Clauses (SCCs)
                - UK International Data Transfer mechanisms
                - Approved safeguards
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Data Security**
                
                We apply industry-grade controls:
                
                - Encryption in transit (TLS 1.2+)
                - Encryption at rest
                - Strict role-based access controls
                - Admin 2FA (Phase 2)
                - Backup & recovery procedures
                - Annual penetration testing**
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Data Retention**
                
                We keep personal data only for the minimum period allowed.
                
                ### **Automatically deleted or anonymised:**
                
                | **Data Type** | **Retention** | **Notes** |
                | --- | --- | --- |
                | Account identity (deleted user) | Removed immediately | GDPR |
                | Listings (property data) | Retained | Non-personal |
                | Messages | Anonymised | Sender replaced by “deleted user” |
                | Viewing logs | Anonymised | For funnel metrics |
                | Offers | Anonymised | For price analytics |
                | Surveys marketplace records | 6 years | Required for accounting |
                | Payment records | 6 years | Required by HMRC |
                | Error logs | 90 days | Security |
                | Support requests | 12 months | Quality & auditing |
                
                ---
                
                # **10. Your GDPR Rights**
                
                You have full GDPR rights:
                
                ### **✔ Access**
                
                Request a copy of everything we hold.
                
                ### **✔ Correction**
                
                Fix inaccurate details.
                
                ### **✔ Deletion**
                
                Delete your account any time.
                
                ### **✔ Portability**
                
                Download your data in standard format.
                
                ### **✔ Restriction / Objection**
                
                Stop certain types of processing.
                
                ### **✔ Withdraw Consent**
                
                Stop marketing at any time.
                
                Contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Cookies & Tracking**
                
                Yalla.House uses only essential cookies:
                
                ### **We do NOT use:**
                
                ❌ Tracking cookies
                
                ❌ Third-party advertising cookies
                
                ❌ Cross-site fingerprinting
                
                A separate **Cookie Policy** contains details.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Children’s Data**
                
                We do not knowingly collect or process data from individuals under 16.
                
                Accounts belonging to minors are deleted upon detection.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Changes to This Policy**
                
                We update this Privacy Policy when needed.
                
                When updates are significant, we will notify users via email.
                
                ---
                
                # **14. Contact**
                
                If you have concerns or requests:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                Or contact the UK ICO: https://ico.org.uk/
                
                ---
                
                # **✔ Privacy Policy Ready**
                
                Fully aligned with:
                
                - GDPR
                - Data Protection Act
                - Yalla.House’s data model
                - Marketplace, Owners, Home-Hunters, Surveys
                - Our plan to expand to Germany

                **Yalla.House — Terms of Service**
                
                *Last Updated: 2025*
                
                Version 1.0
                
                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                These Terms of Service (“Terms”) govern your access to and use of the **Yalla.House** platform (“the Platform”).
                
                By using Yalla.House, you agree to these Terms.
                
                If you do not agree, please do not use the Platform.
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are**
                
                **Yalla.House Ltd**
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: **[Insert once formed]**
                
                Registered Address: **[Insert]**
                
                Email: **support@yalla.house**
                
                Yalla.House is a **technology service**, not an estate agent.
                
                We provide tools that allow:
                
                - Owners to list a place
                - Home-Hunters to book viewings
                - Users to communicate
                - Users to purchase optional property-related services
                
                We do **not** negotiate, represent, or act on behalf of buyers or sellers.
                
                ---
                
                # **3. What Yalla.House Is (and Is Not)**
                
                ### **✔ Yalla.House IS:**
                
                - A property listing platform
                - A scheduling tool
                - A messaging system
                - A document-handling and survey marketplace
                - A payment-enabled service hub (via Stripe)
                
                ### **❌ Yalla.House IS NOT:**
                
                - An estate agency
                - A legal advisor
                - A financial advisor
                - A surveyor or valuation service
                - A party to any sale, rent, or offer
                
                All agreements between Owner and Home-Hunter are **strictly between those parties**.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. Your Account**
                
                You must provide accurate and truthful information when creating an account.
                
                You are responsible for:
                
                - Keeping your account secure
                - All actions taken under your login
                - Not sharing your password or verification codes
                
                If suspicious activity is detected, Yalla.House may temporarily lock or close the account.
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Eligibility**
                
                To use the Platform, you must:
                
                - Be at least 18 years old
                - Have legal capacity to enter contracts
                - Use the Platform only for lawful purposes
                
                We may suspend accounts that violate these Terms.
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Services Provided**
                
                ## **A. For Owners**
                
                The Platform allows Owners to:
                
                - Create listings
                - Upload photos, floorplans, and documents
                - Receive inquiries
                - Manage viewings
                - Receive offers
                - Access paid services (e.g., photos, floorplans, EPCs)
                - Participate in the Survey Marketplace
                
                ## **B. For Home-Hunters**
                
                The Platform allows Home-Hunters to:
                
                - View listings
                - Book viewings
                - Send messages
                - Make offers
                - Upload documents (optionally)
                - Buy surveys where available
                
                ## **C. For All Users**
                
                The Platform includes:
                
                - Scheduling services
                - Messaging tools
                - Account dashboards
                - Survey marketplace
                - Identity verification (optional, Phase 2)
                
                ---
                
                # **7. Payments**
                
                Payments for subscription plans, service packages, or surveys are handled securely through:
                
                **Stripe Payments Europe Ltd**
                
                Yalla.House does not store or handle card details.
                
                ### **Refunds:**
                
                Refund eligibility depends on the service type:
                
                - **Subscriptions**: non-refundable once the billing period has started
                - **One-off services**: refundable only before work has begun
                - **Survey purchases**: non-refundable once unlocked
                
                Disputes must be raised via **support@yalla.house**.
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Messaging & Bookings**
                
                Users agree not to use the Platform to:
                
                - Harass, abuse, or threaten others
                - Send spam or promotional messages
                - Misrepresent their identity
                - Circumvent the Platform to avoid fees
                - Schedule fraudulent bookings
                
                We reserve the right to limit messaging access if abused.
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Offers & Transactions**
                
                Offers made through Yalla.House are **non-binding expressions of interest**.
                
                They do not form a legal contract.
                
                A final sale, tenancy, or agreement occurs **outside the Platform**, between:
                
                - Owner
                - Home-Hunter
                - Their respective lawyers/solicitors
                
                Yalla.House is not responsible for:
                
                - Contract negotiations
                - Accuracy of listings
                - Fraud between users
                - Failed deals
                - Resulting losses or damages
                
                ---
                
                # **10. User Responsibilities**
                
                ### **Owners must:**
                
                - Provide accurate listing information
                - Ensure they have authority to list the property
                - Keep availability up to date
                - Respond to inquiries promptly
                - Comply with local property laws and disclosures
                
                ### **Home-Hunters must:**
                
                - Provide truthful information when booking or offering
                - Attend scheduled viewings or cancel responsibly
                - Not abuse the survey marketplace
                - Comply with relevant laws (anti-money laundering, KYC, etc.)
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Third-Party Services**
                
                Your use of Yalla.House may rely on services provided by:
                
                - Stripe
                - Twilio / WhatsApp
                - Email providers
                - Mapping services
                - Surveyor providers
                - Hosting and analytics platforms
                
                Their terms apply separately.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Content Ownership**
                
                ### **You retain ownership of:**
                
                - Photos
                - Listings
                - Surveys you upload
                - Messages
                - Documents
                
                ### **You grant Yalla.House a license to:**
                
                - Store
                - Display
                - Process
                - and transmit this content **for the purpose of running the Platform**
                
                We do not claim ownership of your material.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Prohibited Activities**
                
                You may NOT use the Platform to:
                
                - Post misleading or fraudulent listings
                - Intentionally mis-price a place
                - Upload harmful files
                - Reverse-engineer the Platform
                - Attempt to bypass payment systems
                - Access accounts that are not yours
                - Conduct illegal activity
                
                We may terminate accounts engaged in violations.
                
                ---
                
                # **14. Liability**
                
                To the maximum extent permitted by law:
                
                ### **Yalla.House is NOT liable for:**
                
                - Loss of income
                - Missed deals
                - Incorrect listing information
                - User fraud
                - Property defects
                - Damages caused by relying on uploaded surveys
                - Downtime or data loss
                
                Total liability is capped at the amount paid by you to Yalla.House in the previous 12 months.
                
                ---
                
                # **15. Suspension & Termination**
                
                We reserve the right to suspend or terminate accounts that:
                
                - Violate these Terms
                - Engage in fraud
                - Misuse the Platform
                - Exhibit unsafe behaviour
                
                Users may delete their accounts at any time.

            - **🧩WF-P4-L3 Cookie Policy**
                
                # **Yalla.House — Cookie Policy**
                
                *Last updated: 2025*
                
                Version 1.0 — UK GDPR + PECR compliant
                
                ---
                
                ## **1. Introduction**
                
                This Cookie Policy explains how **Yalla.House Ltd** (“we”, “us”, “our”) uses cookies and similar technologies on our website and platform.
                
                We believe in **privacy-first design**.
                
                This means we use only the minimum cookies required for the website and platform to function.
                
                If you have questions, contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                ## **2. What Are Cookies?**
                
                Cookies are small text files stored on your device when you visit a website.
                
                They help websites remember:
                
                - your login session
                - your preferences
                - required technical functions
                
                Some cookies are strictly necessary. Others are optional.
                
                Yalla.House uses *almost no optional cookies*.
                
                ---
                
                ## **3. Types of Cookies We Use**
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **A. Strictly Necessary Cookies (Required)**
                
                These cookies are essential for the platform to work.
                
                We use them for:
                
                - session management
                - secure login
                - fraud prevention
                - message and booking functionality
                - Stripe payments
                
                You **cannot disable** these cookies because the platform will not function without them.
                
                Examples:
                
                - session_id
                - auth_token
                - csrf_token
                - Stripe payment cookies
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **B. Functional Cookies (Minimal Use)**
                
                Used to remember basic preferences, such as:
                
                - language preference
                - dashboard theme (Dashfolio+)
                
                These cookies **do not track** you across sites.
                
                Examples:
                
                - lang_pref
                - ui_theme
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **C. Analytics Cookies (Privacy-Safe Only)**
                
                We use **privacy-friendly, cookieless analytics** by default (e.g., Plausible).
                
                This means:
                
                - no personal data
                - no IP addresses
                - no cookies
                - no user-level tracking
                
                If we add optional cookies later (Phase 2), they will require consent.
                
                ### **❌**
                
                ### **D. No Advertising Cookies**
                
                We do **not** use:
                
                - Google Ads cookies
                - Facebook pixel
                - Remarketing trackers
                - Third-party behavioural profiling
                
                Zero advertising cookies.
                
                Zero cross-site tracking.
                
                ---
                
                ## **4. Third-Party Cookies**
                
                Some external providers place essential cookies:
                
                ### **✔ Stripe**
                
                Used for secure payments. Required by law for fraud protection.
                
                ### **✔ Twilio / WhatsApp**
                
                Used for login verification and operational messaging.
                
                ### **✔ Framer (if embedded components are used)**
                
                May set minimal functional cookies necessary for UI rendering.
                
                ---
                
                ## **5. Cookie Duration**
                
                | **Type** | **Duration** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Session cookies | Deleted when you close your browser |
                | Functional cookies | 30–180 days |
                | Stripe cookies | 12–24 months (PCI compliance) |
                | Analytics (cookieless) | N/A |
                
                ---
                
                ## **6. How to Control Cookies**
                
                You can control cookies through your browser:
                
                - Chrome: Settings → Privacy → Cookies
                - Safari: Preferences → Privacy
                - Firefox: Options → Privacy
                
                Blocking **strictly necessary cookies** will break the platform.
                
                ---
                
                ## **7. Legal Basis**
                
                Under GDPR + PECR:
                
                | **Cookie Type** | **Legal Basis** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Strictly necessary | Legitimate Interest |
                | Functional | Legitimate Interest |
                | Analytics | Legitimate Interest (cookieless) |
                | Advertising | Not used |
                
                ---
                
                ## **8. Updates to This Policy**
                
                We may update this Cookie Policy as our services evolve.
                
                Significant changes will be notified via email or platform notification.
                
                ---
                
                ## **9. Contact**
                
                For questions or concerns:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                📍 Address: [Insert when company formed]
                
                ---
                
            - **🧩WF-P4-L4 — GDPR & Safety (Stand-Alone Page)**
                
                # **GDPR & Safety Page**
                
                *Clear. Professional. Fully GDPR-compliant. Ready for your Legal Hub (WF-P4).*
                
                ---
                
                # **Yalla.House — GDPR & Safety Statement**
                
                *Last Updated: 2025*
                
                Version 1.0
                
                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                At **Yalla.House**, safety and privacy are core values.
                
                We are committed to complying with:
                
                - UK GDPR
                - EU GDPR (for EU users)
                - Data Protection Act 2018
                - PECR
                - TMG §5 for Germany (when expanded)
                
                This page summarises:
                
                - How we protect your data
                - How we secure communication
                - How we verify users (optional)
                - How surveys and documents are handled
                - What safety controls exist for Owners and Home-Hunters
                
                This page does **not replace** the Privacy Policy — it complements it.
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are**
                
                **Data Controller:**
                
                Yalla.House Ltd
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: **[Insert once formed]**
                
                Address: **[Insert]**
                
                Email: **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **3. Data Minimisation**
                
                We only collect the minimum data required to provide the service.
                
                ### **We do NOT collect:**
                
                - unnecessary personal data
                - behavioural tracking across websites
                - advertising identifiers
                - sensitive data (ethnicity, religion, health, etc.)
                
                ### **We ONLY process:**
                
                - Account info
                - Listing info
                - Booking + offer info
                - Messages
                - Optional documents for verification (Phase 2)
                - Surveys
                
                Nothing more.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. Data Security**
                
                We use industry-grade protection:
                
                ### **Technical Measures**
                
                ✔ Encryption in transit (TLS 1.2+)
                
                ✔ Encryption at rest
                
                ✔ Database access control
                
                ✔ Passwords hashed with bcrypt
                
                ✔ Regular backups
                
                ✔ Isolated production environment
                
                ✔ Monitoring and anomaly detection
                
                ### **Organisational Measures**
                
                ✔ Role-based access (Support sees less than Admin)
                
                ✔ No external contractors get direct DB access
                
                ✔ Mandatory 2FA for Admins (Phase 2)
                
                ✔ Annual penetration testing (Phase 2)
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Your Rights Under GDPR**
                
                You have full control of your data:
                
                - Access
                - Correction
                - Deletion
                - Restriction
                - Portability
                - Objection
                - Withdraw consent
                
                To exercise your rights:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Data Retention (How Long We Keep Data)**
                
                We follow strict GDPR-compliant retention limits:
                
                | **Data Type** | **Retention** | **Notes** |
                | --- | --- | --- |
                | Account data | Until deletion | Deleted when account removed |
                | Listings | Permitted indefinitely | Not personal data |
                | Messages | Anonymised after deletion | Sender replaced with “deleted user” |
                | Viewings | Anonymised | For platform analytics |
                | Offers | Anonymised | For pricing metrics |
                | Surveys | 6 years | Required for financial compliance |
                | Payments | 6 years | HMRC regulation |
                | Logs | 90 days | Security only |
                
                Full matrix already provided separately.
                
                ---
                
                # **7. Surveys & Document Safety**
                
                The Survey Marketplace requires special handling.
                
                ### **When Owners Upload Surveys**
                
                - Stored encrypted
                - Reviewed manually (no sensitive personal data allowed)
                - Made available only when purchased
                - Access is logged for security
                
                ### **When Home-Hunters Upload Documents**
                
                (e.g., proof of funds / ID verification, optional Phase 2)
                
                - Only visible to the Owner after approval
                - Auto-deletion after the offer completes or 90 days
                - Never shared with third parties
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Messaging & Communication Safety**
                
                Messages inside Yalla.House are:
                
                - Encrypted in transit
                - Logged only for safety
                - Monitored for abuse using automated detection
                - Not accessible by non-admin staff
                
                Abusive behaviour results in account restriction or removal.
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Viewing Safety (Physical Safety)**
                
                For Owners & Home-Hunters:
                
                ### **We strongly recommend:**
                
                - Not sharing full personal details before a viewing
                - Always attending viewings in pairs when concerned
                - Using the platform’s messaging system (not private numbers)
                - Cancelling suspicious bookings
                - Reporting abusive users via **support@yalla.house**
                
                Yalla.House may suspend accounts for unsafe behaviour.
                
                ---
                
                # **10. Fraud Prevention**
                
                We apply multiple fraud controls:
                
                - Suspicious-activity detection
                - Rate-limited messaging
                - Identity verification (Phase 2 optional)
                - Document verification for serious offers
                - Monitoring for survey abuse
                - Manual review of flagged activity
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Data Transfers**
                
                Data is stored in the UK/EU.
                
                If transferred abroad, it is protected by:
                
                - Standard Contractual Clauses
                - UK Addendum
                - Approved security measures
                
                We never transfer data to unsafe jurisdictions.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Children’s Safety**
                
                The platform is **not for users under 16**.
                
                We delete any detected minor accounts.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Contact & Complaints**
                
                📧 privacy@yalla.house
                
                Or contact the UK ICO: https://ico.org.uk/
                
                ---
                
            
            ---

    - **UNIFIED DATA MODEL (MASTER BLUEPRINT)**
        
        **This covers ALL users, ALL listings, ALL surveys, ALL transactions, ALL workflows.**
        
        Nothing outside this model will be required for your MVP.
        
        ---
        
        # **5.1 ENTITY MAP (TOP-LEVEL RELATIONSHIPS)**
        
        Here is the high-level map:
        
        ```
        User
         ├─ Listings (Owner only)
         │    ├─ Viewings
         │    ├─ Messages
         │    ├─ Offers / Applications
         │    ├─ Documents (EPC, floorplan, etc.)
         │    └─ Surveys (uploaded by Owner)
         │
         ├─ Saved Places (HH only)
         ├─ Viewings (HH only)
         ├─ Offers (HH only)
         ├─ Messages
         ├─ Surveys Purchased
         └─ Payments (Stripe)
        
        Admin
         ├─ Tasks
         ├─ Tickets
         ├─ Audit Log
         └─ System Settings
        ```
        
        Everything connects.
        
        ---
        
        # **5.2 CORE TABLES**
        
        Below is the complete reference list of required tables.
        
        ### **(A) USERS**
        
        ```
        id (uuid)
        role (owner | home-hunter | admin)
        name
        email
        phone
        password_hash
        country
        created_at
        last_login_at
        trust_score (0–100)
        verification_status (none | partial | verified)
        devices (json)
        flags (json)
        ```
        
        ### **(B) PROPERTIES / LISTINGS**
        
        ```
        id (uuid)
        owner_id
        address_full
        postcode
        bedrooms
        bathrooms
        size_m2
        description
        price
        rent
        status (draft | live | archived)
        photos (json)
        features (json)
        compliance_docs (json)
        availability (json)
        created_at
        updated_at
        ```
        
        ### **(C) VIEWINGS**
        
        ```
        id
        place_id
        owner_id
        hh_id
        slot_datetime
        status (requested | confirmed | cancelled | attended | no-show)
        notes
        created_at
        ```
        
        ### **(D) MESSAGES (OWNER ↔ HH, MASKED)**
        
        ```
        id
        thread_id
        sender_id
        receiver_id
        place_id
        message_text
        attachments (json)
        origin (web | whatsapp | email)
        created_at
        ```
        
        ### **(E) OFFERS / RENTAL APPLICATIONS**
        
        ```
        id
        hh_id
        place_id
        amount
        type (sale | rent)
        status (pending | accepted | declined | withdrawn)
        position (queue_index)
        extra_terms (json)
        created_at
        ```
        
        ### **(F) SURVEYS**
        
        ```
        id
        place_id
        uploader_id
        survey_type
        file_url
        status (uploaded | pending_verification | approved | rejected | flagged)
        uploaded_at
        verified_at
        metadata (json)
        ```
        
        ### **(G) SURVEY PURCHASES**
        
        ```
        id
        survey_id
        hh_id
        amount
        purchased_at
        ```
        
        ### **(H) SURVEY PAYOUTS**
        
        ```
        id
        survey_id
        uploader_id
        amount
        status (pending | paid | error)
        created_at
        paid_at
        ```
        
        ### **(I) TASKS**
        
        ```
        id
        title
        category
        assigned_to
        priority
        status
        place_id
        user_id
        created_at
        due_at
        history (json)
        ```
        
        ### **(J) SUPPORT TICKETS**
        
        ```
        id
        user_id
        place_id
        category
        priority
        status
        origin (web | whatsapp | email)
        sla_due
        created_at
        ```
        
        ### **(K) SYSTEM SETTINGS**
        
        ```
        id
        data (json)
        updated_by_admin_id
        updated_at
        version
        ```
        
        ### **(L) REVENUE / TRANSACTIONS**
        
        ```
        id
        user_id
        type (subscription | service | survey_purchase)
        source (stripe | marketplace | manual)
        amount
        fee
        net_amount
        status
        created_at
        raw_stripe_event (json)
        ```
        
        ### **(M) AUDIT LOG**
        
        ```
        id
        admin_id
        entity_type
        entity_id
        action
        before (json)
        after (json)
        created_at
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5.3 DERIVED / COMPOSITE VIEWS**
        
        (Not collections, but server-side aggregated responses)
        
        ### **User Overview (A2)**
        
        Returns:
        
        - user info
        - listings summary
        - HH funnel
        - viewings summary
        - offers
        - messages summary
        - surveys (uploaded + purchased)
        - flags
        - trust score
        - device info
        - audit snippet
        
        ### **Admin Dashboard (A1)**
        
        - User counts (active, new)
        - Listings live/drafts
        - Viewings today/week
        - Support tickets SLA
        - Marketplace metrics
        - Revenue KPIs
        
        ---
        
    - **WORKFLOW LOGIC (ALL AUTOMATIONS & TRIGGERS)**
        
        This is the “brain” behind the platform.
        
        Every action triggers a workflow.
        
        ---
        
        # **6.1 USER WORKFLOWS**
        
        ### **(A) Sign Up**
        
        1. Create user
        2. Create empty profile
        3. Send verification email
        4. Add to Admin feed (“New User”)
        
        ### **(B) Owner Creates Listing**
        
        1. Owner enters address
        2. System fetches address metadata
        3. Create listing in **draft** state
        4. Save wizard progress
        5. When >80% complete → “listing_ready” event
        6. When Publish → Listing becomes **live**
        7. Admin A6 task created (Phase 2 optional)
        
        ### **(C) HH Books Viewing**
        
        1. HH picks slot
        2. Create viewing event
        3. Notify Owner
        4. Add to calendar (Phase 2)
        5. Status = “requested”
        6. When Owner confirms → “confirmed”
        7. After slot → “attended” or “no-show”
        
        ### **(D) HH Sends Message**
        
        1. Create masked identity
        2. Write message
        3. Owner notified
        4. Thread created if new
        5. Admin sees in A5 if flagged
        
        ### **(E) HH Makes Offer / Application**
        
        1. Save offer
        2. Add queue position
        3. Notify Owner
        4. Add to HH “Offers” section
        5. If Owner accepts → “offer_accepted” event
        6. Remove other pending offers (optional)
        
        ---
        
        # **6.2 SURVEY WORKFLOWS (MARKETPLACE)**
        
        ### **(A) Owner / HH Uploads Survey**
        
        1. File scanning (AV)
        2. Validate format
        3. Create survey record
        4. Set status: uploaded
        5. Admin notified in A7
        6. Auto-create A6 task (Phase 2)
        
        ### **(B) Admin Verifies Survey**
        
        1. Check quality
        2. Check <12 months
        3. Approve or reject
        4. If approved → visible in HH & Owner dashboards
        5. If rejected → notify uploader
        
        ### **(C) HH Buys Survey**
        
        1. Stripe payment
        2. Purchase saved
        3. Revenue logged
        4. Uploader generates payout entry
        5. HH can download
        6. Owner notified (optional)
        
        ### **(D) Release Payout**
        
        1. Admin initiates Stripe payout
        2. Mark payout = “paid”
        3. Log in A8 revenue
        4. Update A7 survey history
        
        ---
        
        # **6.3 ADMIN WORKFLOWS**
        
        ### **(A) Support Ticket Arrives**
        
        1. Store ticket
        2. Auto-assign if rule matches (Phase 2)
        3. SLA timer starts
        4. If SLA breach → escalate
        
        ### **(B) Task Creation**
        
        Triggered by:
        
        - Admin manually
        - Support conversion
        - Survey verification
        - Error log (A4)
        - Payment failures (optional)
        
        ### **(C) Payment Events**
        
        Stripe webhooks:
        
        - invoice.paid → log revenue
        - invoice.payment_failed → create ticket + task
        - charge.refunded → update A8
        - payout.paid → mark PT-*
        
        ### **(D) Integration Errors (A4)**
        
        1. Ping failure
        2. Write integration_logs
        3. Create task (Phase 2)
        4. Admin sees red component in A4
        
        ---
        
        # **6.4 SYSTEM-WIDE BEHAVIOUR LOGIC**
        
        ### **STATUS CHANGE RULES**
        
        Whenever something moves (viewing, offer, survey), system logs:
        
        ```
        event_log: {
          entity_type,
          entity_id,
          old_status,
          new_status,
          timestamp,
          actor_id
        }
        ```
        
        ### **NOTIFICATIONS (MVP = Email)**
        
        - Signup
        - Listing published
        - Viewing booked / confirmed
        - Offer submitted
        - Survey approved
        - Survey purchased
        - Payout complete
        - Payment failed
        
        Phase 2:
        
        - WhatsApp
        - Push notifications
        
        ---
        
        # **6.5 TRUST & FRAUD LOGIC (LIGHTWEIGHT MVP)**
        
        ### **Trust Score (0–100)**
        
        Components:
        
        - KYC complete (20)
        - Device consistency (10)
        - Message behaviour (10)
        - Offer/viewing behaviour (20)
        - Flags (–20 each)
        - Survey purchases/sales (10)
        - Account age (10)
        
        ### **Flags detected automatically**
        
        - Repeated cancellations
        - Spammy messages
        - Suspicious device changes
        - Payment failures
        - Survey mismatch
        
        Flags appear in:
        
        - A2 User Detail
        - A3 Users List (highlight row)
        - A1 KPI “Users at risk”
    - **PLATFORM EMAIL MATRIX (ALL TRIGGERS + TEMPLATES)**
        
        # **SECTION 7 — PLATFORM EMAIL MATRIX (ALL TRIGGERS + TEMPLATES)**
        
        **Covers all email notifications for Owners, Home-Hunters, and Admins.**
        
        This section is *complete* for MVP + allows Phase-2 expansion.
        
        ---
        
        # **7.1 EMAIL SYSTEM OVERVIEW**
        
        ### **Provider**
        
        - MVP: **SendGrid / Resend / Postmark**
        - API-based (no SMTP)
        - All emails logged in: email_logs table
        
        ### **Format**
        
        - Header + body + CTA button
        - Footer includes:
            - Privacy Policy URL
            - Terms URL
            - Support email (from A9 settings)
        
        ### **Sender Address**
        
        - **notifications@yalla.house**
        - Reply-to = support@yalla.house
        
        ### **Brand Rules**
        
        - Black (#161616)
        - White (#FFFFFF)
        - Yalla Yellow (#ECE269) for CTA buttons
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐7.2 FULL EMAIL MATRIX (MVP)**
        
        **Grouped into 4 categories: Account, Listings, Marketplace, Payments**
        
        Every email has: Trigger → Recipient → Payload → Template Block.
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ CATEGORY A — ACCOUNT & PROFILE EMAILS**
        
        ---
        
        ## **A1 — Welcome Email (Sign Up)**
        
        **Trigger:** User creates account
        
        **Recipient:** Owner OR Home-Hunter
        
        **Payload:** name
        
        **Purpose:** Confirm account, prompt verification/login.
        
        **Template Blocks:**
        
        - Welcome headline
        - “Your account is now active”
        - CTA: **Go to Dashboard**
        
        ---
        
        ## **A2 — Email Verification (Optional MVP)**
        
        **Trigger:** If email confirmation is enabled
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** verify_url
        
        **Purpose:** Reduce fraud
        
        ---
        
        ## **A3 — Password Reset Request**
        
        **Trigger:** User clicks “Forgot password”
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** reset_url
        
        **Purpose:** Secure account recovery
        
        ---
        
        ## **A4 — Password Reset Confirmation**
        
        **Trigger:** After successful reset
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** none
        
        **Purpose:** Security notification
        
        ---
        
        ## **A5 — Account Flagged (Risk / Fraud)**
        
        **Trigger:** system adds new flag (from Section 6.5)
        
        **Recipient:** Admin ONLY
        
        **Payload:** user_id, flag_reason
        
        **Purpose:** Admin quick reaction
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ CATEGORY B — LISTINGS, VIEWINGS & MESSAGES**
        
        ---
        
        ## **B1 — Listing Published**
        
        **Trigger:** Owner publishes listing
        
        **Recipient:** Owner
        
        **Payload:** place_id, address
        
        **Purpose:** Confirmation + what happens next
        
        ---
        
        ## **B2 — Viewing Request (HH → Owner)**
        
        **Trigger:** HH books a slot
        
        **Recipient:** Owner
        
        **Payload:** hh_name, place_id, slot
        
        **Purpose:** Ask Owner to confirm
        
        ---
        
        ## **B3 — Viewing Confirmation (Owner → HH)**
        
        **Trigger:** Owner confirms
        
        **Recipient:** HH
        
        **Payload:** slot, address
        
        ---
        
        ## **B4 — Viewing Cancelled**
        
        **Trigger:** Either side cancels
        
        **Recipient:** Both parties
        
        **Payload:** slot, initiator
        
        ---
        
        ## **B5 — New Message Received**
        
        **Trigger:** Message created (masked)
        
        **Recipient:** Owner or HH
        
        **Payload:** message_preview, thread_url
        
        **Purpose:** Pull users back to platform
        
        ---
        
        ## **B6 — Offer Submitted**
        
        **Trigger:** HH makes offer
        
        **Recipient:** Owner
        
        **Payload:** amount, place_id
        
        ---
        
        ## **B7 — Offer Accepted**
        
        **Trigger:** Owner clicks “Accept”
        
        **Recipient:** HH
        
        **Payload:** amount, address
        
        ---
        
        ## **B8 — Offer Declined**
        
        **Trigger:** Owner declines
        
        **Recipient:** HH
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ CATEGORY C — SURVEY MARKETPLACE EMAILS**
        
        ---
        
        ## **C1 — Survey Uploaded (Owner/HH)**
        
        **Trigger:** User uploads file
        
        **Recipient:** Admin
        
        **Payload:** survey_id, uploader_id, place_id
        
        **Purpose:** Begin verification
        
        ---
        
        ## **C2 — Survey Approved**
        
        **Trigger:** Admin approves
        
        **Recipient:** Uploader
        
        **Payload:** survey_id
        
        **Purpose:** Celebrate + explain revenue model
        
        ---
        
        ## **C3 — Survey Rejected**
        
        **Trigger:** Admin rejects
        
        **Recipient:** Uploader
        
        **Payload:** reason
        
        ---
        
        ## **C4 — Survey Purchased**
        
        **Trigger:** HH buys survey
        
        **Recipient:**
        
        - HH (buyer)
        - Uploader (seller)
        - Admin (audit BCC optional)
        
        **Payload:** survey_id, purchase_amount
        
        **Purpose:** Receipt + access link
        
        ---
        
        ## **C5 — Survey Payout Released**
        
        **Trigger:** Admin pays uploader
        
        **Recipient:** Uploader
        
        **Payload:** payout_amount, payout_id
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ CATEGORY D — PAYMENTS, SUBSCRIPTIONS & BILLING**
        
        ---
        
        ## **D1 — Payment Receipt (Stripe)**
        
        **Trigger:** invoice.paid webhook
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** amount, invoice_url
        
        ---
        
        ## **D2 — Payment Failed**
        
        **Trigger:** invoice.payment_failed
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** retry_date, fix_payment_url
        
        **Secondary recipient:** Admin (alert)
        
        ---
        
        ## **D3 — Refund Processed**
        
        **Trigger:** refund event
        
        **Recipient:** User
        
        **Payload:** amount, reason
        
        ---
        
        ## **D4 — Subscription Renewal Reminder (Optional MVP)**
        
        Sent **3 days before** renewal
        
        **Trigger:** Cron job
        
        **Recipient:** Owner
        
        ---
        
        ## **D5 — Subscription Cancelled**
        
        **Trigger:** User or admin cancels
        
        **Recipient:** Owner
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ CATEGORY E — ADMIN & SYSTEM OPERATIONS**
        
        ---
        
        ## **E1 — Integration Failure Alert (A4)**
        
        **Trigger:** integration_logs new error
        
        **Recipient:** Admin
        
        **Payload:** service, error_message
        
        ---
        
        ## **E2 — SLA Breach (A5)**
        
        **Trigger:** Support ticket overdue
        
        **Recipient:** Admin
        
        **Payload:** ticket_id, user
        
        ---
        
        ## **E3 — Task Assigned (A6)**
        
        **Trigger:** Task created + assigned
        
        **Recipient:** Assigned admin
        
        **Payload:** task_id, title, due_date
        
        ---
        
        ## **E4 — Daily Admin Summary (Optional MVP)**
        
        1 email every morning
        
        **Recipient:** Admin
        
        Includes:
        
        - New Owners yesterday
        - New HH
        - New listings
        - Viewings
        - Revenue last 24h
        - Integration errors
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ 7.3 GLOBAL EMAIL BUILDING BLOCKS**
        
        ### **EMAIL HEADER**
        
        - Yalla.House logo
        - Black strip
        - No navigation (strictly notifications)
        
        ### **EMAIL FOOTER**
        
        - “You are receiving this email because you have an account on Yalla.House”
        - Privacy Policy link
        - Terms link
        - Unsubscribe (only for marketing, not transactional)
        - Support email
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ 7.4 API PAYLOAD FORMAT (for devs)**
        
        All emails MUST use this JSON:
        
        ```
        {
          "to": "user@example.com",
          "template": "welcome_email",
          "data": {
            "name": "Sarah",
            "address": "14 King Street",
            "amount": "£620,000",
            "slot": "2025-02-12 11:00",
            "verify_url": "...",
            "reset_url": "...",
            "invoice_url": "..."
          }
        }
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ 7.5 EMAIL RATE LIMITS / SAFETY**
        
        - Max **3 emails** per user per hour (except critical like password reset)
        - Message notifications: combine if >3 in 10 minutes
        - Support ticket notifications: only 1 until status updates
        - Admin error alerts: combine into digest if >5 in 30 minutes
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ 7.6 FUTURE EXPANSION (PHASE 2)**
        
        - WhatsApp notifications
        - Push notifications (mobile PWA)
        - Email categories for A/B testing
        - Template editor inside A9 settings
        - Multilingual templates (EN/DE)
        
        ---
        
        # **⭐ 7.7 30-SECOND FOUNDER SUMMARY**
        
        This email matrix is:
        
        - **Complete for MVP**
        - Covers ALL workflows (Users, Listings, Marketplace, Payments, Admin)
        - Scalable
        - Developer-ready with templates & triggers
        - No marketing fluff, only operational notifications
        
        ---
        
    - **MOBILE RESPONSIVENESS & COMPONENT RULES**
        
        # **SECTION 8 — MOBILE RESPONSIVENESS & COMPONENT RULES**
        
        This section defines **how every screen behaves on mobile vs desktop**, and how shared components (cards, tables, sidebars, modals) must adapt. It applies to:
        
        - **Owners** (WF-O1–O5)
        - **Home-Hunters** (WF-H1–H6)
        - **Admin** (WF-A1–A9)
        - **Public pages** (P1–P5)
        
        The goal: **one coherent feel**, no surprises, and very little extra design work in Framer.
        
        ---
        
        ## **8.1 Breakpoints & General Rules**
        
        ### **Breakpoints**
        
        - **Mobile:** < 768px (primary target, especially for HH and Owners on the go)
        - **Tablet:** 768–1199px
        - **Desktop:** ≥ 1200px (admin will live here most of the time)
        
        **Rule of thumb:**
        
        Design **mobile-first**, then scale up to desktop. Framer/Figma structure must start from mobile layout.
        
        ---
        
        ### **Global Behaviour Rules**
        
        1. **Sidebars**
            - Desktop: fixed left sidebar (Owner / HH / Admin apps).
            - Tablet: collapsible sidebar with icon-only state.
            - Mobile: hidden by default, open via hamburger/top menu.
        2. **Cards vs Tables**
            - Mobile: **cards** (stacked vertically).
            - Desktop: **tables** (for dense listing data in Admin).
        3. **Modals**
            - Desktop: center modal / side drawer.
            - Mobile: full-screen sheet sliding from bottom or top.
        4. **Typography**
            - Mobile base: 14–16px.
            - Desktop base: 15–16px, headings upscaled proportionally.
            - Always maintain **minimum tap target 44px** height for buttons.
        5. **Horizontal scrolling**
            - **Avoid** horizontal scroll for main content wherever possible.
            - If a table must overflow on mobile → enable horizontal scroll **within the component** with a visible hint (“Swipe to see more columns”).
        
        ---
        
        ## **8.2 Layout Behaviour by Area**
        
        ### **8.2.1 Public Pages (WF-P1–P5)**
        
        **Includes:** Marketing pages, public property page WF-O5 / P5.
        
        - Mobile:
            - Single-column content.
            - Sticky bottom CTA **[Arrange a Visit]** or **[Contact owner]** on property pages.
            - Image gallery = horizontal scrollable carousel.
        - Desktop:
            - Two-column layout for property:
                - Left: images, description, details.
                - Right: booking/CTA panel (H1/H3 integration).
        - Shared rules:
            - Header: compresses to hamburger on mobile.
            - Footer: stacked links on mobile, inline on desktop.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.2.2 Owner App (WF-O1–O5)**
        
        - Desktop:
            - **Fixed sidebar** (Listings, Inquiries, Calendar, Docs, Settings).
            - Main content area with tables and cards.
        - Mobile:
            - Sidebar → top-left menu.
            - Every key table view (listings, inquiries) must have a **card view**:
                - Listing card: photo, address, price, status chips, key actions.
                - Inquiry card: HH name, property, last message preview, CTA to open.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.2.3 Home-Hunter App (WF-H1–H6)**
        
        Most HH traffic will be **mobile-first** (Rightmove → Yalla deep links).
        
        - Mobile:
            - Bottom or top navigation emphasizing:
                - H1 Dashboard
                - H2 Inbox
                - H3 Saved / Bookings
            - **Sticky CTAs** when relevant:
                - “Arrange a Visit”
                - “Make Offer”
                - “View Survey”
        - Desktop:
            - Sidebar with sections H1–H6.
            - Split layout for Inbox (H2), Bookings (H3/H4) and Offers (H5):
                - Left = list.
                - Right = detail.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.2.4 Admin App (WF-A1–A9)**
        
        Admin is **heavily desktop-first**, but must remain usable on mobile.
        
        - Desktop:
            - **Permanent left sidebar** (A1–A9).
            - Content can use 2–3 columns: KPIs, tables, logs.
        - Tablet:
            - Sidebar collapses to icons.
        - Mobile:
            - Sidebar collapses to a top drawer.
            - Tables → card stacks:
                - Users table (A3) → card per user.
                - Support tickets (A5) → card per ticket.
                - Tasks (A6) → vertical Kanban or simple grouped lists.
        
        ---
        
        ## **8.3 Shared Component Rules**
        
        ### **8.3.1 Buttons & CTAs**
        
        - Primary: **Yalla Yellow background**, black text.
        - Secondary: neutral dark background, light border.
        - Destructive: red outline or red text.
        
        **Behaviour:**
        
        - Full-width on mobile (especially CTAs).
        - Right-aligned or grouped on desktop.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.2 Forms & Inputs**
        
        - Max 1–2 columns on desktop; **never** multi-column on mobile.
        - Mobile:
            - Use full-width fields.
            - Generous vertical spacing.
        - Desktop:
            - Two-column layouts allowed only where it increases scanning (e.g. First/Last name, Price / Currency).
        
        Validation:
        
        - Instant inline validation where possible.
        - Error messages below the field in red, concise.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.3 Chips & Status Badges**
        
        Used everywhere for statuses: Saved, Confirmed, Pending, etc.
        
        - Always left-aligned within cards.
        - On mobile: chips wrap to next line gracefully (no horizontal scroll).
        - Color rules:
            - Green: confirmed / success / active.
            - Yellow: pending / attention.
            - Red: cancelled / error.
            - Grey: neutral / info (e.g. “Saved”).
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.4 Cards (Property, Booking, Task, Survey)**
        
        **Mobile (default)**:
        
        - Full-width.
        - Stack:
            1. Title (address or task title)
            2. Key numbers (price, time, priority)
            3. Status chips
            4. Primary & secondary buttons.
        
        **Desktop**:
        
        - Cards sit in grids (2–3 columns) where appropriate.
        - In admin, cards may be replaced with tables (A1, A3, A4, A8).
        
        Spacing:
        
        - Padding: 16–24px.
        - Rounded corners (Dashfolio+ style).
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.5 Tables (Admin-heavy screens)**
        
        - Desktop:
            - Full standard table with:
                - Sticky header
                - Hover highlight
            - Columns never too tight; use ellipsis for long fields.
        - Mobile:
            - Convert each row into a **card**:
                - Show essential columns only (Name, Role, Status, Last Active).
                - Include “View details” CTA (opens A2 etc.).
            - Optional: horizontal scroll for extra technical fields (A4, A8).
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.6 Modals & Drawers**
        
        **Desktop:**
        
        - Center modal for short forms.
        - Right-side drawer for detail views (e.g. Survey detail, Task detail).
        
        **Mobile:**
        
        - Full-screen overlay with back arrow.
        - Close via top “X” or swipe down (if supported).
        
        All modals must:
        
        - Have a clear **title**.
        - Clear primary action and secondary cancel.
        
        ---
        
        ### **8.3.7 Navigation & Sidebars**
        
        - **Owner / HH Apps:**
            - Sidebar entries map directly to WF labels:
                - Owner: Dashboard, Listings, Inquiries, Calendar, Documents, Settings.
                - HH: Dashboard, Inbox, Saved/Bookings, Offers, Surveys, Settings.
        - **Admin:**
            - Sidebar: A1–A9 labelled exactly as in the spec (Admin Dashboard, Users, Integrations, Support, Tasks, Surveys, Billing, Settings, etc.).
        
        On mobile:
        
        - Put the **most important 3–4 items** quick-access (e.g. bottom bar for HH: Dashboard, Inbox, Saved, Profile).
        
        ---
        
        ## **8.4 Performance & Accessibility Rules**
        
        ### **Performance**
        
        - Image sizes:
            - Thumbnails: compressed, lazy-loaded below the fold.
        - Avoid:
            - Heavy animations.
            - Multi-MB background videos.
        - Use:
            - Skeleton loaders for lists (Inbox, Bookings, Tasks).
            - Paginated lists for Admin tables (A3, A5, A6, A7, A8).
        
        ---
        
        ### **Accessibility**
        
        - Color contrast: must meet WCAG AA (especially yellow on dark).
        - Text size: never below 13px.
        - Touch targets: at least 44×44px.
        - Keyboard navigation must work for:
            - Modals
            - Forms
            - Tables
        
        ---
        
        ## **8.5 30-Second Dev/Design Summary**
        
        - **Mobile-first** for HH & Owners; **desktop-first** for Admin — but all responsive.
        - Sidebars collapse; tables become cards; modals become full-screen sheets.
        - Shared rules across cards, chips, buttons avoid custom one-off components.
        - Performance/a11y constraints are baked in (lazy load, skeletons, tap targets).
        
        ---
        
    - **Analytics & Event Tracking Matrix (Master Spec)**
    This is the **single source of truth** for all events fired across Yalla.House.
        
        Everything maps to:
        
        **Frontend → Backend → Analytics → Funnels → Insights → Product Iteration.**
        
        ---
        
        # **🧩 SECTION 9 — Analytics & Event Tracking Matrix (Master Spec)**
        
        **Covers: Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin / System events + funnels + metadata.**
        
        ---
        
        # **9.1 Tracking Principles**
        
        ### **1. Every event must be:**
        
        - **Consistent** (same naming rules everywhere)
        - **Structured** (object-based payload, never raw strings)
        - **Low-noise** (only meaningful events)
        - **Funnel-aware** (belongs to at least one funnel)
        - **GDPR-safe** (no sensitive fields in analytics)
        
        ### **2. Naming Convention**
        
        ```
        category.action.performed
        ```
        
        Examples:
        
        - listing.create.started
        - booking.viewing.confirmed
        - offer.submitted
        - survey.purchase.completed
        - admin.task.created
        
        ### **3. Payload Rules**
        
        Each event sends:
        
        ```
        {
          userID,
          role,
          sessionID,
          placeID (optional),
          listingID (if relevant),
          eventTimestamp,
          metadata: { key:value pairs }
        }
        ```
        
        ### **4. Destinations**
        
        - Internal event_log (DB)
        - Analytics pipeline (Segment-compatible)
        - Optional Phase 2: GA4 / Mixpanel export
        
        ---
        
        # **9.2 Funnels Overview**
        
        We track **three funnels**:
        
        ## **A) Home-Hunter Funnel**
        
        ```
        Page Viewed
        → Saved Place
        → Viewing Booked
        → Viewing Attended
        → Offer Submitted
        → Survey Purchased
        → Completion (sale/rent)
        ```
        
        ## **B) Owner Funnel**
        
        ```
        Signup
        → Create Listing Draft
        → Listing Published
        → First Inquiry Received
        → First Viewing Booked
        → First Offer Received
        → Completion
        ```
        
        ## **C) Admin / Ops Funnel**
        
        ```
        Task Created
        → Assigned
        → In Progress
        → Waiting
        → Completed
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **9.3 EVENTS BY USER TYPE**
        
        ---
        
        # **9.3.1 HOME-HUNTER EVENTS**
        
        *(Mapped to WF-H1 → WF-H6)*
        
        ---
        
        ## **H1 Dashboard**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** | **Metadata** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | hh.dashboard.opened | HH visited dashboard | { tab } |
        | hh.notifications.viewed | Viewed updates | {} |
        
        ---
        
        ## **H2 Inbox**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** |
        | --- | --- |
        | hh.inbox.opened | Thread list opened |
        | hh.message.opened | Thread opened |
        | hh.message.sent | HH sends msg |
        | hh.attachment.uploaded | File added in msg |
        
        ---
        
        ## **H3 Saved Places**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** | **Metadata** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | hh.place.saved | User clicks “Save Place” | { placeID } |
        | hh.place.unsaved | Removed from saved | { placeID } |
        | hh.saved_places.viewed | Opens page | {} |
        
        ---
        
        ## **H4 Viewing Flow**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** | **Metadata** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | booking.viewing.requested | HH clicks “Book viewing” | { placeID, time } |
        | booking.viewing.auto_confirmed | Auto-confirm logic success | { placeID, slotID } |
        | booking.viewing.cancelled | Cancelled by HH | { reason } |
        | booking.viewing.attended | Confirm attended | { placeID } |
        | booking.viewing.no_show | Marked no-show | { placeID } |
        
        ---
        
        ## **H5 Offers / Applications**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** | **Metadata** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | offer.form.opened | HH enters offer | { placeID } |
        | offer.submitted | Offer submitted | { amount, docsUploaded } |
        | offer.updated | Offer modified (counter) | { amount } |
        | offer.withdrawn | Offer withdrawn | { placeID } |
        | application.submitted | Rental application | { docs } |
        
        ---
        
        ## **H6 Surveys**
        
        | **Event** | **Description** | **Metadata** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | survey.card.viewed | HH sees survey options | { placeID } |
        | survey.purchase.started | Stripe checkout open | { surveyID } |
        | survey.purchase.completed | Paid | { amount, surveyID } |
        | survey.view.opened | Opens PDF | { surveyID } |
        | survey.requested | User requests owner to upload | { placeID } |
        
        ---

        # **9.5 EVENT PAYLOAD STANDARDS**
        
        ```
        {
          eventName: "offer.submitted",
          userID: "USR-00192",
          role: "home-hunter",
          placeID: "PLC-22119",
          listingID: "LST-00222",
          timestamp: ISO_8601,
          metadata: {
              amount: 650000,
              docs: 2,
              source: "web",
              referrer: "public_listing_page"
          }
        }
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **9.6 EVENT → FUNNEL MAPPINGS (Critical)**
        
        ### **Home-Hunter**
        
        | **Funnel Stage** | **Events** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Viewed | public.place.viewed |
        | Saved | hh.place.saved |
        | Booked | booking.viewing.requested |
        | Attended | booking.viewing.attended |
        | Offer | offer.submitted |
        | Survey | survey.purchase.completed |
        | Completion | Manual sync from Admin |
        
        ---
        
        ### **Owner**
        
        | **Stage** | **Events** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Draft | listing.create.started |
        | Live | listing.published |
        | First Inquiry | owner.message.received |
        | First Viewing | booking.viewing.requested |
        | First Offer | offer.submitted |
        | Completion | Admin input |
        
        ---
        
        ### **Admin/Ops**
        
        | **Stage** | **Event** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Create | admin.task.created |
        | Assign | admin.task.assigned |
        | Work | admin.task.status_changed |
        | Done | admin.task.status_changed |
        
        ---
        
        # **9.7 ANALYTICS DASHBOARD BLUEPRINT (Phase 2)**
        
        - Owners Funnel chart
        - HH Funnel completion rate
        - Viewings per listing
        - Offer conversion rate
        - Survey revenue per listing
        - Ops task backlog
        - SLA breach rate
        - Integration uptime score
        
        ---
        
        # **9.8 STORAGE**
        
        All events stored in:
        
        ```
        events_log
          - eventID
          - eventName
          - userID
          - role
          - placeID
          - listingID
          - timestamp
          - metadata (JSON)
        ```
        
        Partitioned by month for speed.
        
        ---
        
    - **Database & API Schema (MVP)**
        
        **“What tables do we need + which APIs talk to them + how IDs connect across the whole system.” S**plit it into:
        
        1. Core Identity & Accounts
        2. Listings & Places
        3. Messaging & Inquiries
        4. Viewings & Slots
        5. Saved Places & HH Hub
        6. Offers / Applications
        7. Surveys & Survey Marketplace
        8. Support, Tasks & Admin
        9. Billing & Revenue
        10. Integrations, Events & Settings
        11. API Design Patterns (auth, pagination, errors)
        
        **10.1 Core Identity & Accounts**
        
        **10.1.1 users (Owners, Home-Hunters, Admin)**
        
        Single table with roles.
        
        | **Field** | **Type** | **Notes** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | id | UUID (PK) | Internal primary key |
        | external_id | string | e.g. USR-00214 |
        | role | enum | owner, home_hunter, admin, support, founder |
        | first_name | string |  |
        | last_name | string |  |
        | email | string (unique) |  |
        | phone | string (nullable) | Normalised + country code |
        | country | string | ISO code |
        | password_hash | string | Or external auth later |
        | email_verified | bool |  |
        | phone_verified | bool | Enables WhatsApp etc. |
        | trust_score | int | 0–100 |
        | verification_status | enum | none, partial, complete |
        | created_at | timestamp |  |
        | updated_at | timestamp |  |
        | last_login_at | timestamp |  |
        | last_ip | string | For risk checks |
        | is_suspended | bool |  |
        
        Used by: **WF-A2, A3, ACC, all HH/Owner flows**
        
        **10.1.2 user_profiles (optional extended info)**
        
        | **Field** | **Type** | **Notes** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | user_id | UUID (FK → users.id) | PK |
        | bio | text |  |
        | avatar_url | string |  |
        | language | string | en-GB, later de-DE |
        | timezone | string |  |
        | marketing_opt_in | bool |  |
        
        **10.1.3 user_devices (for behaviour & risk)**
        
        | **Field** | **Type** | **Notes** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | id | UUID |  |
        | user_id | UUID |  |
        | device_type | enum | mobile, desktop |
        | user_agent | text |  |
        | last_seen_at | timestamp |  |
        | last_ip | string |  |
