        **10.11 API DESIGN PATTERNS**
        
        **10.11.1 Auth**
        
        - All Owner / HH endpoints → Bearer token / session-based auth.
        - Admin routes prefixed with /admin/* and role-checked.
        - Support staff can only access WF-A3/A5/A6 parts (RBAC).
        
        **10.11.2 Common Patterns**
        
        **Pagination**
        
        - Query params: ?page=1&limit=20
        - Response:
        
        {
        
        "data": [...],
        
        "pagination": {
        
        "page": 1,
        
        "limit": 20,
        
        "total": 135
        
        }
        
        }
        
        **Errors**
        
        {
        
        "error": {
        
        "code": "VIEWING_SLOT_FULL",
        
        "message": "This slot is fully booked."
        
        }
        
        }
        
        **10.11.3 Key Endpoint Groups (summary)**
        
        I’ll map them to the earlier sections:
        
        **Auth & Users**
        
        - POST /auth/register
        - POST /auth/login
        - POST /auth/logout
        - GET /me — profile
        - PATCH /me — update profile
        - PATCH /me/phone + POST /me/phone/verify
        
        **Places & Listings**
        
        - GET /places/:id (public)
        - GET /listings/:id
        - POST /owner/listings
        - PATCH /owner/listings/:id
        - POST /owner/listings/:id/publish
        - GET /owner/listings (owner dashboard)
        - GET /public/search (property search, Phase 2)
        
        **Saved Places (H3)**
        
        - GET /hh/saved-places
        - POST /hh/saved-places (save)
        - DELETE /hh/saved-places/:id (unsave)
        
        **Viewings (H1/H4/O4)**
        
        - GET /listings/:id/slots
        - POST /hh/viewings (create booking – auto-confirm)
        - GET /hh/viewings
        - POST /hh/viewings/:id/cancel
        - POST /owner/viewings/:id/update (attended/no-show)
        
        **Inbox / Messaging (H2/O3)**
        
        - GET /hh/conversations
        - GET /hh/conversations/:id/messages
        - POST /hh/conversations/:id/messages
        - (owner equivalents under /owner/...)
        
        **Offers (H5 / O-side)**
        
        - GET /hh/offers
        - POST /hh/offers (create/submit)
        - PATCH /hh/offers/:id (update/withdraw)
        - GET /owner/offers
        - POST /owner/offers/:id/respond (accept/counter/reject)
        
        **Surveys (H6 / A7 / O Docs)**
        
        - GET /hh/surveys
        - POST /survey/purchase
        - GET /survey/:id (access control)
        - POST /owner/surveys (upload)
        - GET /admin/surveys (A7 grid)
        - POST /admin/surveys/:id/approve
        - POST /admin/surveys/:id/reject
        - POST /admin/surveys/:id/payout
        
        **Support & Tasks (A5 & A6)**
        
        - GET /admin/support/tickets
        - GET /admin/support/tickets/:id
        - POST /admin/support/tickets/:id/reply
        - POST /admin/support/tickets/:id/assign
        - POST /admin/support/tickets/:id/status
        - GET /admin/tasks
        - POST /admin/tasks
        - PATCH /admin/tasks/:id
        - GET /admin/tasks/:id/history
        
        **Billing (A8)**
        
        - GET /admin/revenue/summary
        - GET /admin/transactions
        - GET /admin/payouts
        - POST /admin/payouts/:id/pay
        - POST /admin/transactions/:id/refund
        
        **Integrations & Settings (A4 & A9)**
        
        - GET /admin/integrations/status
        - POST /admin/integrations/ping-all
        - GET /admin/settings
        - PATCH /admin/settings

---

- **GDPR DELETION WORKFLOW**
    
    ### **Developer Implementation Guide + Legal Logic**
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 0. Trigger Events (when deletion starts)**
    
    Deletion begins when ONE of these happens:
    
    1. **User clicks “Delete Account”**
    2. **User submits GDPR deletion request via Support**
    3. **Admin initiates a deletion (verified request)**
    4. **Automatic deletion trigger** (e.g., 24 months inactivity — optional later)
    
    → The workflow must start with a **2-step confirmation** to avoid accidental deletions.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 1. Identify User + Run Pre-Check**
    
    Before deleting, the system must:
    
    ### **1. Verify identity**
    
    - Login required OR
    - Email confirmation code
    - Admin request requires supervisor approval (Phase 2)
    
    ### **2. Check dependencies**
    
    ```
    IF user has live listing → Block deletion
    IF user has an active subscription → Block deletion
    IF user has open financial transactions → Block deletion (legal)
    IF user has pending dispute → Block deletion (legal)
    ```
    
    System returns:
    
    > “You must unpublish your listing first.”
    > 
    
    > “You have an active Stripe subscription.”
    > 
    
    > “There is an unresolved payment.”
    > 
    
    If nothing prevents deletion → continue.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 2. PERSONAL DATA DELETION PROCESS**
    
    Yalla.House deletes **identity-linked data**, but keeps **analytics**, **property data**, and **pricing data** (anonymised).
    
    ### **Developer rule:**
    
    > Delete anything that identifies the person.
    > 
    
    > Keep anything that describes the property.
    > 
    
    ### **2.1 Delete Account Identity**
    
    - Name
    - Email
    - Phone number
    - Profile info
    - Buyer position
    - KYC fields
    - Communication preferences
    
    ➡ **Fully delete (hard delete)**
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 3. Delete OWNER personal data**
    
    > Only personal data is deleted.
    > 
    
    > Property data stays (legal + strategic advantage).
    > 
    
    ### **Delete (personal):**
    
    - Owner name from listing
    - Owner phone/email
    - Owner preferences
    - Owner message history (or anonymise)
    - Owner calendar preferences
    
    ### **Retain (allowed + important):**
    
    - Address
    - Photos (unless containing person)
    - Floorplans
    - EPC
    - Property description
    - Property size/type
    - Price history → **retain but anonymise source**
    - Viewing stats
    - Offer history → anonymise
    - Survey marketplace metadata
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 4. Delete HOME-HUNTER personal data**
    
    ### **Delete:**
    
    - Identity (name/email/phone)
    - Saved places (or unlink user ID)
    - Inbox messages (or anonymise sender)
    - Offers → anonymise (keep number & price)
    - Viewings → anonymise (keep aggregation only)
    
    ### **Retain:**
    
    - Market interest signals (anonymous)
    - Survey purchases → **keep for 6 years** (legal) but remove name
    - Analytics (views, clicks, funnels)
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 5. Clean SYSTEM DATA (Logs + Billing)**
    
    ### **Keep (required):**
    
    - Stripe invoices → 6 years (HMRC law)
    - Payment history → 6 years
    - Survey marketplace payouts → 6 years
    - Audit logs → 12 months
    
    ### **Delete:**
    
    - Authentication logs older than 12 months
    - Webhook error logs older than 90 days
    - Session cookies
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 6. ANONYMISATION RULES**
    
    Anything used for analytics must be **unlinkable** to a real person.
    
    ### **Replace user ID with:**
    
    ```
    anon_user_82df90c
    ```
    
    Or:
    
    ```
    buyer_deleted
    ```
    
    ### **Fields to strip:**
    
    - IP address
    - Email hash
    - Any ID used across systems
    - Any message content
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 7. SYSTEM-WIDE CASCADE DELETE**
    
    This is the technical heart.
    
    When a user is deleted:
    
    ```
    DELETE FROM Users WHERE user_id = X
    
    UPDATE Listings SET owner_id = NULL WHERE owner_id = X
    UPDATE Listings SET owner_contact = NULL WHERE owner_id = X
    
    UPDATE Messages SET sender_id = NULL, sender_name = 'deleted user'
    UPDATE Viewings SET user_id = NULL
    UPDATE Offers SET user_id = NULL
    UPDATE Surveys SET buyer_id = NULL
    ```
    
    Everything else (property data, market analytics) remains untouched.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 8. CONFIRMATION & EXPORT**
    
    Before final deletion:
    
    ### **Step A — Offer export:**
    
    User can download ALL personal data:
    
    - Messages
    - Offers
    - Bookings
    - Account info
    
    > GDPR requires this (Art. 20 — “Right to portability”).
    > 
    
    ### **Step B — Confirm deletion:**
    
    > “Your account will be permanently deleted in 7 days.”
    > 
    
    ### **Step C — Final purge:**
    
    After **7-day grace period**:
    
    - All personal data destroyed
    - All links severed
    - Anonymous data kept
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 9. POST-DELETION NOTICES**
    
    - Show confirmation page
    - Send final deletion email
    - Log deletion event in audit logs (12 months)
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 10. Internal Requirement**
    
    This workflow must be replicated in:
    
    ✔ Admin Panel → “Delete User (GDPR-safe)”
    
    ✔ Support Inbox → “Process GDPR Request”
    
    ✔ Auto-process in backend
    
    ---
    
    # 
    
- **Big-Picture System Architecture**
    
    ```jsx
                    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
                    │               CLIENT LAYER              │
                    ├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
                    │  A) Public Web (Framer + Dashfolio+)    │
                    │     - Home / Services / About / Legal   │
                    │     - Public Property Page (WF-O5)      │
                    │                                         │
                    │  B) Owner Workspace (Framer)            │
                    │     - Dashboard (WF-O1)                 │
                    │     - My Listings (WF-O2)               │
                    │     - Inquiries (WF-O3)                 │
                    │     - Calendar (WF-O4)                  │
                    │                                         │
                    │  C) Home-Hunter Workspace (Framer)      │
                    │     - HH Dashboard / Inbox / Saved      │
                    │     - Booking flow (WF-H1+)             │
                    │                                         │
                    │  D) Admin Console (Framer / Internal)   │
                    │     - A1–A9 Admin Screens               │
                    └─────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                                      │ HTTPS / JSON (REST or GraphQL)
                                      ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │                    APPLICATION LAYER                      │
            ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │  API Gateway / Backend (Node.js / Nest / similar)         │
            │                                                           │
            │  • Auth Service                                           │
            │  • Owner Service (Listings, Surveys, Billing refs)        │
            │  • Home-Hunter Service (Saved Places, Offers, Surveys)    │
            │  • Messaging Service (Inquiries, threads)                 │
            │  • Booking & Calendar Service                             │
            │  • Survey Marketplace Service                             │
            │  • Billing & Plans Service (Stripe integration)           │
            │  • Integrations Hub (Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM – Phase 2)     │
            │  • Notifications Service (Email + WhatsApp)               │
            │  • Admin/Reporting Service                               │
            │                                                           │
            │  (MVP) minimal services: Auth, Owner, HH, Messaging,      │
            │        Booking, Billing, Notifications, Admin-lite        │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                                      │ Internal service calls / queues
                                      ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │                          DATA LAYER                       │
            ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │  1. PRIMARY APP DATABASE (SQL – e.g. Postgres)            │
            │     • Users (Owner, Home-Hunter, Admin)                   │
            │     • Places (Listings)                                   │
            │     • Viewings / Bookings                                │
            │     • Inquiries / Messages                               │
            │     • Offers                                             │
            │     • Surveys (metadata)                                 │
            │     • Subscriptions / Plans (Stripe IDs)                 │
            │                                                           │
            │  2. FILE STORAGE (Object Store – e.g. S3 / GCS)           │
            │     • Photos                                             │
            │     • Floorplans                                         │
            │     • EPC PDFs                                           │
            │     • Survey PDFs                                        │
            │                                                           │
            │  3. ANALYTICS STORE (Warehouse / events DB)              │
            │     • Anonymised events (views, clicks, funnels)         │
            │     • Channel attribution (RM, Zoopla, Signboard, etc.)  │
            │     • Revenue + cost metrics (owner-level & global)      │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                         ┌────────────┴────────────┐
                         ▼                         ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────────────┐
            │  EXTERNAL INTEGRATIONS    │ │  OBSERVABILITY & SECURITY   │
            ├───────────────────────────┤ ├─────────────────────────────┤
            │ • Stripe (billing)        │ │ • Logging (app + audit)     │
            │ • WhatsApp / Twilio       │ │ • Error tracking             │
            │ • Email provider          │ │ • Performance monitoring     │
            │ • Maps / Geocoding        │ │ • Access logs / admin 2FA   │
            │ • Rightmove / Zoopla /    │ │ • GDPR deletion workflows    │
            │   OnTheMarket (Phase 2)   │ │   (personal vs analytics)    │
            └───────────────────────────┘ └─────────────────────────────┘
    
    ```

    - **Data Flow (Quick Owner + Home-Hunter Story)**
        
        ### **Owner Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. **Owner hits “List Your Place” on Header**
            
            → goes to WF-O2 “New Place” wizard (Step 1 Basics).
            
        2. Fills postcode, address, listing type → Backend Owner Service creates draft place + listing.
        3. Continues through Price / Extras → data saved into primary DB.
        4. Hits “Publish” → Listing visible on Public Property Page (WF-O5).
        5. Views funnel + channel breakdown on WF-O1 Dashboard (via Analytics Store).
        6. Gets bookings → Booking Service writes viewings, Messaging Service starts threads.
        7. Upgrades to a higher package → Stripe subscription → Billing Service → Admin A8 sees it.
        
        ### **Home-Hunter Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. Sees listing on Rightmove → clicks “More Info / Book a Viewing” → lands on WF-O5.
        2. Chooses slot → Booking Service creates viewing, auto-confirms if slot free.
        3. Receives WhatsApp + email confirmation with link to create account (optional).
        4. If they create account → they see:
            - “Upcoming Viewings”
            - “Saved Places”
            - “My Offers”
        5. They can buy a survey → Survey Marketplace Service + Stripe + Surveys DB.
        
        ### **Admin Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. Logs into Admin console.
        2. Sees A1 Dashboard:
            - Active listings, active users, channel performance.
        3. Clicks A2 User Detail → sees per-user metrics, lifetime value, success rate.
        4. A4 Integrations shows any broken feeds (portals, WhatsApp, email).
        5. A6 Tasks & Fulfilment – signboard orders, EPC to schedule, manual actions.
        6. A7 Surveys – verify new uploads, approve payouts.
        
        ---
        
        If you like, next step could be:
        
        - **“Developer Execution Plan v2”**: concrete tasks based on this architecture (what to build first, second, third), or
        - A **simplified “one-slide” version** for pitching / freelancers.
        
        Tell me if you’d like **Dev Plan**, **Pitch Slide**, or **Both**.
        
    - **Component list (with MVP vs Phase 2 flags)**
        
        ### **CLIENT LAYER**
        
        **Public Web (Framer, Dashfolio+)**
        
        - **MVP**:
            - Home, Services & Pricing, About, Legal Hub, Support
            - Public Property Page (WF-O5) with “Arrange a Visit” + “Message Owner”
        - **Phase 2**:
            - Blog/SEO content
            - Market reports (data product later)
        
        **Owner Workspace (Sidebar + Header frozen)**
        
        - Dashboard (WF-O1) – KPIs + funnels + source pie chart
        - My Listings (WF-O2) – listing table + “New Place” wizard
        - Inquiries (WF-O3) – unified inbox
        - Calendar (WF-O4) – slots for open house & 1:1 viewings
        - Account Settings (via WF-ACC)
        
        **Home-Hunter Workspace**
        
        - HH Dashboard (H1/H8) – upcoming visits, saved places, offers
        - Inbox (H2) – messaging with Owners / system
        - Saved Places & Offers (H3/H5 merged funnel)
        - Surveys (H4/H6) – list purchased & available surveys
        - Account Settings (WF-ACC shared)
        
        **Admin Console**
        
        - A1 Dashboard – global KPIs + alerts
        - A2 User Detail View – Owners & HH metrics combined
        - A3 Owners & HH lists
        - A4 Integrations & Status (Stripe, WhatsApp, email, portals)
        - A5 Support Inbox
        - A6 Tasks & Fulfilment (signboards, EPC, photos, etc.)
        - A7 Surveys Marketplace Oversight
        - A8 Billing & Revenue
        - A9 System Settings (roles, language, feature flags – Phase 2 heavy)
        
        ---
        
        ### **APPLICATION LAYER (Backend Services)**
        
        You don’t have to build microservices from day 1; this can be **one monolith with clear modules**.
        
        **1. Auth & Identity Service (MVP)**
        
        - Login/logout, password reset
        - Role: Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin
        - Future: 2FA, KYC hooks
        
        **2. Owner Service (MVP)**
        
        - CRUD for Places (listings)
        - New Place “wizard” flow (O2 4-step progress)
        - Status changes (Draft, Live, Under Offer, Sold, Let)
        - Owner KPIs aggregation for Dashboard
        
        **3. Home-Hunter Service (MVP)**
        
        - Saved Places
        - Offers
        - Viewing booking history
        - Survey purchase references
        
        **4. Messaging Service (MVP)**
        
        - Threads: Owner ↔ Home-Hunter
        - Status: New, Replied, Archived, Offer-related
        - GDPR deletion → anonymise sender
        
        **5. Booking & Calendar Service (MVP)**
        
        - Owner time slots (open house vs 1:1)
        - Booking confirmation logic:
            - Default = auto-confirm if slot is free
            - Owner reschedule → triggers message + new slot suggestion
        - Integration with Google Calendar (Phase 2)
        
        **6. Survey Marketplace Service (Phase 1 lite, Phase 2 full)**
        
        - Upload / verify / price surveys
        - Owners: attach survey to place, set profit share
        - Home-Hunters: browse / unlock survey
        - Admin: A7 oversight + payouts
        
        **7. Billing & Plans Service (MVP)**
        
        - Stripe customer + subscription IDs
        - Track which Owner has which plan + one-off services
        - Expose data to Admin A8 and Owner Billing/Settings
        
        **8. Integrations Hub (Phase 2)**
        
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OnTheMarket feeds
        - Direction:
            - Owner → we push listing
            - Portals → click/call leads → we track channel
        - Signboard QR routing (channel = “Signboard”)
        
        **9. Notifications Service (MVP)**
        
        - Email: booking confirmations, reminders, account events
        - WhatsApp: links to WF-O5/H1 for bookings
        - Configurable in WF-ACC (notifications section)
        
        **10. Admin/Reporting Service (MVP → Phase 2)**
        
        - Aggregates data for A1/A8
        - Owner/HH-level metrics for A2/A3
        - Global funnels + channel performance
        
        ---
        
        ### **DATA LAYER**
        
        **Primary App DB (e.g. Postgres)**
        
        - users (roles, locale, notification prefs)
        - places (non-personal property data)
        - listings (status + owner link)
        - viewings (bookings, slots)
        - messages
        - offers
        - surveys (metadata)
        - subscriptions / invoices (with Stripe IDs, not card data)
        
        **File Storage**
        
        - Put all files under structured prefixes:
            - /places/{placeId}/photos/...
            - /places/{placeId}/docs/epc.pdf
            - /surveys/{surveyId}.pdf
        
        **Analytics Store (Events)**
        
        - Separate from primary DB
        - Events: VIEW_PLACE, CLICK_BOOK, CREATE_OFFER, SURVEY_PURCHASED
        - Fields: timestamp, placeId, channel, device, *anonymised userId*
        - Used for Owner Dashboard, Admin Analytics, future data products.
        
        ---
        
        ### **INTEGRATIONS**
        
        **Stripe (MVP)**
        
        - Subscriptions: Package A/B/C monthly
        - One-off services: photos, EPC, signboards, survey unlock
        - Webhooks into Billing Service and Admin A8.
        
        **WhatsApp (via Twilio or similar)**
        
        - Owner: booking notifications
        - Home-Hunter: booking confirmation + reschedule links
        - Support: “Message us on WhatsApp” from public pages
        
        **Email Provider**
        
        - Transactional emails (SendGrid/Postmark etc.)
        
        **Maps/Geocoding**
        
        - Convert postcode/address to map location & region stats
        - Power WF-O5 map + location info.
        
        **Portals (Phase 2)**
        
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OTM feed handler
        - Channel tracking for Owner Dashboard + Admin.
    1. **How data flows (Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin)**
